Disease: dama (Asthma) Description: sookasham shavaas naliyon men koi rog utapanan ho jaane ke kaaran jab kisi vayakati ko sns lene men pareshaani hone lagati hai tab yah sathiti dama rog kahalaati hai, is rog men vayakati ko khnsi ki samasaya bhi hoti hai। Symptoms: - jab dama rog se pirit rogi ko daura parata hai to use sookhi ya aithamadaar khnsi hoti hai। - jab rog bahut adhik barh jaata hai to daura aane ki sathiti utapanan ho jaati hai jisase rogi ko sns lene men bahut adhik dikakat aati hai tatha vayakati chhatapataane lagata hai। - dama rog se pirit rogi ko kaph sakhata, badaboodaar tatha doridaar nikalata hai। - pirit rogi ko sns lemen men bahut adhik kathinaai hoti hai। - yah rog satari-purush donon ko ho sakata hai। - raat ke samay men lagabhag 2 baje ke baad daure adhik parate hain। - rogi ko rog ke shuruaati samay men khnsi, sarasaraahat aur sns ukharane ke daure parane lagate hain। - sns lete samay adhik jor lagaane par rogi ka chehara laal ho jaata hai। - sns lete samay halaki-halaki siti bajane ki aavaaj bhi sunaai parati hai। - sns leme tatha sns ko baahar chhorane men kaaphi jor lagaana parata hai। Reasons: - aushadhiyon ka adhik parayog karane ke kaaran kaf sookh jaane se dama ho jaata hai। - khaana-paan ke galat tarike se yah rog ho sakata hai। - maanasik tamaava, karodh tatha adhik bhay ke kaaran bhi dama hone ka ek kaaran hai। - khoon men kisi parakaar se dosh utapanan ho jaane ke kaaran bhi dama ho sakata hai। - nashile padaarathon ka adhik sevan karana bhi is rog ka kaaran hai। - khnsi, jukaam tatha najala rog adhik samay tak rahane se dama ho sakata hai। - bhookh se adhik bhojam khaane se dama ho sakata hai। - miracha-masaale, tale-bhune khaaday padaarathon tatha garishath bhojan karane se yah rog ho sakata hai। - phepharon men kamajori, hariday men kamajori, guradon men kamajori, nton men kamajori, sanaayumanadal men kamajori tatha maakara rog ho jaane ke kaaram dama ho jaata hai। - manushay ki shavaas nalika mem dhool tatha thnd lag jaane ke kaaran bhi dama ho sakata hai। - dhool ke kana, khopari ke khuranada, kuchh paudhon ke pushaparaja, anade tatha aise hi anay padaarathon ka bhojan men adhik sevan karame ke kaaran yah rog ho sakata hai। - manushay ke sharir ki paachan naliyon men jalan utapanan karane vaale padaarathon ka sevan karane se bhi dama ho sakata hai। - mala-mootar ke veg ko baara-baar rokame se yah rog ho sakata hai। - garada, dhun, gndagi, badaboo, gnde bisatara, puraani kitaaben aur kaparom ki jhaara, kheton ki jhaara, sakhat saradi, barasaata, jukaama, phaloo, aadi sookasham kanon ka sns davaara phepharon men jaane se dama ho sakata hai। - vaataavaran men paradooshan se home vaali elaraji - isake alaava kai logon mem kuchh mishachit davaaon (esapirin aur betaa- balaokarasa) ke sevan se bhi dama ke risak phaikataras barh sakate hain। - atayadhik bhaavanaatamak abhivayakatiyn (jaise chikhane-chilalaame ya phir joradaar tarike se hnsana bhi) bhi kuchh logon men dama ki samasaya ko barhaakar daure ki sathiti utapanam kar sakati haim। - asathama ya elaraji ka paarivaarik itihaas (aanivnshik damaa) - janam ke samay kam vajam aur samay se pahale bachachon ka janama, janam ke pahale aur / ya janam ke baad tnbaakoo ke dhuen ke snparak - bhira, vaayuparadooshana, dhool (ghar ya baahar ki) ya pepar ki dasata, rasoi ka dhun, nami, silana, mausam parivaratana, saradi-jukaama, dhoomarapaana, phaasataphoodasa, tanaav v chintaa, paalatoo jaanavar ke snparak men rahana aur pera-paudhon aur phoolon ke paraagakanon (paudhe ke phoolon men paaye jaane vaale sookasham kanon ko paraagakan kahate hain) aadi ko shaamil kiya jaata hai। Treatments: - rogi ko garam bisatar par sona chaahie। - dhoomarapaan nahin karana chaahie। - bhojan men miracha-masaaledaar chijom ka sevan nahin karana chaahie। - dhool tatha dhune bhare vaataavaram se bachana chaahie। - maanasik pareshaani, tanaava, karodh tatha laraai-jhagadon se bachana chaahie। - sharaaba, tamabaakoo tatha anay nashile padaarathon ka sevan nahin karana chaahie। Home Remedies: - lahasun dama ke ilaaj men kaaphi kaaragar saabit hota hai। 30 mili doodh men lahasun ki pnch kaliyn ubaalen aur is misharan ka har roj sevan karane se dame men shuruaati avasatha mem kaaphi phaayada milata hai। - adarak ki garam chaay mem lahasum ki do pisi kaliyn milaakar pine se bhi asathama niyntarit rahata hai। sabere aur shaam is chaay ka sevan karane se marij ko phaayada hota hai। - adarak ka ek chamamach taaja rasa, ek kap maithi ke kaarhe aur savaadaanusaar shahad is misharan men milaaen। dame ke marijon ke lie yah misharan laajavaab saabit hota hai। - dama rogi paani men ajavaain milaakar ise ubaalen aur paani se uthati bhaap len, yah ghareloo upaay kaaphi phaayademnd hota hai। - 4-5 laung len aur 125 mili paani men 5 minat tak ubaalen। is misharan ko chhaanakar isamen ek chamamach shudadh shahad milaaen aur garama-garam pi len। har roj do se tin baar yah kaarha banaakar pine se marij ko nishachit roop se laabh hota hai। - 180 mimi paani men mutathibhar sahajan ki patatiyn milaakar karib 5 mimat tak ubaalen। misharan ko thnda hone den, usamen chutakibhar namaka, kaalimirach aur niboo ras bhi milaaya ja sakata hai। is soop ka niyamit roop se isatemaal dama upachaar men kaaragar maana gaya hai। - maithi ka kaarha taiyaar karane ke lie ek chamamach maithidaana aur ek kap paani ubaalen। har roj sabere-shaam is misharan ka sevan karane se nishachit laabh milata hai। - ek paka kela chhilaka lekar chaakoo se lamabaai mem chira lagaakar usamen ek chhota chamamach do garaam kapara chhaan ki hui kaali mirach bhar den। phir use bagair chhile hi, kele ke varikash ke patate mem achachhi tarah lapet kar dore se bndh kar 2-3 ghnte rakh den। baad men kele ke patate sahit use aag mem is parakaar bhoone ki upar ka patata jale। thnda hone par kele ka chhilaka nikaalakar kela kha lem। Disease: madhumeh (Diabetes) Description: madhumeh ya daayabitij haal ke saalon men hone vaala sabase khataranaak jivanashaili rog maana jaata hai। har saal kai hajaar log isase parabhaavit hote hain। aaiyen jaanem madhumeh ke baaren men jise log aam bolachaal ki bhaasha me shugar (Sugar ki Bimari) bhi kahate hain। Symptoms: - atayadhik payaas lagana aur baar baar peshaab aana (Excessive Thirst): yah madhumeh hone ke pukhata lakasham hain - jakhamom ka jaladi nahi bharana aur baar baar snkaraman se parabhaavit hona (Slow Healing Sores and Recurrent Infections) - thakaan mahasoos hona (Feeling Lazy): koshikaaom men galookoz nahi pahunchane ke kaaran sharir ko uraja aapoorati poori tarah se nahi ho paati hai aur madhumeh ka rogi hamesha thakaan mahasoos karata hai - dhundhala dikhana (Blurred Vision): rakat men atirikat shugar ki upasathiti ke kaaran nkhon ki koshikaaon men rakat aapoorati par asar parata hai aur dhire dhire nkhe parabhaavit hone lagati hain - pairo aur haathom men jhanajhanaahat hona (Tingling in Hands & Feet): rakat men atirikat shugar ka kaaran hamaare tntarika paranaali ko mukasaan pahuncha sakata hai - masooron men soojan (Swollen Gums): madhumeh ke kaaran masooron men snkaraman ka khatara barh jaata hai - rakat men atirikat shugar ki upasathiti ke kaaran gurade rakat ko saaf karane ke lie adhik kaam karame lagate hain aur mootar ke davaara atirikat shugar ko sharir se baahar nikalate hain। is kaaran baar baar peshaab aata hai aur atayadhik payaas lagati hai - vajan kam hona (Weight Loss): hamaare sharir men jab koshikaaon ko galookoz nahi milata to sharira, sharir men upasathit vasa tatha mnsapeshio se usaki aapoorati karata hai jisake kaaran sharir men jama vasa aur mnsapeshio men kami aati hai aur vajan bahut jaladi kam hone lagata hai Treatments: madhumeh ya daayabitij se bachaav ka sabase barhiya upaay hai isaki jaamakaari rakhana aur savasath jivanashaili apanaanaa। daayabitij se bachame ke kuchh khaan upaay niman hain: - paratidin ek ghnta vayaayaam jaroor karen। - apane ghar men paratidin madhumeh ka tesat karem। rakat mem shugar ki maatara ka dhayaan rakhen। - inasulin injekasham (Insulin Injetiom) ko taiyaar karama aur savayn lagaana aana chaahie। - ek inasulin pamap (Insulin Pump) saath rakhanaa। - kaarabohaaidaret (Carbohydrate) ki ginati ko dhayaan men rakhanaa। - rakatachaap (Blood Pressure) kam hone par matavapooran jaanakaari ka dhayaan rakhana Disease: vaayaral bukhaar (Viral Fever) Description: vaayaras ke snkaraman se hone vaale bukhaar ko vaayaral phivar (Viral Fever) kahate hain। vaayaral bukhaar ke vaayaras gale men supataavasatha men nishakariy rahate hain। thnde vaataavaran ke snparak men aane, pharij ka thnda paani, shital pey pine aadi se ye vaayaras sakariy hokar hamaare paratirakasha tntar ko parabhaavit kar dete hain। Symptoms: - nkhen laal hona - is bukhaar men sharir ka taap 101 digari se 103 digari ya aur jayaada bhi ho jaata hai - khnsi aur jukaam hona - joron mem darad aur soojan hona - thakaan aur gale men darad hona - naak bahana hona - badan darad hona - bhookh n lagana - letane ke baad uthame men kamajori mahasoos karana - siradarad hona Reasons: vaayaral bukhaar sharir ke kamazor paratirakasha tntar (Immune System) ki vajah se hota hai। agar sharir ki paratirakashan kashamata ya imayoon sisatam majaboot ho to yah bimaari jaladi nahin hoti। Treatments: vaayaral bukhaar ka upaay (Treatment of Viral Fever) - bukhaar agar 102 digari tak hai aur koi aur khataranaak lakashan nahin hain to marij ki dekhabhaal ghar par hi kar sakate hain। - marij ke sharir par saamaanay paani ki patatiyn rakhen। patatiyn tab tak rakhen, jab tak sharir ka taapamaan kam n ho jaae। patati rakhane ke baad vah garam ho jaati hai isalie use siraph 1 minat tak hi rakhen। - agar maathe ke saath - saath sharir bhi garam hai to naoramal paani men kapara bhigokar nichoren aur usase poore sharir ko ponchhen। - marij ko har chhah ghnte men pairaasitaamaol (Paracetamol) ki ek goli de sakate hain। doosari koi goli daokatar se poochhe bina n den। - bachachon ko har chaar ghnte men 10 mili parati kilo vajan ke anusaar dava de sakate hain। - do din tak bukhaar thik m ho to marij ko daokatar ke paas jaroor le jaaen। - saaph - saphaai ka poora khayaal rakhen। marij ko vaayaral hai, to usase thori doori bamaae rakhen aur rogi ke davaara isatemaal ki gai chijem isatemaal n karen। - marij ko poora aaraam karane den, khaasakar tej bukhaar mem। aaraam bhi bukhaar men ilaaj ka kaam karata hai। - marij chhinkane se pahale naak aur munh par rumaal rakhen। isase vaayaral hone par doosaron mem phailega nahin। - vaayaral phivar men entibaoyatik davaaon ki koi bhoomika nahin hoti। vaayaral phivar 5 se 7 dinon men thik ho jaata hai। - is rog ka ilaaj lakashanon ke aadhaar par kiya jaata hai, rogi ko parayaapat maatara men galookoj aur ilekatarolaait lema chaahie। Disease: khasara (Measles) Descriptiom: khasara (Measles), ek ataynt snkaraamak bimaari hai। khasara mijalas vaayaras (Measles Virus) se phailata hai। isase garasit rogi ka pahale gala kharaab hota hai aur usake baad bukhaar aata hai। Symptoms: - nkhon men laali, soojama, chipachipaapana, khujali, paani nikalanaa। - khnsi aur jukaam hona - gale men darad rahata hai। - chaar din ka bukhaara, bukhaar 40°C(104°F) tak pahunch sakata hai। - tinon si -khnsi (Cough), bahati hui naak (Coryza) aur nkh ka aana (Conjunctivitis)। - bachacha baara-baar rota hai। - sharir men tootama, thakaama, chirachiraapan hota hai। Reasons: abhi tak jamyaat kaaranon ke anusaar manushay ke davaara hi khasara ek se doosare manusay tak phailata hai। rogi ke kapare, bisatara, rumaal aadi isatemaal karane se vaayaral phailane ka khatara barh jaata hai। khasara ke jokhim (Risk Factors of Measles or Khasra) khasara men maak se paani bhi a sakata hai। yadi bimaari ka uchit upachaar n ho, to phephare men bhi isaka snkaraman ho sakata hai। baron men yah snkaraman vaayaral nimoniya men badal sakata hai। yah dasha rogi ke lie khataranaak saabit ho sakati hai। Treatments: khasara se bachaav ka sabase behatarin tarika hai isake rogi ke smparak men ma aanaa। lekin agar khasara (Khasra) ho bhi jaae to niman upaay davaara isase bachaav mumakin hai: - parabhaavit bachache/rogi ko unahen roj badalen। - bukhaar ki teji men sir par deshi ghi ki maalish v paani men sooti mota kapara bhigokar rakhen। - mukh v dnt saaph rakhane ke liye gunagune paani mem thori si laal dava (poteshiyam paramaiganeta) daalakar kulala karaaen। - dnton ko nguliyon se jor dekar n saaph karaaen। - bisatar ki sooti chaadar ko paratidin badalen। - khaane men saamaanaya, halakaa, pachane vaala khaana den। - namakin vasatuen kam maatara men den, jisase khujali n ho। - vitaamin yukat padaarath jaise paalaka, gaajar aadi jayaada den। - nkhon men sote samay gulaab jal daalen। subah uthane par borik paaudar gunagune paani men daalakar dhime-dhime rooi bhigokar nkhon ko dhoyen। - ghar se baahar m le jaayem, bahut jaroori ho to sooti mote kapare se dhak kar hi le jaaen। - dhayaan rakhe ki rogi ka kamara bahut thndaa, garam ya silam vaala n ho। - khasare ka ndesha hone par yah aavashayak hai ki kisi yogay daakatar se ilaaj karaaya jaae। isase bachane ka ekamaatar upaay bachachon ka tikaakaram hai। Disease: badahazami (Gastric Problem) Description: paachanakariya ke dauraam pet men gais ka bamana ek saamaamay parakariya hai। sharir ki anay parakariyaaon ki tarah pet men gais ka banana aur baahar mikal jaana bhi ek saamaamay parakariya hai। Symptoms: - khatati dakaaren aamaa, - khaana ya khatata paani (esida) munh men a jaanaa, - gale se kharakharaahat mahasoos hona aur sns hai isi kaaran joron men darad aur ainthan hoti hai। gathiya ko kai sa‍thaanon par aamavat bhi kaha jaata hai। Disease: pila bukhaar (Yellow Fever) Description: pitajavar ya pila bukhaar (Yellow lekin isake lie bahut se ilaaj maujood hain jo is par kaaboo pa sakate haim। pit javar ya pila bukhaar maada machachhar ke kaatane se hota hai। pile bukhaar men rogi ka livar daimej hone ya piliya hone ka khatara rahata hai। saath hi rogi ko ulatiyn bhi ho sakati hain। pile bukhaar se nijaat ke lie bahut se ghareloo musakhe bhi hain, jisase paraakaritik tarike se isaka upachaar kiya ja sake। 1. tulasi aur kaali mirach (Basil and Black Pepper) kaali mirach pile bukhaar ke ilaaj men bahut kaaragar saabit ho rahi hai। aadha litar disatilad paani men kuchh tulasi ke patate daalakar ubalane den। is paani men aadha chamamach kaali mirach ka paaudar milaaen। is paani ko rng badalane tak ubalane den। yah paani n keval pile bukhaar ko kam karata hai balaki aapako turnt uraja bhi deta hai। is paani men tin chamamach shahad bhi milaaya ja sakata hai। ise din men do baar pien। 2. payaaz (Onion) ek kachacha payaaj len aur do hisason men kaat len। ise ovan men daalakar lagabhag 15 minat ke lie 400 digari par senk len। aisa karane se payaaj ka ras aasaani se nikal jaata hai। is ras mem kuchh boonde shahad ki milaaen। is mitaran ko pile bukhaar se nijaat ke lie isatemaal karen। 3. lahasun (Garlic) baar baar ulati hone se dihaaidareshan ho jaata hai jisase sharir aamataur par kamajor ho jaata hai aur isase sharir ki imayooniti bhi ghatati hai। lahasun apame vaayaral virodhi, enti baikatiriyal aur enti aukasident gunon ke lie jaana jaata hai। lahasum paratirakasha paranaali ko majaboot bamaane ke saath saath vaayaral aur baikatiriyal snkaraman se sharir ki rakasha karane men sakariy bhoomika mibhaata hai। chhah se das lahasum ki kali lekar unahen kuchal len। is lahasun ko aap yoon bhi kha sakate hain ya phir shahad milaakar subah subah khaaem। 4. naariyal paani (Coconut Water) pile bukhaar men dihaaidaresham se bachane ke lie naariyal paani behad laabhakaari hai। yah sharir ko haaidaret karake anay poshak tatavon ki poorati karata hai। ek din men kam se kam tin se chaar baar naariyal pien। 5. ganane ka ras (Sugarcane Juice) dihaaidaresham pile bukhaar ka sabase khataramaak lakashan hai। aise men ganane ka ras kamajor sharir ko saphoorati deta hai। ganane ke ras se nirajalit sharir ke lie aavashayak vitaamin aur khanij ki aapoorati ki ja sakati hai। ganane ka ras sharir ki mnsapeshiyon men galookoj ki aapoorati karata hai। sharir men aavashayak parotin ki kami ko poora karane ke lie din men tin baar ganane ke ras ka isatemaal kiya ja sakata hai।yah bhi pile bukhaar se pirit marij ki uchach sharir ke taapamaan ko kam kar deta hai। 6. jau ka paani (Barley Water or Jau k pani) jau ek snpooran anaaj hai jisamen savasath jivan shaili ke lie sabhi aavashayak poshak tatav hai maujood hain। jau mem vitaamin bi 1, bi 2, bi 5, 9 aur vitaamin i hota hai। yah pile bukhaar se pirit marij ki soojan aur sharir ke uchach taapamaan ko kam karata hai। ek din men tin baar jau ka paani pine se pile bukhaar men aaraam milata hai। 7. ninboo aur namak (Lemon and Salt) pile bukhaar se pirit vayakati ko dihaaidareshan ki samasaya ho jaati hai। aise men vayakati aur jayaada thaka hua lagata hai। ek gilaas paani men ninboo ke ras ki kuchh boonde milaakar pine se bhi pile bukhaar men kaaphi aaraam milata hai। is ninboo vaale paani men ek chutaki namak bhi milaaen। yah paani dihaaidareshan ki kami ko poora karata hai aur rogi ko uraja deta hai। Disease: phaaileriya (Elephantiasis) Descriptiom: phaaileriya roga, jise haathi pnv ya phil pnv bhi kahate hain, (Elephantiasis) mem akasar haath ya pair bahut jayaada sooj jaate hain। isake alaava phaaileriya rog se pirit vayakati ke kabhi haatha, kabhi ndakosha, kabhi satan aadi ya kabhi anay ng bhi sooj sakate hain। aam bolachaal ki bhaasha men haathipnv (HathipaonHathipaom) bhi kaha jaata hai। Symptoms: - ek ya zayaada haath v pairon men (zayaadaatar pairon mem) soojan - kaepakaepi ke saath bukhaar aana - gale men soojan aana - gupatmg evn jaogho ke bich gilathi hona tatha darad rahana - purooshon ke ndakosh men soojan (haaidarosila) hona - pairon v haathon ki lasika vaahikaaen laal ho jaati hain Reasons: - jin kashetarom men phaaileriya aam baat hoti hai un kashetaron men jayaada samay tak rahane se snkaraman ka khatara barh jaata hai। ​ Treatments: phaaileriya se bachaav (Treatment of Elephantiasis) - machachharon se bachaav phaaileriya (Hathipaon) ko rokane ka ek paramukh upaay hai। kayoolekas machachhar jisake kaaran phaaileriya ka snkaraman phailata hai aam taur par shaam aur subah ke vakat kaatata hai। - kisi aise kashetar men jahn phaaileriya phaila hua hai vahn khud ko machachhar ke kaatane se bachaana chaahie। - aise kapare pahanen jinase pnv aur bnh poori tarah se dhak jaaen। - aavashayakata pare to perametharim yukat (perametharin ek aam sinthetik raasaayanik kitanaashak hota hai) kaparon ka upayog karen। baajaar men perametharin yukat kapare milate hain। - machachharom ko maarane ke lie kit sapare ka chhirakaav karen। - ilaaj bimaari ki paraarnbhik avasatha men hi shuroo ho jaana chaahie। Home Remedies: eliphentitis yaani shalipad javar ek parajivi ke kaaran phailati hai jo ki machachhar ke kaatane se sharir ke ndar paravesh karata hai। is bimaari se marij ke pair haathi ke pairon ki tarah phool jaate hain। is rog ke hone se n keval shaaririk vikalngata ho sakati hai balaki marijon ki maanasik aur aarathik sathiti bhi bigar sakati hai। parabhaavit karata hai। phaaileriya ke upachaar ke lie yahn ham aapako kuchh ghareloo aur aayuravedik nusakhe bata rahe hain, jinake isatemaal se aap nishachay hi laabh utha paaemge। 1. laung (Laung or Clove)- laung phaaileriya ke upachaar ke lie bahut parabhaavi ghareloo nusakha hai। laung men maujood enjaaim parajivi ke panapate hi use khatam kar dete hain aur bahut hi parabhaavi tarike se parajivi ko rakat se nashat kar dete hain। rogi laung se taiyaar chaay ka sevan kar sakate hain। 2. kaale akharot ka tel (Black walnut oil)- kaale akharot ke tel ko ek kap garam paani men tin se chaar boonde daalakar piem। is mitaran ko din men do baar piya ja sakata hai। akharot ke ndar maujood gunon se khoon men maujood kiron ki snkhaya kam hone lagati hai aur dhire dhire ekadam khatam ho jaati hai। jalad parinaam ke lie kam se kam chhah haphate paratidin is upaay ko karen। 3. bhojan (Food)- phaaileriya ke ilaaj ke lie apane roj ke khaame men kuchh aahaar jaise lahasuna, anaanaasa, mithe aaloo, shakarakndi, gaajar aur khubaami aadi shaamil karen। inamem vitaamim e hota hai aur baikataririya ko maarame ke lie vishesh gun bhi hote hain। 4. nvala (Amla)- mvala men vitaamin si parachur maatara men hota hai। isamen enathelaminthink (Anthelmintic) bhi hota hai jo ki ghaav ko jaladi bharane men behad laabhaparad hai। nvala ko roj khaane se inphekashan door rahata hai। 5. ashavagndha (Ashwagandha)- ashavagndha shilaajit ka mukhay hisasa hai, jisake aayuraved mem bahut se upayog hain। ashavagndha ko phaaileriya ke ilaaj ke lie bhi isatemaal kiya jaata hai। 6. baraahami (Brahmi)- baraahami puraane samay se hi bahut si bimaariyon ke ilaaj ke lie isatemaal ki jaati hai। phaaileriya ke ilaaj ke lie baraahami ko pisakar usaka lep lagaaya jaata hai। rojaana aisa karane se rogi soojam kam ho jaati hai। 7. adarak (Ginger)- phaaileriya se nijaat ke lie sookhe adarak ka paaudar ya sonth ka roj garam paani se sevan karen। isake sevan se sharir mem maujood parajivi nashat hote hain aur marij ko jaladi thik hone men madad milati hai। 8. shnkhapushapi (Shankhpushpi)- phaaileriya ke upachaar ke lie shnkhapushapi ki jar ko garam paani ke saath pisakar pesat taiyaar karen। is pesat ko parabhaavit sathaan par lagaaen। isase soojan kam hone men madad milegi। 9. kulathi (Kulthi)- kulathi ya haoras garaam (Horse Gram) men chintiyon davaara nikaali gai mitati aur nde ki saphedi milaakar parabhaavit sathaam par lagaaen। is lep ko paratidin parabhaavit sathaan par lagaaen, soojan se aaraam milegaa। 10. agar (Agarwood)- agar ko paani ke saath milaakar lep taiyaar karen। is lep ko paratidin 20 minat ke lie din men do baar parabhaavit sathaan par lagaaem। isase ghaav jaladi bharate hain aur soojan kam hoti hai। ghaav mem maujood baikatiriya bhi mar jaate hain। 11. raok saalat (Rock Salt)- shnkhapushapi aur saunth ke paaudar men raok saalat milaakara, ek ek chutaki roj do baar garam paani ke saath len। Disease: apach (Indigestion) Description: khaana imsaan ke lie behad bhojan karen। - man men karodha, irashayaa, tanaava, aadi nakaaraatamak vichaarom ko bilakul n aame den। man ke vichaaron ka sidha parabhaav pet par parata hai। Home Remedies: inadaaijeshan ya apach ki samasaya ko chikitasiy bhaasha men daayasepasiya (Dyspepsia) kaha jaata hai। apach ki samasaya pet men bhojan ko pachaane vaale rason ke sataravit n hone se hoti hai। yah samasaya khaasakar bahut tej masaale vaala khaana ya bahut tailiy khaana khaane se hoti hai। yadi aap bhookh se jayaada kha lete hain tab bhi aapako apach ki samasaya ho sakati hai। apach ke dauraan vayakati ko bahut jayaada gaisa, ulati, pet men darada, sine ya pet men jalan aadi samasayaaen ho sakati hain। apach se raahat ke lie kuchh ghareloo upaay laabhakaari saabit hote hain। aaie jaanate haim aise hi parabhaavi ghareloo nusakhon ke baare men- 1. seb ka siraka (Apple cider vinegar) seb ke sirake men yoon to esidik gun hote hain lekin yah esid se raahat dene men bhi parabhaavi hai। apach se raahat ke lie ek chamamach kachache aur anaphilatarad seb ke sirake ko ek kap paani men milaaen। isake baad isamen ek chamamach kachacha shahad milaaen। is pey ko din men do se tin baar pien। apach se raahat milegi। 2. saunph (Saunf) apach se bachaav ke lie saunph bhi behad gunakaari hai। bahut masaaledaar aur vasa vaale khaane se hone vaali apach ko behad jaladi thik kar deti hai। apach se bachaav ke lie saumph ke daanon ko tave par halaka sa garam karem aur usaka paaudar bana len। paani ke saath is paaudar ko din men do baar len। saunph ke daanon se taiyaar chaay ya saunph ko yoon hi munh men daalakar chabaane se bhi apach se raahat milati hai। saath hi yah maauth phareshanar ki tarah kaam bhi karati hai। 3. adarak (Ginger) adarak mem maujood paachan ras aur enjaaim khaame ko pachaane mem behad laabhakaari hain। apach se raahat ke lie adarak ke chhote chhaate tukaron par namak daalakar unahen yoon hi chabaaya ja sakata hai। isake alaava do chamamach adarak ke ras men ninboo ka rasa, thora sa kaala aur thora sa saphed namak milaakar bina paani ke pine se behad raahat milati hai। isake alaava adarak ke ras aur shahad ko gumagune paani ke saath bhi liya ja sakata hai। adarak ki chaay bhi behad laabhakaari hoti hai। itana hi nahin khaana banaane men adarak ka parayog masaale ke taur par karane se bhi adarak behad laabh deta hai। 4. beking soda (Baking Soda) apach se bachane ke lie beking soda sabase aasaan ghareloo upaay hai। aadhe gilaas paani men thoda sa beking soda milaakar is paani ko pien। isase turnt raahat milati hai। 5. ajavaayan (Ajwain) ajavaayan pet ko duroosat rakhane aur khaane ko pachaane ke saath hi pet darad se bhi raahat deti hai। saunth aur ajavaayan ko milaakar paaudar banaaen। ek chamamach paaudar men kaali mirach milaaen aur garam paani ke saath pien। is pey ko din men ek ya do baar pi sakate hain। ajavaayam ke daanon ko munh men rakhakar chabaane se bhi aaraam milata hai। 6. harabal chaay (Herbal Tea) pudima ya kaimomaail ki harabal ya garin ti bhi paacham shakati ko duroosat rakhati hai। khaana khaane ke baad ek kap harabal ti pine se khaana jaladi pachata hai aur pet men vasa bhi jama nahin hoti। aise mem aapaka vajan bhi thik rahata hai। lekin khaane ke baad saamaanay chaay ya kaophi se bachana chaahie। 7. namakin chhaachh (Salted Buttermilk) khaane ke saath namakin chhaachh ka isatemaal bhi aapaki paachan shakati ko barhaata hai। raat ke samay dahi ki jagah chhaachh mem kaala namak aur bhuna hua jira daalakar pien। pet men jalan se bhi raahat milegi। itama hi nahin subah maashate men aur dopahar ke khaane men bhi chhaachh ka isatemaal saravotatam hai। garamiyom ke dinom mem yah pet ke saath hi poore sharir ke lie bhi phaayademmd hai। Disease: ghutanon ka darad (Knee Pain) Descriptiom: ghutama sharir ka sabase bara tatha jatil jor hai। yah ek saayanoviyal jor (Sinovial Joint) ka udaaharan haim। is jor men mukhayat chaar hadadiyon, lagabhag 15 mnsapeshiyon ke alaava ek aur mahatatavapooran chiz hoti hai jise ghutane sakhat ho jaate hain, unamen chatakhan hoti hai aur kabhi-kabhi ghutanon men soojan bhi a jaati hai। - ghutanon men darad honaa। - mnsapeshiyon ki kamajori tatha jakaran se jor ek taraph ko jhuk jaata hai, tnge terhi home lagati hain v unaka elaainament bigar jaata hai, jisase joron ke ghisane ki parakariya kaaphi tej ho jaati hai tatha rogi ki chaal daradabhari tatha bedhngi ho jaati ka bharapoor sevan karen। inamem entiaukasident bharapoor maatara men hote hain। - ghutanon ko morakar nahin baithana chaahie। pet ko saaph rakhen tatha kabaj m hone den। - ghutanon ke niche athava khaane par bhi pet bhara paratit homa - kisi kaaray ko karane ki ichachha nahin hona - khaana khaane ki ichachha n hona - khoon ki kami hona - chehara kntihin evn kaala par jaana - jayaada payaas lagama - thodi sa kaam karane par thakaan hona - maanasik ashnti se garasat hona - munh men garami evn munh se badaboo aana - sharir ke vajan men dina-ba-din kami hote jaana - sookhi dakaaren aana - hariday ke samip lagaataar jalan hona Reasons: enorekasiya ke shaaririk kaaranon (Physical Reason of Hunger Disorder): - paachan tntar men garabari hone ke kaaran jibh men kisi bhi parakaar ka savaad n hona - bukhaar honaa, visham javar (maleriyaa) ke baad - jigar tatha aamaashay ki kharaabi - pet saaph n rahana yaani kabaj hona - amiyamit dhng se aahaar karana - der tak jaaganaa, subah der se uthana - bhojan ka savaadishat n hona - bhookh kam karane vaale aahaar ka sevan - chaaya-kaophi ka adhik sevan karanaa, aadi Treatments: - gehoon ke chokar men sendha namak aur ajavaayam milaakar roti banaakar khaane se bhookh tej hoti hai। - ek seb ya seb ke ras ke paratidin sevan se khoon saaph hota hai aur bhookh bhi lagati hai। - ek gilaas paani men jiraa, hinga, pudinaa, kaalimirach aur namak daalakar pine se aruchi door hoti hai। - paratidin methi men chhaunki gai daal ya sabazi ke sevan se bhookh barhati hai। - ninboo ko kaatakar isamen sendha namak daalakar bhojan se pahale choosane se kabaj door hokar paachamakariya tej ho jaati hai। Home Remedies: bhojan men aruchi ko emorekasiya (Anorexi Nervosa) bhi kahate hain। kai logom ko apane vajam aur phitanes ki itani chinta ho jaati hai ki vo haarash daayating karane lagate hain aur phir shuru ho jaati hai enorekasiya ki bimaari। isamen sharir ka vajan kaaphi kam ho jaata hai। sharir men hadadi aur mnsapeshiyon par ki jami vasa lagaataar bhookhe rahane se jalane lagati hai aur sharir men siraph hadadi ka rhncha hi shesh rah jaata hai। emorekasiya ki bimaari khaasakar maodaling aur phaishan indasatari men kaam kar rahi kam umar ki larakiyon men jayaada hota hai, kayonki unahem samaarat aur phit dikhame ke lie 'jiro phigara' jaisi kaaya banaani parati hai। lekin baad mem yahi jiro phigar unake lie jaanaleva ban jaati hai। enorekasiya bimaari ke baad n aapako bhookh lagati hai aur n hi kisi chij men ruchi। is bimaari ke baad aap khud ko bhaavanaatamaka, manovaijanyaanika, saamaajik aur shaaririk rup se itana asurakashit mahasoos karane lagate hain ki aapamen khudakushi karane tak ki bhaavana parabal ho jaati hai। enorekasiya ka yadi sahi samay par ilaaj nahin ho to isake kaaphi gnbhir parinaam hote hain, masalana- haarat ki bimaari, sharir men ilekatarolaaitas ka asntulana, jaanaleva enimiyaa, kidani kharaab hone se jaan tak ja sakati hai। akasar kai logon ko pata hi nahin chalata hai ki unahen enorekasiya ki bimaari hai। agar yah pata chal jaae to kai ghareloo upachaar aur manauvaijamyaanik upachaar se isaka ilaaj snbhav hai। khaasakar ghareloo upachaar se marijon mem khaame ke parati ruchi to paida ki hi jaati hai। emorekasiya ke ghareloo upachaar (Home Remedies for Anorexia) lahasun (Garlic) lahasun bhookh jagaane ki sabase kaaragar ghareloo upaay hai। ise khaane ke baad ek khaas tarah ke enjaaim ka saraav hota hai jo bhookh jagaata hai aur paachan kariya ko majaboot karata hai। roj subah kachache lahasun ke tin aur chaar daane ek kap paani ke saath kha len। agar kachacha lahasum khaane men karava lagata hai to use ubaal kar usamen namak aur ninboo ke ras mila kar bhi kha sakate hain। adarak (Ginger) bhookh jagaame ke lie aap aadha chamamach kate hue adarak kaala namak ke saath khaana khaane se aadha ghnte pahale khaaen, kaaphi kaam karegaa। ise isatemaal karen। aap khaane ko na nahin kar sakate hain ise leme ke baada। aap adarak ke chaay ka bhi sevan kar sakati hain। sntara (Oramge) sntaron men bhi bhookh jagaane ki kashamata hoti hai। sntara n siraph aapake paachan tntar ko thik karata hai balaki isase kabaj bhi door hota hai। ise jab man kare chaara-chhah phmk chhilakar khaate rahen। ise kaale namaka, ninboo ke ras ke saath bhi kha sakati hain ya phir joos bhi pi sakate hain। mimt (Mint) mint bhookh lagaane ki kudarati dava hai। enorekasiya ke ilaaj men ise aajamaaya ja sakata hai। isake savaad aur khaas sugndh ke kaaram bhookh ki ichachha jagati hai। ise khaane se dipareshan aur tanaav bhi kam hogi। do chamamach mint ke patate se nikaale joos roj subah pien ya phir mint se bami chaay bhi pi sakati hain। leman baam (Lemon Balm) yah narav taonik ki tarah kaam karata hai aur isase bhookh bhi lagati hai। ise khaane se tamaav kam hota hai aur nind bhi achachhi aati hai। ek chamamach leman baam ki sookhi patatiyon ko ek kap garam paami men daalen aur ise thori der rhnk den। thndha hone par ise chaay ki tarah pien। kaaphi kaam karegaa। harabal chaay (Herbal Tea) harabal chaay ya garin ti aur kai tarah ke jari-bootiyon ko mila kar bani chaay pine se bhookh jagati hai। tanaav aur dipareshan kam hoti hai। enorekasiya men harabal ti pine ki salaah di jaati hai। masaaj (Massage) masaaj therepi siraph tanaav aur dipareshan hi nahin door karati hai balaki isase bhookh bhi lagati hai। medikal jaranal men enorekasiya ke ilaaj men masaaj therepi ko bhi medisin ke rup men shaamil kiya gaya hai। kisi sapa men jaakar harabal masaaj tarend masaajar se len, kaaphi phaayada karegaa। yog (Yoga) enorekasiya bimaari se paida hui bhaavanaatamak asurakasha ko door bhagaata hai yoga। yog men aise kai aasan hain khaasakara- kapotaaasama(kabootar ke samaana), shalabhaaasana। ise karane se aap bahut jalad thik ho sakati hain। ekayoopnkachar aur ekayoopareshar (Acupumcture and Acupressure) ekayoopnkachar aur ekayoopareshar donon ki madad se enorekasiya se lari ja sakati hai। ise aajamaane se aapako achachha anubhav hoga aur rilaikas mahasoos karenge। kisi khaas narav par ekayoopnkachar ya ekayoopareshar karane se bhookh bhi lagame lagati hai। dhayaan (Meditation) man ki ashnti enorekasiya ka khaas lakashan hai। ise bhagaane ke lie subaha-shaam dhayaan karen। man aur aatama ko shnti milegi aur man men sakaaraatamak vichaar aaenge। aur bhi hain kai tipas (Some more tips) niyamit rup men garup therepi men shaamil ho। apana ek daait palaan banaaen aur is par amal karen, isase bhaage nahin। subah nishachit rup se naashata karen, ise apani aadat men shaamil karen। hari sabajiyon aur hare saag ke soop bana kar pien। bhookh jagaane ke lie masaaledaar bhojan khaana shuru karen। Disease: darad (Pain) Description: darad ya pira (About Paim im Hindi) Reasons: darad ke kai kaaran hote hain jaise chot lagamaa, pooraani bimaari aadi। darad (dard) ke kuchh vishesh kaaran niman hain: - kainsar - kaan men snkaraman - achaamak bimaari - mnsapeshi ki chot - jalana - puraama darad poorav ki kisi chot ya shaaririk nukasaan men bhi hota hai Treatments: ​darad hone par sabase aasaan upaay log darad nivaarak lema samajhate hain। kai baar darad nivaarak bhi pooran roop se darad khatam nahin kar paataa। darad ki sathiti men kuchh niman upaay apanaae ja sakate hain। - darad ke nidaan evn upachaar (Diagnosis and Treatment) ka udadeshay rogi ki kaarayaparanaali men sudhaar karana hai jisase ve apane dainik kaam kar saken। - chot ya joron ke darad men raahat ke lie thmda ya garam senk karana aasaan upaay maana jaata hai। - thmda senk - baraph hamaare sharir ki rakat vaahikaaon ko sikor deti hai। jisase hamen darad v jalan se hamem chhutakaara milane ke saath hi chot thik ho jaati hai। thnda senk keval taaja chot ke samay hi karana chaahie। yadi chot lage 6-7 ghnte ho chuke hain to thmde senk se bachana chaahie। lil parane se rokane v joron men aaraam milata hai। - garam paani ka senk bahut adhik saradi ke mausam mem karana phaayademnd hota hai। garami ke mausam men garam senk nahin karana chaahie। saradi ke mausam men joron par sathit nasen sikurane lagati hain। aise men garam paami ke senk se darad paida karame vaale utatak aur nasen khul jaati hain। - gnbhir choton men garam semk n len। yah chot men ho rahi jalan ko aur barha hai jo darad ko m siraph kam karati hai balaki jar se hi khatam kar deti hain। darad ke ghareloo ilaaj (Home Remedies for Pain) kamar darad (Pain in Waist) raat men 60 garaam genhoo ke daane paani men bhigo den। subah men bhige hue gemhoo ke saath 30 garaam khasakhas tatha 30 garaam dhamiya milaakar baarik pis len। is chatani ke doodh men paka le aur khir bana len। is khir ko lagaataar do mahine Pain) subah ke samay methidaana ka baarik chooram ek ya do chamamach paani ke saath len, ghutanon ka darad khatam ho jaaegaa। machhali ke tel (qaod livar auyala) bhi ghutanon ke darad men kaaphi asaradaar hai। subah bhookhe pet akharot ki giriyn khaaen। darad se mijaat milegaa। ghutanom ka darada, joron ka darad hadadiyon ko ghisane ke kaan hoti hai। isamen vijayasaar ki lakari ke vidhivat isatemaal se kaaphi aaraam milata hai। ek kachacha lahasun khaali pet paani ke saath khaaen, darad se nijaat milegaa। ashavagndha aur saunth ko kootakar isake chooran ko khaaen, kaaphi aaraam milegaa। garaare karane se bhi darad kam hoti hai। dmt ka darad (Paim in Teeth and Gum) sarason ke tel ki kuchh boondon men ek chutaki saimdha namak ke saath ek chutaki pisi hui haladi mila li jaae aur gaarha hai vahn haladi ka chooram aur choona mila kar laga diya jaae to phauram darad thik ho jaati hai aur soojan bhi kam ho jaati hai। Disease: anidara (Insomnia) Description: achachhi nind achachhe shaaririk ya maanasik ya donon tarah ke ho sakate hain। aaiyen jaamem anidara ki kuchh khaas vajahon ko: Treatmemts: nind aane ki samasaya se nijaat paane ke lie akasar log nind ki goliyon ka sevam aati hai। Disease: haraniya (Hernia) Description: haraniya (Hernia) mem pet ki mnsapeshiyn kamajor ho jaati hain aur usi kamajor jagah se nten baahar nikal aati hain। yah samasaya purushon v mahilaaon donon men ho sakati hai, kinatu purushon men adhik paai jaati hai। adhiknsh maamalon men purushon men haraniya kamar ke bhaag men hota hai। yah kamar ki mnsapeshiyon men kamazori aane par hota hai। Symptoms: - kisi bhaari vasatu ke uthaane par pet men soojan ka ubhar aanaa, - pet ki charabi ya nton ka baahar ki or nikalanaa, - pet ke michale bhaag men ubhaar ya soojan mahasoos hona - pet men phulaavata, darad aur bhaaripana, - mala-mootar tayaagane men pareshaani - lnbe samay tak khare rahane ya baithame men darad mahasoos honaa, Reasons: - paidaaishi taur par - barhati umar - chot lagana yadi kahin par adhik samay tak khara rahana ho to apani sathiti ko badalate rahen। - daayen-baayen ya pichhe dekhane ke lie garadan ko jayaada ghumaane ke bajaay sharir ko ghumaaen। - der tak daraaiving karani ho to garadam aur pith ke lie takiya rakhen। daraaiving sit ko kuchh aage ki or rakhen, taaki pith sidhi rahe। - adhik uncha ya mota takiya n lagaaem। saadhaaran takie ka isatemaal behatar hota hai। - atayadhik mulaayam aur sakhat gadade par n soen। saparingadaar gadadom ya dhile nivaar vaale palmg par sone se bhi bachen। - pet ke bal ya ulate hokar n soen। - parnparaagat tarikon se aaraam n pahunche to sarajari hi ekamaatar vikalap hai। lekin sarajari hogi ya nahin, yah niranay poori tarah visheshajany ka hota hai। Home Remedies: kamar ki mnsapeshiyon ka asntulit hona hi kamar darad ka kaaran hota hai। kamar darad sahi tarah se m uthane-baithane, sone ya kamar par kashamata se adhik dabaav parame se hota hai। lagabhag 80 % log kabhi n kabhi kamar darad se pareshaan hote hain। kamar darad naya bhi ho sakata hai aur puraana bhi ho sakata hai। satahi taur par dekhame par kamar men hone vaala darad bhale hi ek saamaamay si sathiti lagati hai, lekim ise nazarndaaj karane se samasaya kaaphi barh sakati hai। jaamie kamar darad door karane ke ghareloo nusakhe (Home Remedies for Back Pain): 1. ghutane moren (Band knee)- niche rakhi koi vasatu uthaate vakat pahale apane ghutane moren phir us vasatu ko uthaaen। aisa karane se kamar par anaavashayak dabaav nahin parega aur kam takaliph hogi। 2. lahasun (Garlic)- bhojam men lahasun ka parayaapat upayog karem। lahasun kamar darad ka achachha upachaar maana gaya hai। lahasun ke parayog se puraane se puraana kamar darad bhi thik hone lagata hai। 3. googul (Benzoin)- googul kamar darad men behad raahat deta hai। kamar darad men upachaar ke lie googul ki aadha chamamach garam paani ke saath subaha-shaam sevam karen। aisa karane se kamar darad men aaraam milata hai। 4. masaala chaay (Tea)- chaay banaane men 5 kaalimirach ke daane, 5 laung pisakar aur thora sa sookhe adarak ka paaudar daalen। dim me do baar is tarah ki masaala chaay pien। masaala chaay pite rahane se kamar darad men laabh hota hai। 5. sakhat bisatar (Tough Bedding)- sakhat bisatar par sone se bhi kamar darad men behad aaraam milata hai। aisa karame se kamar samatal rahati hai aur poori kamar par samaan dabaav parata hai। aundhe munh pet ke bal sona bhi haanikaarak hai। 6. daalachimi (Cinnamon)- 2 garaam daalachini ka paaudar ek chamamach shahad men milaakar din men do baar lete rahane se kamaradarad men raahat milati hai। 7. sharir ko garam rakhen (Warm Body)- kamar darad puraana ho to sharir ko garam rakhen aur garam vasatuen khaaen। aisa karane se kamar darad men behad raahat milati hai। saradiyon men darad jayaada ho to dhayaan rakhen ki darad vaala hisasa hava ke snparak men n aae। 8. baraph ki sikaai (Ice Foment)- darad vaali jagah par baraph ka parayog karana bhi laabhakaari upaay hai। isase bhitari soojan bhi samaapat hogi। kuchh roj baraf ka upayog karane ke baad garam sikaai paraarnbh kar dene se anukool parinaam aate hain। 9. paushatik bhojan (Proper Nutrition)- bhojan me tamaatara, gobhi, chukndara, khiraa, kakari, paalaka, gaajara, falon ka parachur maatara men upayog karen। 10. bhaap ki sikaai (Steam Foment)- namak mile garam paani men ek tauliya daalakar nichor len। pet ke bal letakar darad ke sathaan par tauliye davaara bhaap lene se kamar darad men raahat milati hai। 11. maalish (Massage)- roj subah sarason ya naariyal ke tel men lahasun ki tina-chaar kaliyn daalakar (jab tak lahasun ki kaliyn kaali n ho jaayen) garam kar len phir thnda kar parabhaavit jagah par maalish karen। 12. namak (Salt)- karhaai men do-tin chamamach namak daalakar ise achachhe se sek len। thore mote sooti kapare mem yah garam namak daalakar potali bndh lem। kamar par isake davaara sek karen। Disease: sine men darad (Chest Pain) Description: sine men darad ( Chest Pain) ki baat aate hi ham dil ke daure (Heart Attack) ki baat sochane lagate hain, magar sine men darad kai kaaranon se ho sakata hai। phephare, mnsapeshiyn, pasali, ya mason men bhi koi samasaya utapanan hone par sine men darad hota hai। le jaati hai usamen jab rakat ka chaap barh jaata hai tab sine men darad hota hai aur is avasatha ko uchach rakatachaap (Pulmonary Hypertension) kahate hain। esiditi (Acidity): yah saadhaaranat hai, sms lene men takaliph hone lagati hai aur rakat chaap barh jaane ke kaaran bhi hariday men rakat snchaar ki gati ko nukasaan pahunchata hai, in sab kaaranon se bhi sine men darad hota hai। vayaayaam sharir ke lie upayukat ho us vayaayaam ko jaroor karen, jaise- tej kadamon se chalanaa, sirhiyn charhanaa, baidamintan ya tenis khelana aadi। - aahaar men phaaibar ki maatara ko barhaaen aur kailori ki maatara ko kam karen। - khaane men namak ki maatara ko kam karem aur agar ho sake to bilakul chhor den। - dhoomarapaan hariday snbndhi bimaari ko barhaane men aham bhoomika nibhaata hai। ath isako chhorana phaayademnd hai। Home Remedies: sine men darad (Chest Pain) hamesha haarat ataik ka maamala mahin hotaa। sine ya chhaati men darad ke aur bhi kai kaaram ho sakate hain। esiditi, jayaada jor parata hai। yahn ham aapako kuchh ghareloo nusakhom se mnsapeshiyom ke darad ka ilaaj bataaenge lekin asahaniy ho aur jayaada pira ho rahi ho to daokatar ke paas jaana hi behatar upaay hai। kuchh ghareloo nusakhe niman hain- 1. epasam saolat (Epsom salt) garam paani ki ek baalati men ya tab men ek kap epasam namak daal kar parabhaavit sathaan ko is paani men takariban 15 minat ke milaakar parabhaavit sathaan par lagaana chaahie। 6. cheri joos (Cherry juice) masal pen se raahat ke lie cheri joos bhi pina chaahie। cheri joos pine se masalas ka khinchaav kam hota hai saath hi yah mnsapeshiyon ko raahat bhi deta hai। 7. masaaj (Massage) masaaj karane se sharir ka rakatasmchaar behatar hota hai jo ki darad ko teji se thik karane men madad karata hai। yadi masaaj karane ke lie achachhe telon ka parayog kiya jaae to asar doguna ho jaata hai। 8. mirach (Chilli) mirach men maujood kaipasesin (capsaicin) bhi darad ki khaas dava hai। baajaar men mirach se taiyaar kai tarah ki isake baad isamen elovera jel milaaen। is tarah se taiyaar utapaad ko yadi parabhaavit sathaan par lagaakar halake haath se maalish ki jaae to behad aaraam milata hai। 9. aaraam (Rest) kai baar kuchh n karake siraph aaraam karana bhi sharir ko bahut laabh de sakata hai। yadi sharir men akaran mahasoos ho to kam se kam do din aapako sharir ko poori tarah aaraam dena chaahie। isase sharir halaka mahasoos karata hai aur tanaav kam hota hai jisaka sidha asar mnsapeshiyom par bhi parata hai। Disease: parosatet kainsar (Prostate Cancer) Description: parosatet kainsar purushon ko hota hai। ye kaimsar shurooaati daur men pata chal jaae, to aasaani se thik kiya ja sakata hai। Symptoms: - koolahe (hipasa), jngh ki hadadiyn (thaaija) v pith men lagaataar darad hona - peshaab karate samay darad v jalan hona - peshaab karane men dikakat hona - baar baar peshaab jaanaa, khaasakar raat men - viray ya mootar mem khoon aana - sekas ke dauraan viray nikalate vakat darad hona - sekas ke samay ling snbhaavana ko barhaata hai। 50 saal ki umar paar kar rahe logon men yah bahut teji se phailata hai। parosatet kainsar (Prostate Cancer) ke har 3 men se 2 marijon ki umar 65 ya usase jayaada hoti hai। se muenh aur phephare ka kaimsar to hota hai, lekin dhoomarapaan parosatet kainsar ko bhi barhaata hai। Treatments: parosatet kainsar ka bachaav (Treatment of Prostate Cancer) Home Remedies: parosatet kainsar (Prostate cancer) buhat jayaada sunane men nahi aata lekin yah ek khataranaak bimaari hai। haalnki isaka ilaaj snbhav hai। ek umar ke baad aadamiyon men parosatet savabhaavik roop se barh jaate hain। 50 ki umar ke baad lagabhag 40 phisadi purooshon men parosatet kainsar ki smbhaavanaaen ho jaati hain। haalnki yah jaanaleva ho aisa nahin hai lekim ek sathiti ke baad yah khataranaak bhi ho jaata hai। yah jitane jayaada barhate hain inamen kainsar ka khatara bhi utana hi hota hai kayonki parosatet ke ndar maujood selas (jo kainsar ka barhaava dete hain) bhi parosatet ke saaij ke anusaar barhane lagate hain। isake lie kai ghareloo ilaaj bhi hain, jinahen apanaakar ham parosatet kainsar se bachaav kar sakate hain। 1. adarak (Gimger)- adarak ki jar parosatet kainsar se bachaav ke lie behad parabhaavi hai। adarak men entiphalemetari, entiaukasident aur entiparoliphiretiv (antiproliferative) gun hote hain jo kainsar ko barhaava dene vaale selas ko khatam kar dete hain। aise men adarak khaana parosatet kainsar se bachaav aur aaraam donon de sakata hai। 2. khoob pey padaarath piem (Drimk lots of fluid)- dhayaan rahe ki aapako dihaaidaresham n hone paae। isake lie m keval paami khoob pina hai balaki anay heladi pey bhi aapaki bahut sahaayata kar sakate hain। sabajiyon aur phalom ke joos ke saath hi heladi soop bhi behad phaayademnd hain। 3. tamaatar (Tomato)- tamaatar men ekativ tatav laaikopin (lycopene) hota hai jisake kaaran tamaatar mem entiaukasident (antioxidant) ki maatara bhi jayaada hoti hai। yah tatav kainsar ko phailane aur barhane se bhi rokata hai। upachaar ke lie kachacha tamaatar ya tamaatar ki saosa, chatani, kaichaap ya salaad aur sabaji ke roop men bhi khaaya ja sakata hai। 4. anaar (Pomegranate)- risarach men bhi saabit ho chuka hai ki parosatet kainsar se bachaane men anaar behad phaayademnd hain। yah ovar aal kaimsar se bhi bachaav karata hai। anaar men maujood tatav kainsar ko paida karane vaale selas ko maar dete haim jisase kainsar nahim hotaa। anaar ke daanon ko yoon hi khaaya ja sakata hai ya anaar ka joos nikaalakar bhi piya ja sakata hai। 5. kadadoo ke bij (Pumpkin seeds)- kadadoo ke bij dayooretik (diuretic) roop se kaaray karate hain jo ki kai bimaariyon men laabhakaari hain। khaasakar mootar aur parosatet se snbndhit rogon men behad laabhakaari hain। kadadoo ke bijon men bahut sa jimk (zinc) hota hai jo ki imayooniti barhaane men madad karata hai, jisase parosatet kainsar se teji se rikavari snbhav hoti hai। upachaar ke lie kadadoo ke bijon ko ikatatha karake unahen kachacha hi khaaen। isake alaava in bijon ki chaay banaakar bhi pi sakate hain। is chaay ko laabh hone tak rojaana pien। 6. soya (Soya)- soya men saayatosatarojan (phytoestrogen) hota hai jo ki tesatosatiron (testosterone) ka sataraav tej karata hai। is kaaran parosatet galaind men rakat snchaar tej hota hai jisase kainsar paida karane vaale selas ki snkhaya ghatati chali jaati hai। 7. vitaamin di (Vitamin D)- vitaamim di ki uchit maatara hone se parosatet kainsar hone ka khatara nahin rahataa। yah n keval parosatet kainsar se rakasha karata hai balaki hone ke baad isase upachaar bhi snbhav hai। phoratiphaaid (fortified) daalen aur thnde paani men rahane vaali machhaliyn vitaamim di ki achachhi satarot hoti hain। isake saath hi aap vitaamin di 3 ke sapaliment bhi le sakate haim। 8. garin ti (Green tea)- garin ti ek aisi harab hai jisamen bahut se gun hote hain aur yah parosatet kainsar ke upachaar men bhi sahaayak hai। garin ti men poliphinolas (polifenoles) uchit maatara mem hote hain jo kainsar paida karane vaale selas ko maar dete hain। 9. phaiti phish (Fatty fish)- phaiti phish omega 3 ki achachhi satarot hoti hai, jo ki kainsar se bachaav men sahaayak hai। isake alaava phalaik sid bhi omaga 3 ke achachhe satarot hote hain। sharir mem omega 3 ki maatara barhaane ke lie phish auyal ke kaipasool sapaliment ke roop men bhi lie ja sakate hain। Disease: haipetaaitis (Hepatitis) Description: livar sharir ka ek mahatatavapooran ng hai। vah bhojan pachaane men mahatatavapooran bhoomika nibhaata hai। sharir men hone vaali chayaapachay kariyaaon (Metabolic Process) men livar (Liver) vishesh sahaayata karata hai। Symptoms: - atayadhik kamajori v thakaan - nkha, jibha, mootar v tavacha men pilaapan - paachan samasayaaon jaise ulati - bhookh men kami - chirachiraapan Reasons: haipetaaitis ko saamaanayata: paami se honi vaali bimaari maana jaata hai jo poori tarah galat hai। daokataron ke anusaar niman kaaranon se bhi haipetaaitis ho sakata hai: haipetaaitis ke kaaran (Causes of Hepatitis) - aanuvnshika, - kuposhana, - sharaaba, - phaiti livar Treatments: haipetaaitis se bachaav ke lie saapha-saphaai behad aavashayak hai। khaane aur pime men hamesha saaph chijon ke parayog se isase bacha ja sakata hai। haipetaaitis se bachaav ke anay upaay niman hain: - livar ko savasath rakhane ke lie saapha-suthara bhojam aur saaph paani jaroori hai। - baahar ka khaana khaane se bachen, lekin khaana bhi pare to saapha-saphaai dekhakar hi khaaen। - haipetaaitis e (Hepatitis A Vaccine) ka tika jaroor lagavaana chaahie। - kisi doosare ki sui, rejar aur toothabarash isatemaal mahin karana chaahie। - rakat charhaane par is baat ka vishesh dhayaan rakhen ki mai sui ho aur rakat snkaramit n ho। - adhik tela, ghi, haladi aur mirach masaale ka bhojam n karem। - hari patatidaar sabajiyn khaaem, mausami aur ganane ka ras pien। - naariyal paani, chaavala, dahi ya chhaachha, ubale aaloo aur chhaine vaala rasagulala khaaen। - pila bukhaar - livar kainsar Home Remedies: hepetaaitis roga, livar men soojan aur jalan (inflammation) ke kaaram hota hai। livar sharir ko savasath rakhane men mahatavapooran kaaray karata hai। poshak tatavon ko satorej karane ke saath hi sharir mem uraja ke snchaar ko kntarol karana aur kolesataraol aadi ka niramaan bhi livar hi karata hai। livar yaani gurade mem pareshaami tab aati hai jab haanikaarak pey ya bhojan adhik maatara men khaaya jaata hai। sharaab ya anay nashile padaarath livar par bura asar daalate haim। isase imayoon sisatam bhi kamajor ho jaata hai। kai baar yah aanuvnshik samasaya bhi ho sakati hai। hepetaaitis ke lakashanon men pet ke daayim or ke hisase men bhaaripan lagata hai, piliya ho sakata hai, thakaavat mahasoos hoti hai tatha khujali hoti hai। hepetaaitis ka upachaar ghareloo saamagari se bhi snbhav hai lekin sathiti agar kaaboo men m aae to chikitasak ke paas jaana hi thik hota hai। aaie aapako bataate hain hepetaaitis ke upachaar ke lie kuchh ghareloo upaayon ke baare mem- 1. ajavaayan aur jira (Ajwain aur jeera) ek chamamach ajavaayan aur ek chamamach jira pisakar paaudar bana len। isamen ek chutaki namak milaaem। is chooran ko rojaana do baar khaaen। isase imayooniti barhegi aur hepetaaitis men aaraam hogaa। 2. likoris paaudar aur shahad (Liquorice powder and honey) ek bara chamamach likoris paaudar mem do chamamach shahad milaakar paratidin khaaen। hepetaaitis ke upachaar men yah bhi behad phaayademmd hai। isake saath hi likoris ki jar ko paani mem ubaalakar usaki chaay bhi banaai ja sakati hai। 3. lahasun (Garlic) lahasun rakat ko saaph karata hai aur sharir se vishaakat padaarathon ko baahar nikaalata hai aise men rojaama subah khaali pet lahasun ki ek se do kali chabaaen। saath hi khaana banaane men bhi lahasun ka parayog masaale ke roop men jaroor karen। 4. haladi (Haldi) haladi inaphalementari (inflammatory) gunon se bharapoor hoti hai। haladi ka isatemaal bhi hepetaaitis se rakasha kar sakata hai। haladi ko doodh men daalakar pine se bhi bahut laabh hota hai। haalnki piliya hone men haladi leme ki manaahi hoti hai। 5. kaali gaajar (Black carrot) kaali gaajar ke bhi bahut phaayade hain। vitaamin se bharapoor kaali gaajar se khoon ki kami poori hoti hai tatha rakat snchaar sudharata hai। hepetaaitis men bhi gaajar ko salaad ke roop men khaane se bahut phaayade hote hain। 6. garin ti (Green tea) garin ti yaani harabal chaay gunon se bharapoor hoti hai। garin ti men entiaukasident (antioxidant) hote hain jo sharir ke saath hi masatishak ko bhi savasath rakhate hain। hepetaaitis ke upachaar aur bachaav ke lie garin ti ko apani dinacharaya men shaamil karen। 7. nvala (Amla) nvala vitaamin si se bharapoor hota hai jo livar ko har tarah se phaayada pahunchaata hai। mvala ka parayog chayavanaparaash men bhi kiya jaata hai jisase imayooniti barhe aur paachan shakati majaboot ho। aise men nvala ka parayog dainik aahaar men bhi kiya ja sakata hai। nvala joosa, chatani, achaar aadi ko dainik aahaar men shaamil karen। 8. alasi ke bij (Flax seed) alasi ke bij sharir men haaramon ka sntulan donon banaae rakhate hain aur umahen rakat men sahi tarike se bhejane ka kaam bhi karate hain। phalaikas sid men saayatoknsatitayooentas (phytoconstituents) hote hain jo ki haaramon ki baainding ka kaam karate hain aur livar par atirikat bhaar nahin parane dete। phalaikas sid ko yoon hi tosat ke upara, salaad me ya daal aadi men daalakar khaaya ja sakata hai। yah livar ko majaboot banaane men sahaayak hai jisase hepetaaitis rog se bachaav hota hai। Disease: pile dnt (Yellow Teeth) Description: dnt siraph hamen bhojan chabaane men hi madad nahin karate, balaki hamaare vayakatitav ko bhi parabhaavit karate hain। saapha, savasath v sumdar dnt chehare ka aakarashan hote hain। lekin agar dnt pile ho to yah sharamindagi ka bhi kaaran ban sakate hain। Symptoms: - pile dmt Reasons: dnton men pilaapan aana hamaare galat rahana-sahan ke kaaran to kai baar saapha-saphaai na rakhane ke kaaram hota hai। kuchh anay kaaram bhi hain jinake kaaran dnt pile hote haim, jaise: pile dnton ka mukhay kaaran (Causes of Yellow teeth in Hindi) - tnbaakoo, gutakaa, sharaab aadi ke jayaada sevan karane se dnt pile ho sakate hain। - kuchh logon men umar barhane ke saatha-saath dnton par palaik ki parat charhati jaati hai। isase bhi dnt pile dikhane lagate haim। - jayaada maatar men chaaya, kaophi aur kolad darink ka sevan karame se bhi dnt pile hone lagate hain। - phalorosis : desh ke kai shaharon ke paani men phaloraaid ki maatara adhik hone ke kaaran dnton ka rng badarng ho jaata hai। unamen upar pile evm saphed chikatate dikhaai parate hain। Treatments: agar dnton ko saaph karane ke baad bhi dnton se pilaapan na jaae to nimam upachaar apanaame chaahie: - vahaaitanara, shaainar aur vishesh kemikalas ke jariye dnton ki chamak aasaani se lautaai ja sakati hai। - dental balichimg se dnton ka pilaapana, pile-laal dhababe, gutakaa, tnbaakoo aadi ke daag aasaami se khatam kie ja sakate hain। - pile dmton ko saphed karane ka ghareloo upachaara, beking soda hai। garam paani men beking soda mila kar usase kulala (Gargle) karen। jab munh se paani baahar nikaalen tab apane dnton ko umgaliyom se ragaren, isase dnt chamak jaaenge। - dnton ko savasath rakhane ke lie phaloraaid yukat toothapesat aur mulaayam barash se din men do baar dnt saaph karane ki aadat daalen। - isake saath jibh ki saphaai bhi karen, kayonki baikatiriya jayaadaatar yahin panapate hain। - din mem ek baar phalaos bhi karen। isase dnton ke bich phnse bhojan ke tukare nikal jaate hain। - adhik garam chijen n khaaen। - jayaada karak barisal vaale barash se dnt saaph n karen। - mnsaahaari khaana khaane ke baad kulala jaroor karen। isase dnton men phnse reshe bhi nikal jaaenge aur gndh bhi। - dnton men takaliph n ho, tab bhi saal men ek baar dnton ka chekaap jaroor karaaen। - kuchh bhi khaane-pine ke baad saaph paani se kulala karen। - jayaada puraana barash masooron aur dnton ko nukasaan pahuncha sakata hai, isalie har tin mahime men barash badal len। Home Remedies: saphed aur chamakate dnt kisi ki bhi parasaneliti men nikhaar la sakate hain। bahut se log pile dnton ke kaaran logon ke saamane hnsane se bachate hain ya munh par haath rakhakar hnsate hain। dnt jayaadaatar umar ke kaarana, dnton ki thik se saphaai n home ke kaarana, bahut jayaada chaay ya kaophi pine ke kaaran athava tnbaakoo aur sigaret pine ke kaaran pile ho jaate hain। kabhi kabhi kisi bimaari ke kaaran bhi dnt pile ho jaate hain। haalnki pile dnton ko saphed bamaana koi mushakil kaam nahin hai। thori si mehanat se aap pile dmtom ko saphed bana sakate hain। aaie aapako kuchh ghareloo musakhe bataate hain jo aapake dnto ki saphedi aur chamak ko banaae rakhenge। 1. beking sodaa- (Baking Soda) beking soda dnton ko saphed bamaane ka sabase aasaan tarika hai। yah dnton se palaak ko khatam karake dmton ki saphedi aur chamak banaae rakhata hai। kaise upayog karen - roj barash karate samay apane pesat men thora sa beking paaudar daalen aur barash karen। dnton ki saphedi laut aaegi। - ek kap paami men bekimg soda aur haaidarojam par aukasaaid (hydrogen peroxide) milaakar maauth vaosh (mouthwash) ki tarah bhi isatemaal kiya ja sakata hai। 2. sntare ka chhilakaa- (Peel of Orange) sntare ke chhilake se roj dnton ki saphaai karane se kuchh hi dinon men pile dnt chamakane lagenge। kaise upayog karen - roj raat ko sote samay smtare ke chhilake ko dmton par ragaren। sntare ke chhilake men vitaamin si (vitamin c) aur kailashiyam ke saath maaikaroauragenijam (micro organism) hota hai jo dnton ki majabooti aur chamak bamaae rakhata hai। 3. sataraoberi- (Strawberry) sataraoberi men bhi vitaamin si parachur maatara men hota hai jo ki dmtom ko saphed banaane men sahaayak hai। kaise upayog karen - sataraoberi ke kuchh tukaron ko pisakara, is lep ko dnton par lagaakar masaaj karem। ise din men do baar karame se kuchh hi dinon men pile dnt saphed hone lagate hain। - beking soda aur sataraoberi ke palap ko milaakar bhi dnton par ragarane se dnton ka pilaapan khatam hota hai। 4. ninboo- (Lemon) nimboo ke paraakaritik baliching (matural bleach) ke gun dnton par bhi asar dikhaate hain। pile dntom ke lie ninboo ke chhilake ko dnton par ragara ja sakata hai, ya ninboo ke paani se garaare bhi kie ja sakate haim। kaise upayog karen - ninboo ke saath namak milaakar dmton ki masaaj karen। - do haphaton tak rojaana do baar karane se dnt chamakane lagenge। 5. namaka- (Salt) namak ko puraane samay se hi dnto ki saphaai ke lie isatemaal kiya jaata raha hai। yah dnton ke khoe minaralas lautaata hai jisase dntom ka saphed rng bana rahata hai। kaise upayog karen - rojaana subah toothapesat ki tarah namak ko dntom ki saphaai ke lie isatemaal kiya ja sakata hai। namak ko chaarakol men milaakar bhi dnton ki saphaai ki ja sakati hai jisase dnt saphed hote haim। - namak aur beking paaudar milaakar bhi mnjan taiyaar kiya ja sakata hai। 6. tulasi- (Basil) tulasi men bhi dnton ko saphed banaane ka gun hota hai। isake saath hi tulasi paayariya aadi se bhi dnton ki rakasha karati hai। kaise upayog karem - tulasi ke pataton ko sukhaakar paaudar bana len। is paaudar ko rojaana isatemaal karane vaale toothapesat men milaakar dnton ki saphaai karen। - tulasi ke pataton ka pesat banaakar usamen sarason ka tel (mustard oil) milaaem। is pesat se dnton ki saphaai karane par bhi bahut phaayada hota hai। 7. seba- (Apple) seb ko daait men shaamil karane se bhi dnton ki saphedi lautaai ja sakati hai। seb ki karnchines dnton ko paraakaritik taur par sakarab karati hai। rojaana ek ya do seb jaroor khaaen aur khoob chaba chaba kar khaaen। isi tarah gaajar aur khira bhi kachacha khaane se dnt saphed tatha majaboot banate hain। Disease: ti. bi. (Tuberculosis) Description: tayoobarakayulosis (Tuberculosis) maayakobekatiriyam tayoobarakayulosis naamak jivaanu ke kaaran hota hai। ti.bi. rog ko amay kai naam se jaana jaata hai, jaise tapedika, kashay rog tatha yakashamaa। Symptoms: - agar aapaka vajana, bagair koshish kiye huye, pichhale 2 mahinon men, 5 kilogaraam se adhik ghat gaya hai - agar aapako khnsi men khoon aata hai - agar aapako khnsi men balagam aata hai - agar aapako tin haphate se adhik se khnsi hai - agar aapako bhookh kam lagati hai - agar aapako raat men adhik pasina aata hai - agar aapane apane balagam ka kabhi ti bi ka jnch karavaaya hai, jise pozitiv kaha gaya ho Reasons: tibi kai kaaranon se phailata hai lekin isake paramukh kaaranon men aparayaapat v apaushatik bhojana, kam jagah mem adhik logon ka rahanaa, gndagi, gaay ka kachacha doodh pina aadi hain। isake anay kaaran niman hain: tibi ke kaaran (Causes of Tuberculosis) - ti bi ke marij ke jahn-jahn thookane se isake vishaanu savasath vayakati ke sharir men paravesh karake use rogi bana dete hain। - kapara mil men kaam karane vaale sharamik ya reshe-roe ke smparak mem rahane vaale loga, - bunakara, dhool ke smparak mem rahane vaale log tatha ndheri kothariyon ya chaalon men rahane vaale log bhi is rog ka shikaar ho jaate hain। - madiraapaana, dhoomarapaan tatha rogagarasat pashu ka mns khaame vaale log bhi tibi ka shikaar ho sakate hain। - asaavadhaamivash rogi ka khoon anay kisi rog ke sharir men charhaane se vah vayakati rogagarasat ho jaata hai। Treatments: tibi ka upachaar (Treatment of Tuberculosis in Hindi) - yadi tin athava adhik sapataah se khnsi ho rahi ho to kaf ki do baar jnch karaaen। ye jnch sarakaari kaf sookashamadarashi kenadaron par ni:shulak ki jaati hai। - sabhi davaaon ko niyamit roop se, bataai gai poori avadhi tak len। - khnsate ya chhinkate samay roomaal ka parayog karen। Home Remedies: tibi yaani tayoobarakulosis (Tuberculosis), ek parakaar ka inphekashan hota hai jo ki maayakoikatiriyam tayoobarakulosis (mycobacterium tuberculosis) baikatiriya ke kaaran phailata hai। tibi adhikatar phephepharon mem hoti hai lekin yah sharir ke kisi bhi hisase mem ho sakati hai। tibi ke marij ke kaph men khoon aana tibi ka aam lakashan hai isake alaava smson ka tej chalamaa, vajan ka kam honaa, bukhaar honaa, kidani aur sine men darad hona aadi bhi tayoobarakulosis ke lakashan hain। vaise to tibi se poori tarah nijaat ke lie chikitasak se paraamarash aavashayak hai lekin kuchh ghareloo upachaaron ke davaara bhi tibi ko thik karane ki parakariya tej ki ja sakati hai। aaie aapako bataate hain tibi ke upachaar ke lie kuchh ghareloo nusakhe- 1. lahasun (Garlic)- lahasun men salaphayoorik esid (sulphuric acid) parachur maatara men hota hai jo ki tibi ke kitaanuom ko maarame men sakasham hai। isake saath hi lahasun men elisin (allicin) aur ejoini (agoeni) bhi hote haim jo ki tibi ke panapane vaale kitaanuon ka khatam karane ka kaam karate hain। itana hi nahin lahasun ke entibaikatiriyal gun imayooniti ko bhi barhaate hain। kaise karen upayog aadhi chamamach lahasuna, ek kap doodh aur chaar kap paani ko ek saath milaakar ubaalen। ise tab tak ubaalem jab tak yah misharan ek chauthaai rah jaae। is misharan ko din men tin baar pien। garam doodh men lahasun ka ras milaakar bhi piya ja sakata hai। isake baad paami m pien। garam doodh men lahasun ko ubaalen। isake baad lahasun ko chabaakar bache hue doodh ko pi len। 2. kela (Banana)- kela poshak tatavon aur kailashiyam ka bahut achachha satarot hai। yah tibi ke marij ka imayoon sisatam badhaane men sahaayak hai। isake saath hi bukhaar aur kaph se bhi raahat deta hai। kaise karen upayog ek pake hue kele ko ek kap maariyal ke paami men masalakar milaaen। isake baad isamen dahi aur shahad milaaen। ise din men do baar khaaen। kachache kele ka joos banaakar rojaana pien। kele ke tane ka joos banaakar bhi piya ja sakata hai। 3. nvala (Amla)- nvala men entiphalemetari (anti inflammatory) aur entibaikatiriyal (antibacterial) gum hote hain। jo sharir ka imayoon sisatam majaboot karake sharir ko uraja paradaan karate hain। kaise karen upayog nvala ke bij nikaalakara, joos banaaen aur isamen ek chamamach shahad milaakar subah subah pien। 4. sntara (Orange)- sntare men bhi jaroori minaralas (minerals) aur knpaaund (compound) hote hain। sntare men maujood salaain (salain) sharir ko inphekashan se bachaata hai saath hi imayoon sisatam ko majaboot karata hai। kaise karen upayog taaja sntare ke ras men thora sa namak aur shahad milaakar rojaana subah shaam pien। sntare ko chhilakar usaki salaais par bhi namak chhirak kar khaaya ja sakata hai। 5. sharipha (Custard apple)- tibi ke upachaar ke lie sharipha bhi behad phaayademnd hai। shariphe ka palap nikaalakar ise khaana chaahie। kaise karem upayog do shariphon ka palap nikaalakar use paani men ubaal len, isake saath pachachis kishamish (kishmish) ko bhi ubaal len। jab paani ek tihaai rah jaae tab ise chhaanakar isamen paaudar shugar milaaen। is pey men ilaayachi aur daalachini milaakar din men do baar pien। 6. kaali mirach (Black pepper)- kaali mirach phepharon (lungs) ki saphaai ka kaam karati hai। jisase tibi ke dauraan hone vaale sine ke darad se raahat milati hai। isake saath hi yah tibi ke kitaamuom ko maarame ka kaam bhi karati hai। kaise karen upayog makakhan men aath se das kaali mirach pharaai karem। isamem ek chutaki himg milaaen aur paaudar bana len। is misharan ko tin baraabar bhaagon mem bnt len। kuchh kuchh ghnte ke ntaraal par isaki ek ek doj khaaem। 7. akharot (Walnut)- akharot tibi ke marijon ko taakat deta hai, unaki imayooniti barhaata hai aur jaladi thik home men bhi madad karata hai। kaise karen upayog akharot ke paaudar men kuchh kali lahasun ki milaakar kuchal len। isamen kaleriphaaid makakhan (clarified butter) milaakar khaaen। akharot ko yoon bhi khaaya ja sakata hai ya isake paaudar ko salaad men daalakar khaaen। 8. pudina (Mint)- pudina men maujood entibaikatiriyal (antibacterial) gunon ke kaaran isamen bhi tibi ke rog ko thik karame ka adabhut gun hota hai। kaise karen upayog ek chamamach pudine ke ras men do chamamach shahad milaaen, isake saath hi is ghol men maalat vinegar (malt vinegar) aur aadha kap gaajar ka joos milaaen। is ghol ko kuchh kuchh ghnton par poore din pien। Disease: pharozan sholadar (Frozen Shoulder) Description: kndhe ka darad ek bahut hi aam shikaayat hai। aisa maana jaata hai ki kndhon ke aasapaas joron men soojan aane ke kaaran yah darad hota hai। aise darad men kabhi-kabhaar kndhe sunan bhi par jaate hain। yah sathiti kai baar mahinon tak rah jaati hai। Symptoms: - kndhon ka sunan par jaana - kndhon ko ghumaane men asamarathata mahasoos homa - raat men kndhon men tivar darad hona Reasons: - daayabitij ke marijom men, hariday samasaya se garasit logon men paarakisan bimaari ke marijon men ho sakati hai। - garadan men hone vaali saravaaikal disak ki samasaya bhi aise darad ka kaaran ho sakati hai। - vo marija, jinahen kndhon par kisi parakaar ki chot lagi ho ya kndhon ki kisi parakaar ki sarajari hui hai, unamen pharojan sholadar ki aashnka adhik hoti hai। Treatments: kndhon ki jakaran men akasar maalish ya senk se aaraam milata hai। agar isase aaraam nahim milata hai to niman upaay apamaane chaahie: - darad ko anadekha m karen। yah lagaataar ho to daokatar ko dikhaaen। - saamaanay kndhon ke darad men darad nivaarak davaaon se hi raahat mil jaati hai। aisa darad kndhon men soojan ke kaaran hota hai, isalie soojan kam karane vaali davaaen bhi raahat pahuncha sakati hain। lekin darad ki davaaon ka parayog keval aapaat sathiti men hi karen। - kndhon ko garam ya thnda sek den। - darad se jalad aaraam ke lie ekayoopnkachar chikitasa ka sahaara le sakate hain। - pharojam sholadar ki chikitasa ka sabase achachha upaay phijiyotherepi (Physiotherapy) maana jaata hai। phijiyotherepi men kndhon men khinchaav utapanan kar kndhon ko dobaara gatimaan banaana hota hai। aisa karane ke lie kndhom ke vibhinan binduon ko vayaayaam davaara dhire-dhire saamaanay sathiti men laane ka parayaas kiya jaata hai। - pharojan sholadar (Frozen Shoulder) ki chikitasa samay par nahim ki gai to marij ko poora jivan is samasaya ke saath bitaana par sakata hai। Disease: saravaaikal sapaonadilaaitis (Cervical Sypondolysis) Description: umar ke saath hadadiyon men ghisaav v badalaav a jaata hai। yah garadan ki hadadiyom men bhi hota hai। hadadiyom men ghisaava, amatar ho jaane ya inake jor vaale bhaag ki mnsapeshiyon men soojan se garadan ka darad yaami saravaaikal sapndaailosis (Cervical Spomdolysis) hota hai। yah sab garadan ki us hadadi men hota hai jise saravaaikal sapaain kahate hain। rirh ki hadadi ka garadan vaala yah bhaag merudanad (Spine) ki saat kasherookaaon (Vertebrae) evn unake madhay ki disak se banata hai। garadan ki 85 paratishat gatividhiyn upar ki do kasherookaaon ke kaaran hoti hai। garadan ke darad se hone vaali pareshaani isamen baadha pahunchaati hain। saravaaikal sapndaailosis pahale 40 varash se adhik aayu ke logon ko hota tha kinatu varatamaan samay ki jivanacharaya evm aajivika ne bachache aur baron sabhi ko garadan mem darad ka marij bana diya hai। Symptoms: - garadan men akarana, - garadan ghumaane men chat ki aavaaj aana - garadan ghumaane men dikakat - chakakar aana - darad v bhaaripan - nason men khinchaav se haathom men knpan aadi lakashan dikhate hai - sir ke pichhe bhaag men darad - haathon ka sunan par jaanaa, jaan n rahana Reasons: - sote samay mote takie ka upayog isaka ek kaaran hai। - baithane ki galat sathiti ke kaarana, lnbe samay tak ek jaisi sathiti men baithanaa। knpayootar par jayaada der tak kaam karame vaale vayakati, dnt chikitasaka, vaahan chaalaka, helamet dhaarak aadi ko yah anay logon ki apekasha jayaada hota hai। - vidayaarathi evm aise vayakati jo bhaari baig pith ya kmdhe par latakaae rahate hain, ve isase pirit hote hain। - kisi chot ya pharaikachar ke kaaran yah darad hota hai। - kuchh anay rogon men bhi yah darad parakat hota hai। - ek jaisi sathiti men lagaataar tivi, knpayootara, vidiyo gem aadi ke upayog se hota hai। Treatments: - garadan evn kndhe ka vayaayaam miyamit karen। - sahi sathiti men baithen। - pair jamin par evn pith kurasi ke parishath bhaag par sidhi rakhen। - jhukakar ya ek jaisi sathiti men lagaataar kaam n karen। - bicha-bich men kndhe, garadan ko ghumaaen। - mote takie v masanad ka upayog kam ya bnd kar den। - garadan ke darad vaale bhaag ki garam kapare se sikaai karame ya baraph ghisane se darad thik ho jaata hai, phir bhi darad bana rahe to hadadi rog visheshajany se milen aur upachaar laabh len। Home Remedies: saravaaikal sapndalaaitis (cervical spondylosis) ko garadan ki gathiya (neck arthritis) ke naam se bhi jaana jaata hai। is rog men garadan ke jor men darad ki shikaayat rahati hai। yah jor kaaratileja, utak aur saravaaikal sapaain men jure rahate hain। saravaaikal sapndalaaitis adhikatar umar barhane ke saath hone lagata hai lekin kai dapha garadan par dabaav parane, baithane-uthame ke galat poshachar se, dhoomarapaan karane, vajam ke bahut jayaada hone, jenetik kaaramon aur aalasi rahan sahan se bhi shuroo ho sakata hai। haalnki kuchh ghareloo upaay apanaakar saravaaikal saponadiloyasis ka upachaar snbhav hai। aaie jaanate hain kuchh aise hi upachaaron ke baare men- 1. niyamit vayaayaam (Daily excersise)- niyamit vayaayaam m karana bhi saravaaikal sapndalaaitis hone ka bara kaaran hai। niyamit vayaayaam se garadan ke darad ko kam kiya ja sakata hai। (yadi kisi bhi tarah ke vayaayaam se darad barh jaae to vayaayaam ko chhor den) 2. garam aur thndi sikaai (Hot and cold fomentation)- garadan darad se nijaat ke lie garadan ki garam aur thndi sikaai karane se bhi bahut aaraam milata hai। garam sikaai karane se rakat snchaar behatar hota hai vahin thndi sikaai se soojan aur chubham kam hoti hai। kaise karen upachaara- garam sikaai ke lie garam paami ki botal ko tauliya men lapet kar garadan ki sikaai karen। thndi sikaai karane ke lie baraph (ice) ke tukarom ko tauliya men lapetakara, us tauliya se sikaai karen। sikaai karate vakat kam se kam do se tin mimat tak garadan ki lagaataar sikaai honi chaahie। 15 se 20 minat men dobaara doharaaen। is vidhi ko aaraam home tak din mem do baar karen। 3. lahasum (Garlic)- yadi saravaaikal sapndalaaitis ke lakasham majar aaen to lahasun ka isatemaal behad achachhe parinaam de sakata hai। isake aushadhiy gun garadan ke darada, soojan aur jalan ko thik karate hain। kaise karen upachaara- lahasun ki do kali har subah khaali pet paani ke saath khaaen। khaana banaane vaale kisi bhi tel men lahasun ki kuchh kaliyn daal kar bhoon len। is tel ko gunaguma hone tak thnda karen aur parabhaavit hisase ki maalish karen। is vidhi ko din men do baar kiya ja sakata hai। 4. haladi (Haldi)- haladi ke aushadhiy gun kisi se chhipe nahin hai lekin achachhi baat yah bhi hai ki yah saravaaikal sapndalaaitis ke darad men bhi utani hi parabhaavi hai। haladi rakat snchaar tej karake garadam ke darad se aaraam deti hai aur garadan ki akaran ko bhi kam karati hai। kaise karen upachaara- ek chamamach haladi ko doodh men daalakar ubaalem aur thnda hone par isamen shahad milaaen, ise din men do baar pien। 5. til (sesame seed)- saravaaikal sapndalaaitis ke upachaar ke lie aayuraved ki besat aushadhi hai tila। isamen kailashiyama, maiganishiyama, maiganija, kaopara, jinka, phaosaphoras aur vitaamin ke (vitamin k) tatha di (vitamin d) parachur maatara mem paae jaate hain। isi kaaran yah hadadiyon ke saath saath poore sharir ke lie phaayademnd hai। kaise karen upachaara- til ke tel ko gunaguna karake lagabhag 10 minat parabhaavit hisase ki masaaj karen। is kariya ko dinabhar men tin se chaar baar karen। garam sisam ke tel men kuchh boomde levendar ke tel ki daalakar bhi masaaj ki ja sakati hai। til ko halaka sa bhoonakar roj subah chabaaem। isake alaava garam doodh men bhune hue til daalakar bhi piya ja sakata hai। ek din men lagabhag do gilaas doodh pien। 6. adarak (Ginger)- saravaaikal sapmdalaaitis ke ilaaj ke lie adarak bhi behatarin parabhaav dikhaata hai। yah rakat snchaar (blood circulation) ko tej karata hai jisase garadan ke darad se raahat milati hai। kaise karen upachaara- ek din men lagabhag tin kap adarak ki chaay pien। adarak ki chaay banaane ke lie paani mem adarak ubaalen aur thnda karake isamen shahad milaaen। is pey ko pien। parabhaavit hisase ki adarak ke tel se masaaj bhi ki ja sakati hai। 7. seb ka siraka (Apple cider vinegar)- seb saaidar siraka bhi saravaaikal sapndalaaitis se raahat dene men bahut achachha asar dikhaati hai। yah garadan ke darad aur soojan se raahat deta hai। kaise karen upachaara- kisi kapare ko se saaidar siraka men bhigokar parabhaavit sathaan par lapeten aur kuchh ghnton ke lie chhor den। din men do baar is vidhi ko karen। do kap seb ke sirake ko gunagune paani men daalakar nahaaya bhi ja sakata hai। ek gilaas paani mem kachacha seb ka siraka aur shahad milaakar pine se bhi laabh hota hai। Disease: vaakavikaar (Dyslexia) Descriptiom: disalekasiya koi bimaari nahin hai aur n hi yah koi maanasik ayogayata hai। disalekasiya (Dyslexia) parhane-likhane se snbndhi ek vikaar hai, jisamen bachachon ko shabadon ko pahachaanane, parhane, yaad karane aur bolane men pareshaani aati hai। ve kuchh akasharon aur shabadon ko ulata parhate hain aur kuchh akasharon ka uchachaaran bhi nahin kar paate। unaki parhane ki raphataar aur bachachon ki apekasha kaaphi kam hoti hai । Symptoms: - agar aapaka bachacha inamen se ek ya do pareshaaniyon se gujar raha hai aur vo sathaayi samasaya nahin hon to thori madad se hi bachache ko raahat mil sakati hai, chaahe vo ghar par ki gai madad ho ya kakasha men - uchachaaran saaph nahin homa - utatejit rahana - kavita vaale shabadon men dikakat - kaaphi thaka hona ya ekaagarata (ek chiz par dhayaan lagaame) mem kami - ginati, shabada, din aur mahinon ke naam samajhane men dikakat - daaem aur bne men ntar samajhane men dikakat hona - disha aur niradesh samajhane mem pareshaani - doosare bachachom ke mukaabale der se bolana shuru karana - nnbaron ke karam aur ganit ke chinahon men ulajhan - mai chijen sikhane men deri - parhaai ke dauraan shabadon ki galatiyn lagaataar karana - paraaimari parhaai ke dauraan lakasham parhane - baatachit karane men dikakat - bina soch vichaar ke kaaray karana ya kisi kaaray ko karane yojana nahin banaana - yadi ghar par aap apane bachache ke vayavahaar ke baare men satarak hain to shikashakon se jaanakaari lijie ki kaya sakool men bhi vo aisa hi vayavahaar karata hai. - logon se bolachaal karane men dikakata, apane aasapaas ki chijon ke parati asnvedanashilata jisake kaaran duraghatana ki snbhaavana bani rahati hai - varamamaala aur snkhaya ko sikhane men dikakat homa - shabadon aur dhavani ke mel ko kaaphi der se samajhana - shabadon ka matalab samajhane men deri, jayaadaatar sahi shabadon ko nahin pakar paana - shabadon ki pahachaan mem dikakat jaise (b/d), ulate (m/w), milate julate (felt/left) aur vaikalapik (house/home) shabad - samay ke baare men yaad rakhane ki kami - sakool se pahale ke lakashan Reasons: - vnshaanugat (Herediatary), yah tntarika tntar (Nervous System) ki samasaya hai, jo janam poorav kaarakon par nirabhar karati hain। - maata ke sntulit aahaar ki kami, dhoomarapaan ka sevan bhi isake kaaran ho sakate hain। - bachachon men kuposhan bhi isaka ek bara kaaran hai। Treatments: - kuchh kes men bachache ke janam se pahale hi disalekasiya ka ndaaja lagaaya ja sakata hai। aise men daokatar un garabhavati mahilaaom ko paushatik aahaar lene ki salaah ke
