bachachon ki samajh dhimi hoti hai, isalie imahen jayaada samay dene ki aavashayakata hoti hai। - disalekasiya se pirit bachachon ke saath apana parhane ka apama tarika badalen, chijon ko aasaan karake bataaen, tora-torakar samajhaaen। chitaron aur kahaaniyon ka sahaara len। jin akasharon ko pahachaanane aur likhane men samasaya hoti hai, unahen baara-baar likhavaae। - vokeshanal tareming karaaen। Disease: pitataashay ki pathari (Gallstones) Description: pitataashay (Gall Bladder) pitat (Bile) bhndaaram ke lie ek chhoti si thaili hai (pitat jigar davaara utapaadit ek paachak ras hai jo khaame men maujood vasa ke tootane men parayog kiya jaata hai)। pitataashay men vasaayukat khaaday padaarathon ki maatar adhik hone se pitataashay ki pathari (kolesataraola, pitat varanak aur kailashiyam lavan se bana chhota sa patathara) ka niramaan hota hai। Symptoms: - darad chhaati, kndhe, garadam men bhi phail sakata hai - pet aur pith men achaanak darad uthana - vasaayukat bhojan khaame ke baad pet ke darad men teji aanaa, piliyaa, bukhaar Reasoms: - pitat men kolesataraol ki atayadhikata (Over Saturation) - pitat men lesithin - aur pitat lavan ki kam aapoorati (Undersupply)। Treatments: pitataashay ki pathari kisi bhi samasayaaon ka kaaran nahin hai lekin yadi pitataashay ki pathari snkaraman paida kar raha hai to aapareshan jaroori hai। Home Remedies: asasi phisadi pitat ki thaili ki pathari kolesataraol (cholestrol) ke jamane ya sakhat hone ke kaaram hoti hai। pitat ki pathari ke kaaran pet men asahaniy darad hota hai, kai baar ulati (vomit) bhi ho sakati hai। rogi ka khaana pachane men dikakat hone lagati hai jisase pet men apach (indigestiom) aur bhaaripan rahata hai। pitat ki thaili men pathari hone ke baare men yahi kaha jaata hai ki bina aupareshan ke ise nikaalana mushakil hai। aise men yadi aapako gaol baledar saton ki shikaayat hai to jaahir hai aapane bhi aupareshan ka vichaar banaaya hogaa, lekin aupareshan se pahale kuchh ghareloo upaay apanaakar dekhen, snbhav hai ki pathari gal jaae। kuchh ghareloo upaay n keval pathari ko gala denge balaki paachan ko duroosat karake darad ko bhi thik kar denge। aaie jaanate hain, aise hi ghareloo upaayon ke baare men। 1. seb ka joos aur seb ka siraka (Apple and Apple cider vinegar)- seb mem pitat ki pathari ko galaame ka gun hota hai, lekin ise joos ke roop mem seb ke sirake ke saath lene par yah jayaada asarakaari hota hai। seb mem maujood mailik esid (mallic acid) pathari ko galaane men madad karata hai tatha seb ka siraka livar men kolesataraol nahin banane detaa, jo pathari banane ke lie jimamedaar hota hai। yah ghol n keval pathari ko galaata hai balaki dobaara banane se bhi rokata hai aur darad se bhi raahat deta hai। upachaar ke lie- ek gilaas seb ke joos men, ek chamamach seb ka siraka milaaen। is joos ko rojaana din bhar men do baar pien। 2. naashapaati ka joos (Pear juice)- naashapaati ke aakaar ki pitat ki thaili ko naashapaati davaara hi saaph kiya jaana snbhav hai। naashapaati men maujood paikatin (pecteme) kolesataraol (cholesterol) ko banane aur jamane se rokata hai। yoon bhi naashapaati gunon ki khaan hai jisake kai savaasathay laabh haim। upachaara- ek gilaas garam paani men, ek gilaas naashapaati ka joos aur do chamamach shahad (honey) milaakar pien। is joos ko ek din men tin baar pina chaahie। 3. chukndara, khira aur gaajar ka joos (Beetroot, Cucumber and carrot juice)- joos therepi ko pitat ki thaili ke ilaaj ke lie ghareloo upachaaron men sabase jayaada isatemaal kiya jaata hai। chukndar n keval sharir ka majabooti deta hai balaki gaol baledar ko saaph bhi karata hai saath hi livar ke kolon (colon) ko bhi saaph karata hai। khira men maujood jayaada paami ki maatara livar aur gaol baledar donon ko ditaokasiphaai (detoxify) karati hai। gaajar men bhi vitaamim si aur uchach poshak tatav (high nutrient) hone ke kaaran yahi gum hote hain। upachaara- ek chukndara, ek khira aur chaar gaajar ko lekar joos taiyaar karen। is joos ko paratidin do baar pina hai। joos men paratayek saamagari ki maatara baraabar honi chaahie, isalie sabaji ya phal ke saaij ke hisaab se maatara ghataai ya barhaai ja sakati hai। 4. pudina (Mint)- pudina ko paachan ke lie sabase achachhi ghareloo aushadhi (home remedy) maana jaata hai jo pitat vaahika tatha paachan se snbndhit anay rason ko barhaata hai। pudina men taarapin (terpenes) bhi hota hai jo ki pathari ko galaame men sahaayak maana jaata hai। pudime ki patatiyon se bami chaay gaol baledar satom se raahat de sakati hai। upachaara- paani ko garam karen, isamen taaji ya sookhi pudine ke patatiyon ko ubaalen। halaka gunaguna rahane par paani ko chhaanakar isamen shahad milaaen aur pi len। is chaay ko dim men do baar piya ja sakata hai। 5. khaana-paan aur dinacharaya men badalaav (Chamges im diet and daily activity) rojaana 8 se 10 gilaas paani jaroor piem। chaahe payaas n bhi lagi ho। vasaayukat ya tej masaale vaale khaane se bachen। paratidin kaophi jaroor pien। bahut jayaada bhi nahin lekin din men ek se do kap kaaphi hain। kaophi bhi pitat vaahika ko barhaati hai jisase pitat ki thaili men pathari nahin hoti। apane khaane men vitaamin si ki maatara badhaaen। dinabhar men jitama jayaada snbhav ho vitaamin si se bharapoor chijen khaaen। haladi, sauntha, kaali mirach aur hing ko khaane men jaroor shaamil karem। Disease: rebij (Rabies) Description: rebiz ek nayooro imavesiv (Neuro-Invasive) vaayaral bimaari hai। rebiz ka vaayaras tntarika tntar yaani sentaral naravas sisatam (Central Nervous System) par ataik karata hai, jisase pirit vayakati saamaanay nahin rah paataa। Symptoms: - gale ki mns peshiyon men khinchaav paida ho jaata hai - pirit vayakati kutate ki tarah bhaunkane bhi lagata hai - bechaini, nshik pakashaaghaata, bharama, anidara aur nigalane mem kathinaai aadi kuchh anay lakashan hain - rebij ka shikaar bane jaamavaron ka dimaagi sntulan bigarane lagata hai - rebij ho jaame par marij paami se darame lagata hai Reasons: rebij pashuon ke kaatame ke kaaran hota hai। paalatoo jaanavara, kutate, bilali ya chamakaadar ke kaatane se sabase adhik rebiz hota hai। Treatments: rebij se bachaav ke lie jaroori hai isake baarem men jaanakaari honaa। rebiz (Rabies) akasar pashuon ke kaatane ke kaaran hota hai, saath hi aise mem is baat ka dhayaan rakhana chaahie ki yah siraph kaatane hi nahin chhilane ke kaaran bhi hota hai। rebiz hone par niman baaton ka dhayaan rakhana chaahie: - pashuom ke kaatane par kaate gae sathaam ko paani v saabun se achachhi tarah dho dema chaahie। - dhome ke baad kaate gae sathaan par achachhi tarah se tinchar ya povodim aayodin lagaana chaahie। aisa karane se kutate ya anay pashuon ki laar men paae jaane vaale kitaamu sirotaaipavan laayasa vaayaras ki gayaalakoparotin ki paraten ghul jaati hain। isase rog ki maar ek bare had tak kam ho jaati hai, jo rogi ke bachaav men sahaayak hoti hai। - isake turnt baad rogi ko titenas ka injekashan lagavaakar chikitasaalay mem le jaana chaahie। yahn chikitasak ki salaah se kaate gae sathaan par kaarabolik esid lagaaya jaata hai, jisase adhikatam kitaanu nashat ho jaate hain। - isake baad chikitasak ki salaah par aavashayakataanusaar injekashan lagaae jaate hain, jo tin ya das din ki avadhi ke hote hain। - tatapashachaat aavashayakataanusaar nishachit dinon par busatar doj bhi die jaame ka paraavadhaan hai, jo chikitasak ke vivek v kaate gae pashu ki jivit ya marit hone ki avasatha par mirabhar karate hain। - injekashan lagaane ki karamabadadhata men laaparavaahi ghaatak sidadh ho sakati hai। - is rog ka parakop pashu ke kaatane ke tin karati hai। yadi raibij ke lakashan ubharane se pahale isaka ilaaj m kiya jaae to vayakati ki maut bhi ho sakati hai। aise jaanavar jo is vaayaras se aphekated (affected) hote hain, unake salaaiva kaatane, chaatane, kharonch lagaane ya kisi jakham ko chaatane se bhi raibij phail sakati hai। aise men kisi bhi jaamavar ke snparak men aane se pahale saavadhaan rahana chaahie tatha sabhi paalatoo snparak men aane par aapako lagata hai ki raibij inphekated thaa, to sabase pahale parabhaavit hisase ko paami aur phir saabun se achachhi tarah dhoen। yadi jaanavar ne kaata ho ya aapake jakham par kharoncha ho to bilakul bhi laaparavaahi n karen। saabun aur paami se dhone ke baad turnt chikitasak se milen। 2. akharot (walnut) akharot men kutate davaara hone vaali raibij ke jahar ko maarane ki kashamata hoti hai। upachaar ke lie akharota, payaaj aur namak ki baraabar maatara lekar pis len। is mitaran men thoda shahad milaaem। parabhaavit hisase ya ghaav par yah lep lagaaen। 3. levendar (lavander) jaanavar ke kaatame ke sathaan par ya raibij parabhaavit hisase par levendar ko pis kar lep lagaane se bhi inphekashan se bacha ja sakata hai। 4. lahasun (garlic) lahasun men paraakaritik taur par entibaayetik (antibiotic) gun hote haim। raibij ke ghaav ko jaladi bharane ke lie din men tin baar lahasum ki kali chabaaen। 5. jira (cumin) kutate ke kaatane se phailane vaali raibij par jira bhi kaaphi asar dikhaata hai। do bare chamamach jira ko pisakar usamen bis kaali mirach pisakar milaaen। domon paaudar men paani milaakar lep banaaen aur parabhaavit hisase par lagaaen। isase bhi ghaav jaladi bharane men madad milegi। 6. vitaamin si (vitamin c) yadi aap raibij se inphekated hain to apane aahaar men vitaamin si ki maatara barhaaen। isake lie amarood (guawa), laal mirach (red pepper), kivi (kiwi), phool gobhi (cauli flower), smtara aur ninboo aadi len। vitaamin si sapaliment bhi le sakate hain। 7. vitaamin bi (vitamin b) raibij ke inphekashan se bachane ko vitaamin bi bhi bahut laabhakaari hai। raibij ke upachaar ke lie apane aahaar men aise bhojan ko shaamil karen jisamen vitaamin bi parachur maatara men ho। aise khaaday padaarathon ke lie aap bndagobhi (cabbage), tamaatara, rasapabairi, tarabooja, anaanaas (pine apple) aur paalak aadi le sakate hain। isake alaava vitaamin bi ke sapaliment lena bhi phaayademnd hota hai। nota- yah sabhi upachaar ghareloo hain। inamem se kuchh upachaar jaanavar ke kaatane ke turnt baad daokatar ke paas pahunchane ki deri ki avasatha men pahale kie ja sakate hain, taaki inphekashan jayaada n barhe ya avasatha ghaatak n ho। saath hi kuchh upachaar ilaaj ke dauraan lagaataar kie ja sakate hain। lekin raibij hone ki sathiti men chikitasak ke paas jaana jaroori hai, ghareloo upachaar atirikat laabh ke lie hain। Disease: jukaam (Common Cold) Description: jukaam vishaanuon (vaayarasa) davaara phailaaya jaane vaale snkaraman hai jo khaasakar hamaare sns paranaali ke aage vaale hisase ko parabhaavit karata hai। jukaam sharir ki roga-paratirodhak kashamata ka parichaayak hai। Symptoms: - nkh se paani bahana - kaan men darad hona - gale men darad hona - naak se paani bahana - saradarad hona - haraarat mahasoos hona Reasons: - hava men maujood baikatiriya ya vaayaras jab kabhi sns ke jarie sharir men paravesh karate haim, to elaraji ho jaati hai। natija yah hota hai ki paani ya balagam naak se baahar aane lagate hain। - hamaare gale men do tarah ke baikatiriya maujood hote hain - kuchh achachhe aur kuchh bure। kabhi-kabhi saradi-garami barhame, ekadam thndaa-garam khaame, thnde se garam v garam se thnde maahaul men jaane, thnda paani jayaada pine ya baarish men bhigame se gale ke bure baikatiriya sakariy ho jaate hain। ye baikatiriya hi gale men imaphekashan kar dete hain aur jukaam (Jukam) ki vajah banate hain। Treatments: jukaam ek savabhaavik kariya maani jaati hai। agar kuchhek din men yah apane aap thik ho jaae to ise bimaari mahin maana jaata lekin adhik din rahane par isaka upachaar karaana jaroori hota hai। jukaam ke kuchh khaas upaay niman hain: - saadhaaran jukaam apane aap pnch din men thik ho jaata hai। - agar balagam saphed ho to yah elaraji ki mishaani hai। yah saadhaaran jukaam hota hai। - jukaam ko pnch din se jayaada ho jaaen ya saath men khnsi, balagama, badan darad v bukhaar bhi ho, to samajhana chaahie ki aam jukaam nahin hai। - agar balagam pila ho ho v sns ki dikakat ke saath bukhaar bhi ho to baikatiriyal inphekasham hota hai। - aise men daokatar ke paas jaana chaahie। - agar kaf ke saath khoon bhi aae to chintaajanak baat hai। yah ti.bi. ka lakashan ho sakata hai। aise men turanat daokatar se paraamarash len। Home Remedies: jukaam snkaraman (Infection) ka ek parakaar hai jo ki vaayaras ke vibhinam parakaar ke kaaranom se ho sakata hai। sir darada, naak bahanaa, khnsi, tej bukhaara, nkhon men jalama, gale men kharaash (Sore throat) aur sharir men darad (Body pain) aadi saamaanay jukaam ke kuchh lakashan hain। jukaam se raahat ke lie kai ghareloo upachaar hain jo ki jukaam ki samasaya se raahat de sakate hain। yah ghareloo upachaar kisi bhi dushaparabhaav ke bina saradi ke vibhinan lakashanom se parabhaavi raahat paradaan karate hain। 1. lahasun (Garlic) - lahasun ka jivaamurodhi aur entivaayaral (antiviral) gun saradi ke lakashanon se chhutakaara paraapat karane men bahut sahaayak hota hai। lahasun paratirakasha paranaali (immunity) ke lie achachha hai aur shavasan maarag (respiratory process) ko kholane mem madad karata hai। kaise karen upayog - ek kap paani men lahasun ki kali, do chamamach nimboo ka rasa, ek chamamach shahada, aur aadha chamamach laal mirach ya laal mirach paaudar milaaem। ise tab tak roj khaaen jab tak saradi jukaam se aaraam na ho। - ek kap paani men 4-5 kate hue lahasun ki kali ubaal len aur ek chamamach shahad daalen। ise din men do se tin baar sevan karem। 2. shahad (Honey) - shahad men maujood enjaaim (enzyme) men, uchach maatara men baikatiriya aur vaayaras ko maarane ke gun hote hain। shahad se gale ka sookhaapan door hota hai aur jukaam jaladi thik ho jaata hai। kaise karen upayog - sabase saral upaay ghar par ek chamamach ninboo ka ras aur do chamamach shahad milaaen। thndak aur gale men jukaam men bahut jaladi raahat deti hai। kaise karen upayog - ek chauthaai kap sookha bhume hue dhaniya bij pisakar isamen aadha chamamach jira aur saumph ke bij aur ek chauthaai chamamach methi ke bij milaaen। ab ek kap paami ubaal len aur isamen aadha chamamach taiyaar masaala aur aadha chamamach mishari daalen। tin se chaar minat ubaalen। isake baad doodh daalem aur garam garam pien। 4. adarak (ginger) - adarak apane emtivaayarala, esapekatarenat (expectorant) gunon ke kaaran saradi se raahat deta hai। kaise karen upayog - kachacha adarak khaane ya ek din men adarak ki chaay kai baar pine se laabh hota hai। adarak ki chaay ke parabhaav ko barhaane ke lie, chaay mem ninboo ka ras aur shahad milaaen। - adaraka, laung aur namak ka ek pesat taiyaar karen। aadha chamamach kha sakate hain। - naak bah rahi ho to baraabar maatar men sookha adarak paaudar (Dry ginger powder) makakhan ya ghi aur gur (jaggary) milaakar chhoti chhoti goli banaaen। subah rojaana khaali pet ek goli khaaen। 5. laal payaaj ka sirap (Syrup of red onion) - ghar ke bane laal payaaj sirap se bhi saradi se pirit logon ko raahat milati hai। kaise karem upayog - 2-3 laal payaaj ko baarik gol tukaron men kaat len। ek baratam men payaaj ka ek tukara rakhen aur kachacha shahad milaaen। jab tak baratam bhar n jaae tab tak parakariya ko doharaaen। katore ko dhak kar rakhen aur 12 se 15 ghnte ke lie chhor den। payaaj sirap ki tarah moti parat mem jam jaaegaa। 6. chikan ka soop (Chicken soup) - chikan soop kai men kai aavashayak poshak tatav vitaamin hain jo aam saradi ke lakashanon ke upachaar men madad karate hain। chikan soop ke uchach entiaukasident gun jukaam ko thik karane ki parakariya mem teji laate haim। saravotatam parinaamon ke lie, jaivik sabajiyon aur chikan ka upayog kara, ghar ka bana chikan soop taiyaar karen। Disease: bukhaar (Fever) Description: bukhaar aana ek behad aam bimaari hoti hai। vijanyaam ke anusaar yah bukhaar rog nahin balaki rog ka lakashan hota hai। jaanien bukhaar ke baaren men visataar se: Reasons: - shavasan snsathaan vaale bukhaar jaise ki jukaama, phaloo, gale ki soojana, shavaasanali shotha, nayoomoniyaa, ti.bi. aadi। - tavacha ke snkaraman (Infection) se hone vaale bukhaar jaise ki jakham mem pip honaa, phore ya daame vaale bukhaara। - machachhar ya pisasoo se hone vaale bukhaar jaise ki maleriya (Malari Fever), phaayaleriya (Flaria), dengoo (Demgue), chikunagunaya (Chickengunia), masatishak javar (Meningitis), paleg (Plague), aadi। in sabhi bukhaaron men pahale knpaknpi hoti hai। - paachan snsathaan ke bukhaar jaise dasat ya pechisha, piliyaa, taayaphaoid aadi। pechish mem khoom aur balagam girata hai। taayaphaaid khoon ke jaonch se hi pata chalata hai। - parajamam aur mootar snsathaan ke bukhaar - isamen peshaab ke samay jalan hoti hai। - anay snkaraamak bukhaar jaise ki baruselaosisa, edasa, tapedik ke kuchh parakaara, joron ka bukhaara। asnkaraamak bukhaaron men jaise loo lagana aur elaraji se hone vaale bukhaara। Treatments: bukhaar aane par rogi ke sharir ka taapamaan dekhana chaahie aur agar taapamaan adhik ho to daokatar ki salaah leni chaahie। bukhaar (Bukhar) aane ke dauraan rogi ko niman saamaanay khaana jaise chaaval ki knji, saaboodaane ki khir ya khichari, jau ka paani aadi dema chaahiye। - rogi ko achachhe havaadaar kamare men rakhana chaahiye। - savachachh evm mulaayam vasatar pahanaaen। - yadi javar 39.5 digari se. ya 103.0 phairenahaait se adhik ho ya phir 48 ghnton se adhik samay ho gaya ho to daokatar se paraamarash len। Home Remedies: jab bhi sharir ka taapamaan saamaanay se mnsapeshiyon men darad (Muscle pain) , dihaadareshan (Dehydration) , kai dapha knpakapi (Shivring) to kai baar pasina aana aur kamajori ho sakate hain। yoom to bukhaar kuchh din men thik ho jaata hai aur parakariya ko doharaaen। lahasun (Garlic) lahasun ki garam taasir bhi sharir men pasina laakara, sharir ka taapamaan kam kar sakati hai। yah sharir se haanikaarak vishaakat padaarathon ko bhi baahar nikaalane men sahaayak hai। itana hi nahin lahasun entiphngal (antifungal) aur entibaikatiriyal gunon se bhara hai jo sharir ko imayooniti (Immunity) deta hai। lahasun ki ek kali ko pisakar din mem do baar pien। adarak (Ginger) adarak men sharir ke taapamaan ko niyntarit karane ke gun hote hain। yoon bhi adarak paraakaritik roop se enti vaayaral (Anti Viral) aur entibaikatiriyal (Anti sakata hai। Disease: gale men kharaash (Sore Throat) Description: mausam badalate hi gale men kharaash hona aam baat hai। saamaanay shabadon men gale men kharaasha, gale ka snkaraman (Infection) hai। aamataur par gale ka snkaraman (Infection) vaayaras ya baikatiriya ke kaaran hota hai। Symptoms: - 100.5 darigi F ya 38 darigi selasiyas se adhik bukhaar homa - garadan men soojan hona - gale men Throat) - namak ke gunagume paani se garaare karem। isase gale men aaraam milegaa। - adaraka, ilaayachi aur kaali mirach vaali chaay gale ki kharaash (Sore Throat) men aaraam pahunchaati hai। - kam vaise to gale ki kharaash tin chaar din mem thik ho jaati hai, lekin kuchh ghareloo upaayom se gale ki kharaash men jaladi raahat milati hai। aaie jaanen gale ki kharaash door karame ke ghareloo upaay 1. garam paani aur mamak ke garaare (Gargle of warm water amd salt)- jab gale men kharaash hoti hai to shaleshama jhilali (mucous membrane) ki koshikaaon men soojan ho jaati hai। namak is soojan (swelling) ko kam karata hai jisase darad men raahat milati hai। upachaar ke lie ek gilaas gumagune paani men ek bara chamamach namak milaakar ghol len aur is paani se garaare karen। is parakariya ko din men tin baar karen। 2. lahasun (Garlic)- lahasun inphekasham (infection) paida karane vaale jivaanuon ko maar deta hai। isalie gale ki kharaash mem lahasun behad phaayademnd hai। lahasun men maujood elisin (allicin) jivaanuon ko maarane ke saath hi gale ki soojan aur darad ko bhi kam karata hai। upachaar ke lie gaalon ke donom taraph lahasun ki ek ek kali rakhakar dhire dhire choosate rahen। jaise jaise lahasun ka ras gale men jaaega vaise vaise aaraam milata rahegaa। lahasun ka ras nikaalane ke lie bich bich men dnton se kuchalate rahen। 3. bhaap lena (Steaming)- kai baar gale ke sookhame ke kaaram bhi gale men inphekashan ki shikaayat hoti hai। aise men kisi bare baratan men garam paani karake tauliya se munh dhakakar bhaap len। aisa karane se bhi gale ki sikaai hogi aur gale ka imphekashan bhi khatam hogaa। is kariya ko din mem do baar kiya ja sakata hai। 4. laal mirach (Red chilli)- gale ki kharaash ko thik karane ke lie laal mirach bhi behad phaayademnd hai। upachaar ke lie ek kap garam paani men ek chamamach laal mirach aur ek chamamach shahad milaakar pien। 5. bekimg soda (Baking soda)- gale ki kharaash door karane ke lie beking soda ki chaay behad phaayademnd hai। kaarana, beking soda men enti baikatiriyal (antibacterial) gum hote hain jo ki jivaanuon ko nashat kar dete hain। isake lie ek gilaas garam paami men beking soda aur namak milaakar din mem tin baar garaare karem। 6. laung (Laung or Clove)- laung ka isatemaal upachaar ke lie sadiyon se hota a raha hai। gale ki kharaash ke upachaar ke lie laung ko munh men rakhakar dhire dhire chabaama chaahie। shahad milaaen। is pey ko din men do se tim baar pien। gale ki kharaash se aaraam milegaa। 8. masaala chaay (Masal Chay)- launga, tulasi (basil), adarak aur kaali mirach (black pepper) ko paani men Disease: ubakaai (Nausea) Description: ubakaai aana ulati hone ka ehasaas maatar hai। kuchh logon ko mitali jayaada aati hai। visheshakar yaatara ke samay kuchh logon ko ubakaai ki samasaya hoti hai। ise moshan sikanes (Motion Sickmess) bhi kahate hain। yah gaadi se yaatara ke dauraan ya ya naav se yaatara ke dauraan (Se Sickness) vishesh roop se mahasoos kiya jaata hai। Symptoms: - dil ki dharakam barh jaati hai - pasina aane lagata hai - pet men garabari ka ehasaas hone lagata hai Reasoms: yaatara ke dauraan mitali aana behad saamaamay baat hai lekin kai vajahon se yah agar lagaataar aae to ek samasaya ho sakati hai। mitali niman kaaranon se bhi aati hai: mitali aur ulati ke saamaanay kaaran (Reason of Nausea) - ainti baayotik (Anti Biotic) davaaiyon ke kaaram akasar pet men badahajami se, amalata (Acidity), sharaab aadi se bhi mitali ki samasaya ho sakati hai। - garabhaavasatha men pahale timaahi men mitali ya ulati ki samasaya (nause during pregnancy) hoti hai। yah ki samasaya ho sakati hai। - phood elaraji aur phood asahishanuta (Food Intolerance) - maaigaren men sir ke bhitar kisi bhi parakaar ke dabaav se seribaro-sapaainal phalooid (Cerebro-Spinal Fluid) aur mitali aur ulati hone lagati hai। - kabhi kabhi ekasident ya gndagi badaboo ke kaaran bhi mitali a sakati hai। - tanaava, bhay aur bechaini ke kaaran sharir ki kariya men asntulam paida ho jaata dhilaa-dhaala kapara pahane। - zaroorat se zayaada paani nahin pina chaahie। - agar sathiti gnbhir ho jaay to daokatar se salaah leni chaahie। Home Remedies: matali ya ji michalaane ki pareshaani mosham sikanes (Motion sickness), pet ke phaloo (Stomach flu) ya phir aapake davaara khaae gae khaame ke inphekashan se hoti hai। kabhi kabhaar matali kisi gnbhir bimaari jaise haarat ataika, kaimsar ya kimotherepi lene ke dauraan bhi ho sakati hai। aaie jaanen kuchh aise ghareloo upachaar jo matali ya ji michalaane ki pareshaani se aapako raahat denge। 1. adarak (Gimger) adarak ji michalaane ya ulati men raahat deme ke lie saravotatam aushadhi hai। isake upachaar ke lie adarak ki chaay ya adarak ko yoon hi chabaana bhi laabhadaayak ho sakata hai। haalnki garabhaavasatha (Pregnancy) men adarak isatemaal ki manaahi hoti hai। saath hi do saal se kam umar ke bachachon ko bhi adarak nahin di jaani chaahie। 2. ninboo (Lemon) ninboo bhi ji michalaane ki samasaya se raahat deta hai। ninboo patatiyn chabaai ja sakati hain। isake alaava pudine ki chaay (Mint tea) banaakar pina ya kaindi khaama bhi laabhaparad hota hai। 4. doodha-bared (Milk amd bread) matali se raahat ke lie doodh bared thik se kaam karane ke lie kaaphi aham hota hai , kai kaaranon se reda-balad sel nashat ho jaate hain jis avasatha ko himolaayatiis kahate hain, aisi sathiti men reda-balad selas thik tarike se kaam nahin kar paate hain, himolaayatis ki sathiti kai kaaranon se paida ho sakati hain, kaaran aanuvnshik aur reda-balad selas ka ati miramaan ho sakata hai isake alaava kai avasatha men saamaamay reda-balad selas men bhi himolaayatik enimiya ho sakata hai। - vitaamin bi-12 ki kami: sharir men vitaamin bi-12 ki kami se paranisiyas enimiya hone ki snbhaavana hoti hai। paranisiyas enimiya chot ya ghaav se saraava, gaisatarointesataainal alasara, kolan kainsar itayaadi mem dhire-dhire khoon lagaataar risame se enimiya ho sakata hai। - lnbe samay se bimaar hone para: kisi bhi parakaar ki diraghakaalik bimaari se enimiya ho sakata hai। Treatmemts: emimiya se bachaav ka sabase behatarin upaay hai paushatik aahaar lenaa। isake saath hi niman bindooon par dhayaan dekar bhi is bimaari se isaka ek nukasaan yah bhi hai ki sharir ki koshikaaon men aukasijan ki aavaajaahi (Oxygen circulation) kam ho jaati hai jisase sharir ka parayaapat uraja nahin mil paati aur vayakati enimiya se garasat ho jaata hai। isake saath hi yadi sharir mem pholik esid aur vitaamin bi 12 ki kami hai tab bhi vayakati enimiya se garasat ho sakata hai। purooshon ki tulana men mahilaaen jayaada enimik paai jaati haim। sharir ka jaladi thakanaa, chakakar aanaa, tavacha men pilaapana, lagaataar rahame vaala sir darad aadi kuchh enimiya ke lakashanon men shaamil hain। aaie aapako bataate hain, enimiya se raahat paane ke ghareloo upaay (Home remedies for anemia) 1. paalak (Spinach) paalak men bharapoor lauh tatha vitaamin bi 12 hota hai। isake saath hi paalak pholik esid (Folic Acid) ka bhi uchach satarot hai। aise men paalak khaane se khoon ki kami poori hoti hai। upachaar ke lie paalak ka soop banaakara, ya paalak ka saag aadi ko apane roj ke khaane mem shaamil karana chaahie। 2. anaar (Pomegranate) anaar sharir men himogalobin (Haemoglobin) ko bahut teji se barhaata hai। amaar men parotin aur kaarabohaaidaret ki uchach maatara hoti hai। isamen aayaran aur kailashiyam bhi hota hai। yah khoon men himogalobin ki maatara ko teji se barhaakar rakat snchaar ko thik rakhata hai। enimiya ke upachaar ke lie subah khaali pet anaar khaaen aur rojaana anaar ka joos pien। 3. chukndar aur seb ka ras (Beetroot amd Apple Juice) chukmdar men pholik esid uchach maatara mem hota hai jabaki seb men lauh tatav hote hain, aise men donon hi enimiya ki kami ko door karate hain। upachaar ke lie ek kap chukndar ke ras aur ek kap seb ke ras men ek se do chamamach shahad milaakar din men do baar pien। 4. tamaatar (Tomato) sharir ke lie bahut jayaada aayaran ki maatara leme ke saath hi yah bhi jaroori hai ki aayaran ko aapaka sharir sokhe। isamen tamaatar aham bhoomika nibhaata hai। rojaana ek se do kachache tamaatar jaroor khaaen। ek gilaas tamaatar ka ras bhi roj pien aur khaana banaane aur salaad men bhi tamaatar ka bharapoor upayog karen। 5. khajoor (Dates) khajoor bhi aayaran bahut achachha satarot hai। sau garaam khajoor men 90 miligaraam aayaran ki maatara hoti hai। do khajoor ko ek kap doodh men raat bhar ke lie chhor den। in khajoor ko subah khaali pet chaba chabaakar khaaen। bache hue doodh ko bhi pi len। khajoor ko garam paami men do ya tin ghntom ke lie bhigaakar us paani ko pima bhi phaayademnd hota hai। jim logon ko lekatoj (lectose) se elaraji hai aur doodh nahin le sakate, unake lie yah behatar tarika hai। 6. kishamish (Kishmish) kishamish bhi enimiya ki behad achachhi ghareloo dava hai। kishamish men aayarana, parotina, phaaibara, sodiyam jaise uchach poshak tatav hote hain। upachaar ke lie ek kap paani men 10 se 15 kishamish raatabhar ke lie bhiga den। subah in kishamish ko shahad milaakar kha len aur bache hue paani ko pi len। 7. shahad (Honey) shahad bhi lauh aur vitaamin bi 12 ka uchach satarot hai। shahad ko rojaana khaane se bhi sharir men enimiya ki kami poori hoti hai। shahad ko phalon men milaakara, doodh men daalakar ya chimi ki jagah shahad isatemaal karake bhi rakat ki kami poori ki ja sakati hai। Disease: dimenshiya (Dementia) Description: dimenshiya (Dementia) vayakati ke masatishak ko parabhaavit karame vaali bimaari hoti hai। alajaaimaras ki bimaari (Alziehmers Disease) aur vasakayular dimenshiya (Vascular Dementia) isake sabase aam parakaar (Common Type) haim। Symptoms: - apane aap men gumasum rahanaa, mela-jol bnd kar denaa, chupapi saadhana - kapade ulate pahananaa, saafa-suthara n rah paana - kisi baat ko ya parashan ko doharaanaa, jidad karanaa, tarak n samajh paana - kisi vasatu ka chitar dekhakar yah n samajh paana ki yah kaya hai - kuchh kaam shuroo karanaa, phir bhool jaana ki kaya karana chaahate the, aur bahut koshish ke baad bhi yaad n kar paana - chizon ko galata, anuchit jagah par rakh chhodana (jaise ki ghadi ko, ya auphis phaail ko pharij men rakh denaa) - chhoti chhoti samasayaaon ko bhi m sulajha paana - chhoti-chhoti baat para, ya bina kaaran hi baukhala jaanaa, chilalaanaa, romaa, itayaadi - dimenshiya se parabhaavit vayakati men, rog ke barhane ke saath jayaada aur adhik gnbhir lakashan nazar aate hain। (yaad rakhen ki har vayakati men alag alag lakashan nazar aate hain) - nnbar jorane aur ghataane men dikakata, ginati karane men dikakat - bolate ya likhate hue galat shabad ka parayog karanaa, ya shabadon ke arath n samajh paana - bari rakam ko phaalatoo ki sakim mem daal denaa, paise se samabndhit ajib niranay lenaa, laaparavaahi ya gairajimamedaari dikhaana - yah bhool jaana ki taarikh kaya hai, kaunasa mahina hai, saal kaunasa hai, vayakati kis ghar men hain, kis shahar men hain, kis desh men Reasons: ​dimenshiya kai kaaranon se ho sakata hai lekin isaka mukhay kaaran aanuvnshik hi maana jaata hai। saath hi barhati umar men is bimaari se pirit hone ki snbhaavama bhi barh jaati hai। isake aham kaarak nimam hain: dimenshiya ke paramukh kaaran (Causes of Dementi ​in Hindi) - aanuvmshika: agar parivaar men koi bhi is bimaari se pirit ho, to khatare ki snbhaavana badh jaati hai - barhati umar men is bimaari ke khatare barh jaate haim। - uchach se sharir se jaroori poshak tatav nahin mil paate jis kaaran dimenshiya (Dementia) hone ki snbhaavana barh jaati hai। Treatments: dimenshiya se bachaav aur isaka ilaaj donon hi smbhav hai। jaroori hai to keval sahi samay par isaki jaanakaari honaa। dimenshiya ke dauraan niman baaton ka dhayaan rakhana jaroori hai: - dimenshiya ka vayakati aur parivaar par kaya asar paregaa, yah samajhem aur savikaaren। - dekhabhaal kai varashon tak chal sakati hai, isalie yah jaamana jaroori hai ki rogi ki dekhabhaal ke alaava aur kaya kaya jimamedaariyn nibhaani hain aur dekhabhaal ke lie samay aur paise ka intajaam kis parakaar karenge। - isalie apami jindagi men usi parakaar se badalaav laaen taaki rogi ki dekhabhaal ke saath saath aap apami anay jimamedaariyn bhi mibha saken। isake lie jo bhi sikhana hai, vah sikhen, aur khushi khushi apane karatavay ka niravaah karen। Home Remedies: dimenshiya ya yaadadaashat ka jaana sabhi ke lie chinta ka kaaran ho sakata hai। ham sabhi apame dimaag ko savasath rakhama chaahate hain। dimenshiya ke marij ki yaadadaashat (memmory) jaane ke saath hi usake vayavahaar mem bhi parivaratan hota hai jisase n keval marij balaki parivaar ke anay sadasay bhi parabhaavit hote hain। aaie jaanen dimenshiya se bachane ke lie kuchh ghareloo upachaara- 1. chini ko avaoid karen (Avoid sugar) sabase pahale apane khaane se mitha (sweet), kaarabohaaidaret (carbohydrate) tatha riphaaimd kaarabohaaidaret (refined carbohydrate) sabhi ko alag kar den। jab tak ki aapaka vajan niyntarit nahin ho jaata hai, kaarabohaaidat vaali chijon ko khaane se bachen। bahut adhik chini kho se bhi dimaagi utak (brain membrane) kamajor hote hain jisaka asar yaadadaashat (memmory) par parata hai। 2. haladi (Haldi) haladi men maujood tatav karakayoomin (curcumin) dimenshiya se surakasha paradaan karata hai। haladi men entiaukasident (amtioxidant) tatav bhi hote hain jo dimaagi vikaas ke lie jaroori haim। aise men bhojan mem haladi ka isatemaal jaroor karen। 3. naariyal tel (Coconut oil) naariyal tel men khaana banaane se bhi dimenshiya ka upachaar snbhav hai। naariyal tel men vasa ki maatara bahut jayaada nahin hoti aur yah dimaag ko bhi tej karata hai। 4. shaamil kiya jaana behad jaroori hai। ek din men do nde jaroor khaaen। 5. adarak (Ginger) adarak bhi dimenshiya se bachaav ke lie behad phaayademnd hai। adarak ki chaay (ginger tea), khaane mem adarak ka parayog ya sookha adarak (dry ginger), kisi bhi roop men adarak khaana dimenshiya men behad laabhadaayak hai। 6. garin ti (Green tea) garin ti bhi achachhe savaasathay v achachhe dimaagi vikaas ke hoti hai। 7. baadaam (Almond) baadaam bhi tej dimaag ke lie phaayademnd hota hai। baadaam ke tel men vasa hoti hai jise khaane se charabi nahim barhati aur dimaag ko anay poshak tatav (nutrient) bhi milate hain, jisase n keval sharir balaki dimaag bhi savasath hota hai। Disease: taaiphaaid (Typhoid) Description: taaiphaaid ya nt javar ek gnbhir bimaari hai। is bimaari men rogi ko tej bukhaar ke (salomonel typhi) naam ka yah baikatiriya (bacteria) paani, kisi pey ya khaane ke saath hamaare sharir ke ndar paravesh karata hai aur paachan tntar men jaakar yah baikatiriya barh jaate hain। yah se hota hai। taaiphaaid ke lakashanon men sir men darad (headache), pet men darad (pain in stomach) aur bukhaar ka homa hai lekim taaiphaaid ke bigarame par ulati (Vomitimg), daayariya (diarrhea), mal men khoon aana (blood in stool), livar ka barhana (enlargement of liver) aadi bhi ho sakate hain। taaiphaaid men laaparavaahi nahin baratani chaahie tatha isaka koras poora kiya jaana bhi jaroori hai kayonki isake dobaara hone ke chnses bhi rahate hai। taaiphaaid se nijaat ke lie yahn ham aapako kuchh ghareloo nusakhon ke baare men bataaenge jinahen apanaakar aap taaiphaaid se raahat pa sakate hain। 1. thnda paani (Cold water) kisi kapare ko thmde paani mem bhigokar sharir ko ponchhe। isake alaava thnde paani ki patatiyn sir par rakhane se bhi laabh hota he aur sharir ka taapamaan kam hota hai। kapare ko samay samay par badalate rahana chaahie। saamaamay bukhaar ke lie yah behad achachhi parakariya hai jo taapamaan ko barhane nahin deti। nota- isake lie baraph ya baraph ke paani ki isatemaal n karake, taaje paani ka isatemaal karen। 2. seb ka siraka (Apple cider vinegar) seb ka siraka bhi bukhaar ke lie behad sasati aur parabhaavi dava hai। isase bukhaar ko teji se door hota hai kayonki isamen maujood esid garamaahat ko sharir ki tavacha se baahar kar deta hai। saath hi isamen maujood minaral sharir ko bukhaar se door bhi rakhate hain। kaise karen upayog kisi kapare ko ek bhaag siraka aur do bhaag paani lekar usamen bhigoen। atirikat paani ko michor den aur is patati ko maathe aur pet par rakhen। ek patati pair ke talavon par bhi rakhi ja sakati hai। jaise hi kapara garam ho jaae, dobaara ghol men dubaaen aur parakariya ko doharaaen। 4. lahasun (Garlic) lahasun ki garam taasir bhi sharir men pasina laakara, sharir ka taapamaan kam kar sakati hai। yah sharir se din men is pey ko do baar pien। agale hi din aap bukhaar se raahat mahasoos karenge। do chamamach auliv auyal (olive oil) men do kali lahasun ki daalakar bhoonen। is tel ko thnda karake pair ke karane ke gun hote hain। laung ke tel men entibaikatiriyal (Antibacterial) gun hote hain jo ki baikatiriya ko maar dete hain। kaise karen upayog aath kap paani men 5 se 7 laung daalakar ubaal len। jab paani aadha rah jaae ise chhaan len। is paani ko poora din pien। is upachaar ko ek haphate lagaataar karen। Disease: joon (Lice) Description: joon (Head Lice) til ke aakaar ki ek chhoti parajivi hai jo manushay ke sharir mem paida ho jaati hain। saamaanayata: yah baalon men paaye jaate hain। ye bari teji se chal sakati hain। is kaaran baalom ke bich inahen khojama kathin ho jaata hai। ye sabhi umar tatha parajaatiyon ke logon ko snkaramit karati hain। Symptoms: - sir mem khujali hona Reasons: juen teji se, ek vayakati se doosare vayakati tak phail sakati hain। yah behad teji se chalati hain। juon ke phailane ke kuchh kaaran niman hain: juen phailane ke kaaran (Cause of Head Lices in Hindi) - haita, sakaarapha, knghi, barasha, heyar kalip athava baireta, heyar baimda, helamet athava kaparon, ka adala-badalakar isatemaal karate hain। - ek hi bisatara, palng athava kaalin ka parayog karate/karati hain। - bahut nikat rahakar khelate hain। - aise alamaari athava laokar mem rakhi gai, vasatuon ka parayog karate hain, jin men juen athava unake nde maujood hote hain। Treatments: kaise roke joon ko phailane se (Treatment of Head Lice in Himdi) - saamaanay shaimapoo se baal saaph karen, jab tak yah dho n liya jaae। - baalon par saphed siraka lagaaen - yah us ‘gonda’ ko dhila karane mem sahaayak hota hai, jo ‘likhom’ ko baalon se chipakaae hue hai। - baalon ko mahin kmghi se saaph karem, jisase ye nde nikal aaen। baalon ko idhara-udhar karake knghi karana upayogi ho sakata hai। - sabhi ndon ka hataaya jaana aavashayak hai। isamen 2 athava 3 ghnte ya adhik samay lag sakata haim, tatha yadi knghi kaam nahin karati hai to aapako haathon sn nde chunane par sakate hain। - parivaar men jitane logom ko joonem hain sab ka upachaar ek saath ho। - kapare bisatar aadi dhoop men rakhen ya garam paani men dhoen। - roosi - roosi - baalon ka jharana Home Remedies: joon ek chhota parajivi (parasite) hai jo baalon ki jaron aur baalon ke nichale hisase par chipake rahate hain, jahn yah sir ki tavacha se khoon ko pikar jinda rahate hain। bachachom men joon hone ki samasaya aam hai। yadi aap joon vaale kisi vayakati ke snparak men aate hain to yah aapako bhi ho sakate hain। saath hi inphekated vayakati ka saamaan jaise knghi aur kapare aadi isatemaal karane se bhi joon hone ki snbhaavana rahati hai। sir men joon hone ka sabase aam lakashan hai sir men khujali hona aur sir ki tavacha par laal chakatate paranaa। yah bahut teji se barhate hain isalie inahen jaladi khatam karana bahut mushakil hota hai। kuchh ghareloo upachaar ke davaara joon se nijaat paai ja sakati hai। aaie aapako bataaen aise hi kuchh ghareloo upachaar ke baare men- 1. lahasun (Garlic)- lahasun ki tej mahak juom ka dam ghotati hai aur unahen maar deti hai। kaise karen upayog aath se das lahasum ki kaliyon ko pisakar isamen ninboo ka ras milaaen aur baalon ki jaron men lagaaem। aadhe ghnte baad baalon ko garam paami se dho len। lahasun ki kaliyon ko pisakara, usamen khaane vaala tel milaaen। isake baad isamen shainpoo ya kndishanar men milaakar baalon men lagaaen। aadhe ghnte ke lie baalon ko yoon hi chhor den aur dho den। 2. bebi auyal (Baby oil)- bebi auyal men kapare dhone vaala ditarajent aur kuchh siraka milaakar baalon men lagaane se bhi joom ka ilaaj snbhav hai। bebi auyal bhi joon ka dam ghont deta hai jisase vah mar jaati haim। kaise karen upayog bebi auyal ko baalon men lagaakara, patale dnton vaali knghi se baal kaarhen। joon girani shuroo ho jaaengi। isake baad baalom ko ditarajent aur garam paani se dho len। sone jaane se pahale baalon men siraka lagaaen aur baalon ko shaavar kaip se dhak lem aur poori raat yoon hi chhor den। subah saamaanay shainpoo se baal dho len। shainpoo ke baad kndishanar karen। 3. auliv auyal (Olive oil)- auliv auyal bhi joon maarane men bahut parabhaavi hai। kaise karen upayog baalon men kisi bhi parakaar ka auliv auyal sone se pahale lagaaen। shaavar kaip lagaakar raat bhar tel ko baalon men yoon hi chhor den। subah men baalon ko knghi karem, joon baahar nikal aaengi। isake baad baalon ko shainpoo kar len। aadha kap auliv auyal men aadha kap kndishanar milaakar isamen kuchh likavid saabun milaaen। ise baalon ki jaron men lagaakar ek ghnta chhor den aur baal dho lem aur knghi karake joon baahar nikaal den। ise ek haphate baad dobaara doharaaen। 4. namak (Salt)- namak bhi joon nikaalane men behad asarakaari hai। kaise karen upayog ek chauthaai kap namak men itana hi siraka milaakar is ghol ko baalon men sapare karen। sapare kie hue gile baalon par shaavar kaip pahanen aur do ghmte yoon hi chhor den। isake baad baal dho len aur baalon par kndishanar karen। har tisare din is parakariya ko doharaaen। 5. petaroliyam jeli (Petrolium jelly)- petaroliyam jeli remgame vaale (roamimg around) juon ko turnt maar deti hai। kaise karen upayog sone se pahale baalon ki jaron men petaroliyam jeli lagaaem। isake baad kapare se baalon ko bndh kar so jaaen। subah bebi auyal se jeli hataaen aur knghi karake joom ko seb ke sirake (Apple cider vimegar) se dhoen। baalon ko poori rah sukhaakar jaron mem maariyal ka tel lagaaen। chhah se aath ghnton ke lie baalon ko yoon hi chhor den। isake baad baalon ko shainpoo karake knghi karen aur joom nikaalen। 7. saphed siraka (White vinegar) saphed sirake mem maujood esitik esid joon ko maarata hai। yah joon ko maarane ka surakashit aur sasata tarika hai। kisi tel men saphed siraka milaakar baalon men lagaakar kuchh ghnte chhor den aur phir shainpoo karen। Disease: kabaj (Constipation) Description: kabaj ek behad aam bimaari ban chuki hai। mal tayaag ek paraakaritik kariya hai। lekim jab mal tayaag karane men agar pareshaani aati hai to us samasaya ko kabaj (Kabj) kahate hain। aniyamit khaanapaan aur galat jivanashaili ke kaaran yah bimaari lagaataar barhati ja rahi hai। Symptoms: - ainthan ho, darad ho, pet phool jaae ya matali ho - aisa mahasoos ho ki aapaki ntariyn poori tarah se khaali nahin hui ho - mal tayaag ke lie zor lagaana pare Reasons: - aise aahaar jinamen charabi aur shakakar jayaada hon aur reshe kam hon। - kaaphi maatara men taral padaarath n lenaa। - nishakariy rahamaa। - jab aap ko mal tayaag ki ichachha ho tab shauchaalay m jaanaa। Treatments: kaise door karen kabaz (Treatmemt of Comstipation in Hindi) - din men kam se kam 8-10 gilaas paani pima chaahie। gunagune ya garam paani se aapaki nton ko aasaani se kaam karane nikalane men madad karate hain। - chiza, chaokalet aur anakaden aadi kam khaana chaahie kayonki inase kabaj (Kabj) barh sakati hai। - mal ko naram karane ke lie aaloo bukhaare ya seb ka ras pijie। - apani nton ko thik se kaam karane men madad karane ke lie kasarat kijie। - kabaj men paidal chalane se laabh hota hai। - jab aap ko mal tayaag karane ki ichachha ho, shauchaalay jaaen। - enima ka upayog karane se pahale apane chikitasak ki salaah len। Home Remedies: - ek chutaki kaala namak gunagune paani men daalen aur use subah khaali pet pikar 15 minat tak chahalakadami karen, kabaz mem avashay hi raahat milegi। - apane bhojan men mote anaaj (Bran) ka samaavesh karen। mausam ke anusaar upalabadh salaad ko shaamil karame se kabaj aur pet ki doosari tamaam samasayaaon se sathaai roop se chhutakaara paaya ja sakata hai। - alasi ke bij (Flaxseed) ka sevan bhi kabaz se aaraam dilaata hai। alasi ke bij ko subah kaoranaphalekas (Cornflax) ke saath milaakar kha sakate hain ya phir mutathi bhar alasi ke bij ko garam paani ke saath subah kha sakate hain। - kishamish phaaibara(Fiber) se bharapoor hoti hai aur paraakaritik julaab ki tarah kaam karati hai। १०-१२-kishamish ko raat men paani men bhigokar rakh den aur subah khaali pet khaaen। garabhaavasatha (Pregnancy) men mahilaao ko akasar kabaz ki shikaayat rahati hai, garabhavati mahilaaon (Pregnant Females)ke lie yah bahut laabhakaari upaay hai। - amarood (Gauva) bhi kabaz men bahut raahat pahunchaata hai। isake goode aur bij men phaaibar ki uchit maatara hota hai। isake sevan se khaana jaladi pach jaata hai aur esiditi (Acidity) se bhi raahat milati hai, saath hi pet bhi saaph ho jaata hai। - ek gilaas gunagune paami men ninboo (Lime) aur namak (Salt) milaakar subah khaali pet pine se bhi kabaz men kaaphi aaraam milata hai। Disease: uchach rakatachaap (High Blood Pressure) Description: haai balad pareshar ya uchach rakatachaap ki samasaya aajakal behad aam hoti ja rahi hai। uchach rakatachaap ke dauraan marij ke sharir men rakat ka paravaah behad tej ho jaata hai। is sathiti men aapake hariday ko adhik kaam karana parata hai। aaiye jaanem isase juri anay baaten: Symptoms: - ulati hone ki shikaayat aur chidachidaapan - kam mehanat karane par sns phoolanaa, thakaavat rahana - chakakar aana - tngon men darad - tanaav hona - naak se khoon aana - nind n aana - lagaataar siradarad honaa, sir chakaraana - sns lene men kathinaai - sir ke pichhe v garadan men darad - hariday ki dharakan tej rahana - hariday kashetar men pira mahasoos karana Reasons: uchach rakatachaap ke hone men bahut saare phaikataras aham bhoomika nibhaate hain jinamen se sabase mahatavapooran hai aasin jivanashaili। shaaririk sharam ki kami ke kaaran bhi kai baar yah bimaari logon ko pareshaan karati hai। uchach rakatachaap ke kai anay kaaran niman hain: uchach rakatachaap ke kaaran (Reason for High Blood Pressure) - dhoomarapaan - motaapa - nishakariyata - namak ka jayaada sevan - sharaab pina - tamaav - barhati umar - aanuvnshikata - paarivaarik itihaas - puraani kidani ki bimaari - thaairoid disaauradar Treatments: rakatachaap (Blood Pressure) barhane par kis tarah apana dhayaan rakhana isaki jaamakaari homa behad jaroori hai। saath hi samaya-samay par daokatari jnch is bimaari se bachaane men bahut kaaragar hoti hai। uchach rakatachaap se bachane ke kuchh paramukh upaay niman hain: - paratidin ek ghnta halaka ya tej kisi parakaar ka vayaayaam jaroor karen। - khaane men haai phaaibar vaale chijen leni chaahie। - khud ko ekativ rakhane ka adhik se adhik parayaas karama chaahie। - samaya-samay par daokatar ki salaah leni chaahie। Home Remedies: uchach rakatachaap (High Blood Pressure) yoon to jivanashaili se snbndhit ek saamaanay bimaari hai lekin yahi kai anay bari bimaariyon ki shuroovaat ya vajah bhi hai। kai baar uchach rakatachaap se vayakati ki maritayu tak snbhav hai। dil ki bimaariyn (Heart Disease), enajaaina (Engina) aur satarok (Stroke) aadi sabhi samasayaaem uchach rakatachaap ke kaaran hoti hain yahn tak ki kai baar shugar ke lie bhi uchach rakatachaap jimamedaar hota hai। haalnki yadi apane savaasathay ka dhayaan rakha jaae to kai ghareloo upaayon se bhi uchach rakatachaap ko thik kiya jaana snbhav hai। aaie jaamate hain kuchh aise hi ghareloo upachaaron ke baare men। uchach rakatachaap ke lie ghareloo nusakhe (Home Remedies for High Blood Pressure) lahasun (Garlic) lahasun ko khaali pet subah kachacha hi khaaen। lahasun men rakat ko patala karane ke gun hote hain jo ki rakat ka thakaka jamane se bhi rokata hai। chikitasak se paraamarash lekar lahasun kar parayog shuroo kar sakate hain। shahajan ki phali (Drum Sticks) shahajan men parotina, vitaamim aur anay poshak tatav maujood hote hain jo ki shaaririk savaasathay ki darishati se behad jaroori haim। shahajan ka upayog karane ka aasaan tarika hai ki isaki phaliyon ko daal ke saath banaakar khaaya jaae। isase bhi uchach rakatachaap naoramal hota hai। nvala (Indian Gooseberry) nvala men vitaamin si ki uchach maatara hoti hai jo ki sharir se kolesataraol (cholesterol) ki maatara ko kam karati hai। isase dil savasath rahata hai aur uchach rakat chaap niymtarita। mooli (Radish) rasoighar men parayog hone vaali aam sabaji hai mooli, lekin isamen uchach rakatachaap ko miyntarit karane ke gun hote hain। mooli ko salaad ke roop mem kachacha ya dahi ke saath milaakar khaaya ja sakata hai। til (Sesame) til daayasatolik aur sisatolik (Diastolic and Systolic) , donon tarah ke rakatachaap ko niyntarit karata hai। til ke tel men sisamin (Sesamin) aur sisaminaol (Sesaminol) donon hote hain jo ki sharir ke tamaav ko kam karane men aham bhoomika nibhaate hain। til ka khaane men parayog karane se uchach rakatachaap ko miyntarit kiya ja sakata hai। til ke ladadoo ya til ka paaudar salaad ya daal sabaji mem upar se chhirakakar khaane se laabh hota hai। alasi ke bij (Flex Seed) alasi ke bij omegaa-3 phaiti esid men se ek hai jisase isamen alapha linolemik esid (Alf Linolenic Acid) naamak yaugik ki uchach maatara hoti hai। yah uchach rakatachaap ko niyntarit karane ke saath hi kelaosataraol ki maatara bhi ghataata hai jisase hariday bhi savasath bamata hai। Disease: dnt ka darad (Toothache) Descriptiom: dnt hamaare sharir ka mahatavapooran hisasa haim। baat musakuraane ki ho ya kuchh khaane ki bina dnt sab bekaar hai। lekin kisi bhi kaaran yadi dnton men darad ho jaae to vayakati baichen ho jaata hai। dntom ka darad yoon to ek aam samasaya hai, lekim isaka darad asahaniy hota hai। Symptoms: - chabaane men darad hona - bukhaara, siradarad - sns lene men kathinaai Reasons: dmton men darad ke kai kaaran ho sakate hain। dnton ki thik se saphaai n karanaa, dnton men kaiviti hona ya atayadhik mitha khaanaa। isake saath hi chaay kaaphi jayaada pinaa। isake saath hi kuchh anay kaaran bhi hain jaise: dnton men darad ka kaaran (Causes of Tooth Pain) 1. masooron men inphekashana- yadi kisi bhi kaaran se masoorom men inphekashan hai to yah dmt darad ka kaaran ho sakata hai। isake kaaran tooth inemal (Tooth Emamel) ki samasaya bhi hoti hai। isase dnton men thnda garam laganaa, munh ka savaad bigaranaa, garadan ki galaind men soojam aanaa, masooron men soojan aamaaaadi samasayaaem a sakati haim। 2. kaivitija- isake kaaran dmton ki upari parat nashat ho jaati hai। kaorabohaaidaret vaala khaana jisamen bareda, soda kek ya kaindi aadi dnton par chipak jaae aur achachhi tarah se saaph m ho to kaiviti (Cavity) ho sakati hai jisaka parinaam hota hai dnton mem darada। 3. dnt men kiraa- isase dnt poori tarah khokhala ho jaata hai aur unamen khaana bhar jaata hai। jo ki darad ka kaaran bamata hai। darad ke kaaran dnt kaam mahin karata aur un par ek parakaar ki gndagi jamane lagati hai। 4. toote dnta- kuchh khaate vakat ya kisi anay kaaran se yadi dnt toot gae hain to aise dnton men darad ki shikaayat akasar rahati hai। aise dnton ke inemal kamajor ho jaati hai jisase ye sensitiv ho jaate hain। 5. philinga- yadi dnton men philing (Tooth Filling) karaai gai ho to yah bhi kai baar yah dnt darad ka kaaran ho sakati hai। Treatments: ​dnt darad hone par thnde paani se kulala karana phaayademnd hota hai lekin agar isase pooran aaraam nahin mil paae to niman upaay karane chaahie: - koi penakilar len। - aais paik ya taovel mem aais lapetakar use gaalon par kuchh der ke lie rakhen। agar gaalon men soozan a jaae aur darad ho to pharozen piz ko aaisapaik ki jagah lagaaen। ye chehare ke aakaar ke anusaar badal sakate hain। - agar do dinon mem darad nahin jaata to denatisat (Dentist) ke paas jaaem। ho sakata haim zayaada kaeviti ya karaik ki vajah se darad ho। - dnt ka daokatar aapake munh ki jmch karega aur ekasa-re legaa। phir dnt ka daokatar dnt ko thik karega ya nikaal degaa। aapako darad mivaarak davaaen ya entibaayotik leme ke lie kaha ja sakata hai। daokatar ki bataai gai davaaen len। Home Remedies: dmton ka darad vaise to ek saamaanay samasaya hai, lekin isaka darad asahaniy hota hai। yadi aapako bhi kabhi dnt men darad ho to ghabaraaen nahim, kuchh ghareloo upaay apanaakar aap is takaliph se bach sakate hain। 1. launga- yadi dnt men darad ho to laung ka tel rooi men bhigokar dnt par lagaaie। koshish kijie ki tel masooron par n lage kayonki isase halaki jalan mahasoos ho sakati hai। 2. elakohala- ji hn aapane thik parha elakohala। ek sip elakohal se kulala karame par bhi darad men aaraam milata hai। isase darad vaala hisasa sunan ho jaata hai। lekin sathaai yah ilaaj nahin hai। 3. vikasa- vikas ko apane chehare ke us hisase ki taraph lagaaie jis taraph dnt men darad ho। isake baad chehare ko dhnk len। isase darad men aaraam milata hai। 4. aaisa- baraph ke tukare se sikaai karane par bhi dnt darad men behad aaraam milata hai। 5. kaali miracha- kaali mirach ke paaudar ko masooron par ragarane se bhi darad ka hisasa sunan ho jaata hai aur darad men aaraam milata hai। 6. kachachi payaaja- kachachi payaaj ko 3 minat tak darad vaale hisase par ragaren, isase bhi darad men bahut aaraam milata hai। 7. lahasuna- lahasun ki kali ko chabaakar usake ras ko laar ke saath milakaar kulala karen। kuchh hi sekend men darad men aaraam milegaa। 8. vamila araka- vanila arak ki kuchh boonde rooi men lekar darad vaale hisase par lagaaen। dnt darad men aaraam milegaa। 9. gehoon ke paudhe ka rasa- mkurit gehoon ke paudhe ka ras bhi kulale ke roop men parayog kar dnt darad se bacha ja sakata hai। yah masooron ke visham padaarathon ko nikaalakar jivaanuon ki varidadhi ko rokata hai। 10. pairaokasaaida- dnton mem darad hone par pairaokasaaid se kulala karen। lekin dhayaan rahe ise kabhi nigalen nahin। isase bhi dnt darad mem aaraam milata hai। Disease: dengoo (Dengue) Description: dengoo, maada edij (Female Aedes) machachhar ke kaatane se hota hai। ye machachhar din men, khaasakar subah kaatate hain। marij men agar jatil tarah ke dengoo ka ek bhi lakashan dikhaai de to use jaladi - se - jaladi daokatar ke paas le jaaen। diechaeph ( DHF - Dengue Hemorrhagic Fever) aur diesaes (DSS - Dengue Shock Syndrome) bukhaar dengoo ke do parakaar hain jinamen paletaletas (Platelets) kaaphi kam ho jaate hain, jisake kaaran sharir ke jaroori ngon par bura asar par sakata hai। Symptoms: - ulati v sharir par laala-laal daane nikal aate hain - kamajori ho jaati hai aur chakakar aate hain - dengoo bukhaar ke lakashan aam bukhaar se thore alag hote hain - dengoo shaok sindarom (DSS) ke marijon men saadhaaran dengoo bukhaar aur dengoo haimarejik bukhaar ke lakashanen ke saatha-saath bechaini mahasoos ho - dengoo hemorejik bukhaar men uparokat lakashanon ke alaava paletaletas ki kami se sharir men kahin se bhi khoon bahana shuroo ho sakata hai, jaise naak se, dnton v masooron se, khoon ki ulati v mal men khoon aana aadi - thakaavat v kamajori hai - naari kabhi tej aur kabhi dhire chalanelagati hai aur rakat chaap (Blood Pressure) ekadam kam ho jaata hai - bukhaar bahut tej hota hai - siradarada, kamar v joron men darad hota hai - halaki khnsi v gale men kharaash mahasoos hoti hai Reasons: - khaali baratanon ko ulata karake rakhem। - pakashiyon ke khaame- pine ke baratanom ko har roj saaph karen। - agar ghar men koolar hai to usaka paani do ya tin din baad avashay badalen। - ghar men sathit haudiyom, tainkaron mem paani ko saaph rakhane ke lie usamem kalorin ki do chaar goliym daal den। - ghar ke aasa- paas ya chhat par pare bekaar taayara, tayooba, toote hue matake, khaali dibabon aadi men barasaat ka paani ikathatha n hone dem। - paarak men jaate samay ya aisi jagah jaate samay jahn machachharon ke kaatane ka khatara ho, vahn poori baajoo ke kapare pahanane chaahie taaki machachhar na kaaten। - machachharon se bachane ke lie karima, machachharadaani aur amay upaayon ka isatemaal karana chaahie। Treatments: dengoo se bachaav ka sabase behatarin upaay hai gndagi ka jama na home denaa। agar maada edij machachhar panapenge hi to dengoo hone ki aashnka bhi behad kam hogi। dengoo hone par niman upaay karane chaahie: - saadhaaran dengoo bukhaar ka ilaaj ghar par hi ho sakata hai। marij ko poora aaraam karame den। use har chhah ghnte men pairaasitaamol (Paracetamol) dem aur baara- baar paani aur taral chijen ( miboo paani, chhaachha, naariyal paani aadi ) pilaaem। - bachachon ka khaas khayaal rakhen। - bukhaar kam hone ke baad bhi eka-do din men ek baar paletaletas kaaunt tesat jaroor karaaem। demgoo men marij ke rakatachaapa, khaasakar upar aur miche ke rakatachaap ke ntar par lagaataar nigaraani ( din men 3-4 baar ) rakhana jaroori hai। donon rakatachaap ke bich ka pharak 20 digari ya usase kam ho jaae to sathiti khataranaak ho sakati hai। rakatachaap girane se marij behosh ho sakata hai। - bachache naajuk hote hain aur umaka imayoon sisatam (Immune System of Kids) kamajor hota hai isalie bimaari unahen jaladi pakar leti hai। aise men unaki bimaari ko najarndaaj n karen। - bachache khule men jayaada rahate hain isalie inaphekashan hone aur machachharon se kaate jaane ka khatara unamem jayaada hota hai। - bachachon ghar se baahar poore kapare pahanaakar bhejen। - machachharon ke mausam men bachachon ko nikar v ti - sharat n pahanaaen। - raat men machachhar bhagaane ki karim lagaaen। - agar bachacha bahut jayaada ro raha ho, lagaataar soe ja raha ho, bechain ho, use tej bukhaar ho, sharir par raishej hon, ulati ho ya inamen se koi bhi lakashan ho to phauran daokatar ko dikhaaem। - aamataur par chhote bachachon ko bukhaar hone par unake haath - pnv to thnde rahate hain lekin maatha aur pet garam rahate hain isalie unake pet ko chhookar aur rekatal temaparechar lekar unaka bukhaar chek kiya jaata hai। bagal se taapamaan lena sahi tarika nahim hai, khaasakar bachachon men। agar bagal se taapamaan lena hi hai to jo riding aae, usamen 1 digari jor den। use hi sahi riding maana jaaegaa। - bachache ko dengoo ho to use asapataal men rakhakar hi ilaaj karaana chaahie kayonki bachachon men paletaletas jaladi girate hain aur unamen dihaaidareshan (paani ki kami) bhi jaladi hota hai। Home Remedies: dengoo edij machachhar (Adeej Mosquito) davaara phailane vaali bimaari hai jo ki haal ke samay men teji se barh rahi hai। dengoo ke baare men sabase khaas baat yah hai ki isake machachhar din ke samay kaatate hain tatha yah machachhar saaph paani (Cleam Water) men panapate hain। dengoo ke dauraan rogi ke joron men tej darad (Pain im Joints) hota hai tatha sir men bhi darad (Headache) kaaphi tej hota hai। baron ke satar bahut teji se niche girata hai jisase kai baar ndarooni rakatasataraav (Internal Bleeding) hone ki snbhaavana bhi rahati hai। dengoo se bachaav ke lie kuchh ghareloo upaay bhi hain jinahem apamaakar demgoo se bachaav smbhav hai। aaie aapako bhi bataate haim ki kaun se ghareloo upaay aapako dengoo se bacha sakate hain- dengoo ke lie ghareloo nusakhe (Home Remedies for Dengue) dhamiya patati (Coriander Leaves) dengoo ke bukhaar se raahat ke lie dhamiya patati ke joos ko taonik ke roop men piya ja sakata hai। yah bukhaar ko kam karata hai। nvala (Indian Gooseberry) mvala men vitaamin si ki uchach maatara hoti hai jisase ki sharir men ebajaorab karane ki kashamata barhati hai। isase sharir jayaada lauh tatav ebajaorab kar paata hai jo ki demgoo ke bukhaar ko thik karane ke lie jaroori hai। tulasi (Basil) tulasi ke pataton ko garam paani men ubaalakar chhaanakara, rogi ko pine ko den। tulasi ki yah chaay dengoo rogi ko behad aaraam pahunchaati hai। yah chaay dinabhar men tin se chaar baar li ja sakati hai। papite ki patati (Papay Leaves) papite ki patatiyn, dengoo ke bukhaar ke lie sabase asarakaari dava kahi jaati hai। papite ki patatiyon men maujood papen enjaaim (papain enjymes) sharir ki paachan shakati ko thik karata hai, saath hi sharir men paraatin ko gholane ka kaam karata hai। dengoo ke upachaar ke lie papite ki patatiyon ka joos nikaal kar ek ek chamamach karake rogi ko den। is joos se paletaletas ki maatara teji se barhati hai। bakari ka doodh (Goat Milk) dengoo bukhaar ke lie ek aur buhat parabhaavashaali dava hai bakari ka doodha। bahut kam hochuki paletaletas ko bhi bakari ka doodh turnt barhaane ki kashamata rakhata hai। dengoo ke upachaar ke lie rogi ko bakari ka kachacha doodh thoraa-thora karake pilaaen, isase paletaletas barhenge aur joron ke darad men bhi aaraam milegaa। chiraayata (Chirayta) chiraayata men bukhaar ko thik karane ke gum hote hain। dengoo ke bukhaar ko bhi chiraayata ke isatemaal se thik kiya ja sakata hai। dhatoora (Dhatura) dhatoore ki patatiyon men dengoo ke bukhaar ko thik karane ke gun hote hain, lekin isaki khuraak 2 desigaraam se adhik nahin honi chaahie। methi ke patate (Femugreek Leaves) methi ke patate bhi dengoo ke bukhaar ko thik kar sakate hain। methi ke pataton ko paami men ubaalakar harabal chaay ke roop men isaka payog kiya ja sakata hai। methi se sharir ke vishaakat padaarath baahar nikal jaate hain jisase dengoo ke vaayaras bhi khatam hote haim। anaar aur kaale mgoor (Pomegramate amd Black Grapes) demgoo bukhaar men rakat ki kami ko poora karane aur paletaletas ke satar ko barhaane ke lie anaar aur kaale ngoor ka ras pina chaahie। sntare ka joos (Orange juice) vitaamim si se bharapoor sntaraa, paachan shakati ko barhaava deta hai saath hi sharir ka imayooniti bhi barhaata hai। aise men dengoo rogi ko jalad se jalad savasath hone ke lie sntare ke ras ka sevan karana chaahie। Disease: maleriya (Malaria) Description: maleriya bukhaar ke kaaran parativarash ki kai log apani jaan gnva dete hain। gmde paami men panapane vaale machachharon ke kaatame se phailani vaali is bimaari ke vishay men jaanakaari behad kaaragar hai। aaie jaanen maleriya rahata hai Reasons: - aasapaan maujood paani ko samay par ma badalana - rahane ke sathaan ke aasapaas gndagi hona - paani ka jamaav hona - machachharon ke ndon ka jama hona Treatments: maleriya ka paraathamik upachaar (Treatmemt of Malari in Hindi) - maleriya mem kalorokavin jaisi enti-maleriyal dava (Chloroquine- Anti malarial medicine) di jaati hai। in davaaon ke saaid - iphekatas ho sakate hain, isalie inahen daokatar ki salaah ke bina n len। - marij ko poora aaraam karane den। use har chhah ghnte men pairaasitaamol (Paracetamol in Malaria) den aur baara- baar paani aur taral chijen ( niboo paani , chhaachh , naariyal paami aadi ) pilaaen। - maleriya bukhaar ke dauraan bachachon ka khaas khayaal rakhen। - bachache naajuk hote hain aur unaka imayoon sisatam kamajor hota hai isalie bimaari unahen jaladi pakar leti hai। aise men unaki bimaari ko najarndaaj n karen। - bachache khule men jayaada rahate hain isalie imaphekashan hone aur machachharom se kaate jaane ka khatara unamen jayaada hota hai। - bachachon ghar se baahar poore kapare pahanaakar bhejen। - machachharon ke mausam men bachachon ko mikar v ti - sharat n pahanaaen। - raat men machachhar bhagaame ki karim lagaaem। - agar bachacha bahut jayaada ro raha ho , lagaataar soe ja raha ho , bechain ho , use tej bukhaar ho , sharir par chakatate (Rashes) hon, ulati ho ya imamen se koi bhi lakashan ho to phauram daokatar ko dikhaaen। - aamataur par chhote bachachon ko bukhaar hone par unake haath - pnv to thnde rahate hain lekin maatha aur pet garam rahate hain isalie unake pet ko chhookar aur rekatal temaparechar lekar unaka bukhaar chek kiya jaata hai। bagal se taapamaan lena sahi tarika nahin hai , khaasakar bachachon men। agar bagal se taapamaan lena hi hai to jo riding aae, usamen 1 digari jor den। use hi sahi ridimg maama jaaegaa। Home Remedies: maleriya bukhaar ke dauraan tej sir darad (Headache), jor ki thmd ke saath knp knpi (Shivrimg) honaa, mnsapeshiyon me bhaynkar darad hona (Muscle pain) aur behad kamajori jaise lakashan mahasoos hote hain। bukhaar utarate samay pasina hota hai। sharir ka taapamaan 104 digari se bhi jayaada ho sakata hai। ji ghabaraana aur pitat ki karavi ulati hona aur paratidin nishachit samay par bukhaar charhama bhi maleriya ka paramukh lakashan hai। jaanie maleriya se raahat ke ghareloo upaay (Home Remedies for Malaria) 1. choona (Chuna)- tin garaam choona lem, ise 60 mili paani mem gholen। ek ninboo isamen nichoren। maleriya bukhaar ki snbhaavana hone par yah misharan pien। yah nusakha paratidin lene se bukhaar se raahat milati hai। 2. chiraayataa- (Chirata)- chiraayata maleriya bukhaar ki sabase asaradaayak aushadhi maani gai hai। ek paav garam paami men 15 garaam chiraayata milaaen, kuchh laumg aur daalachini bhi mila den। is paani ke isatemaal se bhi maleriya bukhaar utarane lagata hai। 3. minboo (Lemon)- garam paani men ninboo ka ras milaakar pine se bukhaar ki tivarata ghatane lagati hai। 4. phitakari (Alum)- thodi si fitakari tave par bhoonakar chooran bama len। aadha chamamach paaudar bukhaar aane ke 3 ghmte pahale paani se pien। baad men har doosare ghnte par yah dava lete rahane se bukhaar khatam hota hai। 5. tulasi patata (Basil leaves)- jab bukhaar n ho, 10 garaam tulasi ke pataton ke ras mem aadha chamamach kaali mirach ka paaudar milaakar chaat len। isase maleriya bukhaar khatam ho jaata hai। 6. shahad (Honey)- ek gilaas paani len। isamen ek chamamach daalachini, ek chamamach shahad aur aadha chamamach kaali mirach ka paaudar milaakar garam karen। thnda home par piem, yah ataynt laabhakaari nusakha hai। 7. dhatoora (Dhatoora)- dhatoora ki nai kopal 2 nag lekar gur ke saath achachhi tarah milaakar isaki goli bana len। imahen din men 2 baar leme se maleriya khatam ho jaata hai। 8. anam n khaaem (Avoid solid food)- maleriya hone par anan n khaaen। keval phal aur paani lete rahen। aisa karane se bukhaar se jaladi laabh milata hai। 9. adarak (Ginger)- ek gilaas paani men 10 garaam adarak aur 10 garaam munakaka daalakar itana ubaalen ki aadha rah jaaya। thnda hone par pien। 10. amarood (Guava)- ek bara amarud garam raakh men bhoon len। yah amarood khaana bhi, maleriya rogi ke lie laabhakaari hai। 11. thndi patati rakhen (Cold compress)- tej bukhaar ki haalat men maathe par thnde paani ki patati rakhane se taapamaan niche a jaata hai। thnde paami men gila kiya taavel saare sharir par lapetane se turnt laabh milata hai। 12. payaaj ka ras (Onion juice)- payaaj ka ras maleriya men laabhakaari hai। 5 mili ras men 4 kaali mirach ka paaudar milaakar din men 3 baar pine se laabh hota hai। 13. jaamun (Black berry)- jaamun ke per ki chhaal sukhaakar pis len। 5 garaam choorana, gur ke saath dim men 3 baar lene se maleriya se raahat milati hai। Disease: chhimkama (Sneezing) ke upaay (Remedies for Sneezing in Hindi) Home Remedies: chhinkana (Sneezing), bhale hi aapako pareshaan karata ho lekina, yah vaasatav men aapako kai tarah ki elaraji se bachaane ki savabhaavik vayaayaam karana chaahie। - subah ki dhoop ka sevan laabhadaayak hota hai। - sharaab aur kisi anay nashe se door rahana chaahie। Home Remedies: ausatiyoporosis (Osteoporosis) hadadiyon men hone vaali samasaya hai, jisamen hadadiyon ka biemadi (Bone Mineral Density) leval kam ho jaata hai, jisase hadadiyon ke tootane ka khatara barh jaata hai। ausatiyoporosis men hadadiyn patali ya khokhali hokar kamajor ho jaati hain। hamaari hadadiyn kai tarah ke minaral se milakar bani hoti hain, jo ki umar ke saath kam home lagate hain। kai baar to hadadiyn itami kamajor ho jaati hain ki maamooli si chot se bhi toot jaati haim। ausatiyoporosis parotina, vitaamin di aur kailashiyam ki kami ki vajah se hota hai aur mahilaaen isaki jayaada rogi milati hain। aaie aapako bataate hain ki kis tarah ghareloo upaayon ko apanaakar aap ausatiyoporosis se bach sakati hain। ausatiyoporosis ke lie ghareloo nusakhe (Home Remedies for Osteoporosis) paroonas (Prunes) paroonas yaani sookhe palama, khaane se (sela) se bane hote hain। kainsar in koshikaaon ka ek rog hai। baresat kainsar duniya mem teji se phailane vaali khataranaak bimaariyon men se ek hai। baresat kainsar (Breast Cancer) ya satan kainsar
