bamaavat ( shape or texture) mem koi badalaav hai? kaya satanon ke aakar ya aakariti (size or shape) men koi badalaav hai (koi ek satan doosare ke mukaabale chhota ya bara haim)? satanon ki tavacha ki banaavat men koi badalaav jaise fati fati si ya koi gadada sa par jaanaa? rng men badalaav jaise ki nipapalas ke aasapaas surakh laal rnga.ho jaanaa? kaya nipapal ki disha sahi hai, kahin vah ndar ki taraph to nahi mur gaya hai? kisi bhi nipapal se taral padaaradh ka risanaa? nipapal ke aas paas kisi paradaarath ka risana ya papari ka jamanaa? C - CHECK any unusual findings with your doctor (kuchh asaamaanay sa mahasoos ho to turnt hi daokatar se salaah len) kaya aapako kuchh asaamaanay ya alag sa mahasoos ho raha hai? agar aisa hai to turnt hi daokatar se salaah len। samay samay par apane satanon ki jnch savayn karate rahem aisa karane se aap umame saamaanay taur par aane vaale badalaavom aur asaamaanay badalaav ke baare mem jaan jaayenge, akasar maasik dharam (Menses) ke samay satanon men kuchh badalaav avashay aata hai। lakashanon ke ubharane ka intazaar n karen, niyamit roop se satanon ki jnch karavaaen। yah saravavidit hai ki rokathaam ilaaz se behatar hai Reasons: baresat kainsar ke kaaran (Reason for Breast Cancer) kai log maanate hain ki baresat kainsar anuvnshik hota hai jo poori tarah sahi tathay nahin hai। satan ya baresat kainsar ke kuchh aham kaaran niman hain: - aayu-satan kainsar hone ka jokhim aayu ke saath barhata hai। - yadi aapako pahale kainsar ya satan ka koi anay rog hua ho। - paarivaarik itihaas - keval 5–10% satan kainsar hi anuvnshik roop se paraapat jin ke kaaran hote hain। satan kainsar ka khatara kin mahilaaon ko jayaada hota hai? - adhik umar ki mahilaaen। - jin mahilaaon ki mn, bahan ya beti ko satan kainsar hua ho - janam ke samay se hi karomozom (gunasootaro) men badalaav ho। - mahila jise bachache na hue hon, ya 30 saal ki umar ke baad bachache hue hon। - jise 12 saal ki umar se pahale hi piriyadas shuru ho gae hom। - jis mahila ko 50 saal ki umar ke baad menopaoj (rajonivaritati) hui ho। - jis mahila ki satan ke utak kaaphi ghane hon। aapaki memogaraaphi karake daokatar ye jaanakaari de sakate hai। - jo mahila garabh nirodhak goliyon ka lnbe arase se isatemaal kar rahi ho। - jo mahila din men 2 se 5 baar sharaab ka sevan karati ho। - jis mahila ko menopaoj ke baad jayaada motaapa a gaya ho। - jis mahila ne haaramon ripalesament therepi isatemaal ki ho। - jo mahilaaen apane bachachon ko satanapaan nahin karavaatin। haaramon snbndhi kaarak esatarojan aur parojesatarojan naamak haaramon se lnbe samay tak samaparak mem aame se aapaka satan kaimsar ka jokhim barh sakata hai। jivanashaili smbndhi kaarak lamabe samay tak paratidim do peg se jayaada sharaab pina tatha dhoomarapaan se aapaka satan kainsar ka jokhim barh sakata hai| vajan jayaada hona bhi satan kainsar ka kaaram ban sakata hai। Treatments: - agar aapako thora sa bhi snshay ho to turmt daokatar ki salaah lijiye। - chhote satan Home Remedies: satan kainsar (Breast cancer), sabase aam kainsar men se ek hai। satan kainsar ek knpalekas bimaari (Complex disease) hai jisake hone ke lie kai phaikatara, jaise aanuvnshik (Heredity), khaana-paan aur jivan shaili jimamedaar hote hain। chikitasa visheshajanyon ki maanen to aame vaale samay men satan kaimsar se pirit rogiyon ki snkhaya aur bhi teji se barhagi। haalnki jivan shaili men badalaav karake satan kainsar se kaaphi had tak bacha ja sakata hai। jaanie satan kainsar se bachaav ke ghareloo upachaar (Home Remedies for Breast Cancer): 1. garin ti (Green tea)- ek gilaas paani men harabal garin ti ko aadha hone tak ubaalen aur phir use pien। yah phaayademnd hoti hai aur isase satan kainsar ka khatara kaaphi kam ho jaata hai। 2. ngoor aur amaar ka joos (Grapes and pomegranate juice)- rojaana ngoor ya anaar ka joos pine se satan kainsar se bacha ja sakata hai। in donon phalon ke joos men kainsar ke selas ko maarane ki kashamata hoti hai, jisase satan kainsar ka khatara kam ho jaata hai। 3. lahasun (Garlic)- lahasun men phalevonas (flavons) aur phalevonolas (flavonols) jaise enti baikatiriyal tatav hote hain। roj lahasun ka sevan karane se satan kainsar ki snbhaavana ko roka ja sakata hai। 4. haladi (Turmeric)- haladi men karakayoomin (curcumin) naam ka tatav hota hai jo ki vibhinan tarah ke kainsar ko thik karame men sakasham hai। haladi ke sevan se kaimsar sel barhane ki snbhaavana kam hoti hai tatha kainsar thik hota hai। 5. tamaatar (Tomato)- tamaatar khaane se bhi mahilaaen satan kainsar se bachi rah sakati hain। tamaatar mem laayakopin (lycopene) hota hai jo ki ek shakatishaali entiaukasident hai aur kainsar ko barhane se rokata hai। 6. paalak (Spinach)- paalak men entiaukasident layootin (lutin) hota hai jo kainsar se bachaane mem sahaayak hai। haphate men do se tin baar paalak khaana chaahie jisase satan kaimsar se bacha ja sakata hai। 7. barokali (Broccoli)- barokali men kainsar se larane vaale tatava, indola-3-kaarabinol (indole-3-carbinol) hota hai jo ki satan kainsar ke selas ki garoth ko kam kar dete hain। barokali ke niyamit sevan se kainsar se bacha ja sakata hai। barokali ke saath patata gobhi aur gobhi ko milaakar khaana chaahie। 8. akharot (Wallnut)- akharot men bahut se poshak tatav hote hain jo satan kainsar ki garoth ko kam kar dete hain isalie akharot ka rojaana sevan karana chaahie। 9. balooberi (Blueberries)- balooberi vitaamin aur mimaral se bharapoor hoti hain। inamen emtiaukasident elejik bhi hote hain jo satan kainsar se bachaav karate hain। baloobairi ke saath sataraoberi aur balaikaberi bhi behad phaayademnd hoti hai। Disease: siradarad (Headache) Description: siradarad ek aam samasaya hai। sir ke kisi bhi hisase men darad ho sakata hai aur yah darad keval lakashan hota hai jo ki sir ki kisi bimaari ko darashaata hai। kai baar bahut jayaada tamaav lene, thakaavat hone, bhookhe rahane, garami tej hone ya kisi aam shaaririk samasaya jaise ki bukhaar ya jukaam ke kaaran bhi sir darad ho sakata hai। Symptoms: - uchach rakat chaap hona - kabaj ya dasat hona - jayaada sharaab pina - tanaavagarasat hona - pet thik n hona Reasons: sir darad ke kaarana- (Cause of Headache) sir ka darada, dimaag men rakat koshikaaon (blood vessels) aur shiraaom (merves) ke aapas men takaraane se hota hai। darad ke samay rakat koshika ki ek nishachit sira aur sir ki mmsapeshiym sakariy hoti hain aur dimaag ko darad ka siganal bhejati hain। jisase sir darad mahasoos hota hai। sir darad ke anay kaaran (Other Reasons of headache) 1. jab vayakati kisi chij ko lekar khud par dabaav mahasoos karata hai ya kisi sathiti ya parisathiti ko lekar asamnjas mem hota hai। aise mem usaka mam ashnt ho jaata hai aur dimaag par jayaada gahara parabhaav parata hai jisake kaaran tanaav hota hai aur sir darad hone lagata hai। 2. dimaag ki rakat vaahiniyon men badalaav hone se home vaale darad ko maaigaren ka darad kaha jaata hai। is tarah ke sir darad mem sir ke kisi ek hisase men chubhan bhara darad hota hai aur darad ke saath ji michalaane, gais aur ulati jaisi samasayaaen bhi hoti hain। itana hi nahin vayakati photophobiya (roshani se pareshaani) aur phonophobiya (shor se pareshaani) se bhi pareshaani mahasoos karata hai। parayaapat nind n leme, bhookhe rahane ya kam paani pine se maaigaren ho sakata hai। 3. kuchh mahilaaen haaramon men badalaav ke dauraan gnbhir sir darad mahasoos karati haim। yah sathiti momopoja, maasik sataraava, ovelayooshan aadi ke dauraan bhi ho sakati hai। maasik sataraav men utaara charhaav se bhi is tarah ka sir darad bana rah sakata hai। 4. kuchh khaas tarah ki davaaiyon ka jayaada din tak lene ke kaaran ribaaund siradarad ki samasaya ho ho sakati hai। kai bimaariyn aisi hoti hain jinamen davaaiyn lnbe samay tak chalati hain, aise men yah masatishak ko parabhaavit kar sakati hain। is tarah ka sir darad davaaen bnd hone ke saath khud hi bnd ho jaata hai। 5. dmt darad se bhi sir ki nasen parabhaavit hoti hain। dnt aur sir ki nasen jabare par jaakar milati hain jisase dnt aur sir ek doosaren ko kanekat karate hain। jisase dnt men kisi bhi tarah ki takaliph hone se sir men darad home lagata hai। 6. chaay aur kaophi ke aadi logon ko yadi samay par chaay n mile to bhi unahen sir darad ki shikaayat ho sakati hai। 7. kuchh logon ko subah uthate hi siradarad ki shikaayat hoti hai jabaki kuchh der baad yah apane aap thik ho jaata hai। kai baar raat men achachhi nind n lene ya bhookhe pet sone ke kaaran subah subah sir darad ho sakata hai। 8. nkhon men kisi tarah ki samasaya hone, nkh kamajor hone, chashama n pahaname ya kntekat lains men garabari hone se sir darad ho sakata hai। aisi koi bhi samasaya jisase nkhon par tamaav parata ho, sir darad hone ki vajah ho sakata hai। aise men yadi koi vayakati sir darad se pareshaan hai to use apani mkhon ko bhi jaroor chaik karaama chaahie। 9. kuchh logon ko aaisakarim ya bahut thndi chijon ko khaane se bhi sir darad ki shikaayat ho sakati hai। aaisakarim ya bahut thndi chijen khaane ke baad maathe ke bich men bhaaripan mahasoos hota hai jisase sir darad shuroo ho jaata hai। is tarah ka darad aaisakarim khaane ke turnt baar shuroo ho jaata hai। Treatments: sir darad se raahat ke lie tipasa- (Tips to Prevent Headache) Home Remedies: aajakal ki tej bhaagati jindagi aur vayasat jivanashaili men tanaav aur saradarad ek aam bimaari ho gai hai। saradarad ke kai kaaran hote hain। sir men rakat pahunchaane vaali naariyon men snkuchana, sanaayu tntar ki asamaanay gatividhi, jayaada dhoomarapaan karanaa, jayaada alakohal lenaa, sharir men paani ki kami, jayaada der tak bevajah sonaa, darad nivaarak davaaon ka jayaada sevan karanaa, saradi-jukaama, bukhaar samet aise kai vajah hain, jisase saradarad hoti hai। yahn yah jaanana jaruri hai ki saamaanay saradarad aur maaigaren ke saradarad mem ntar hai। maaigaren men saradarad kaaphi pareshaani vaala hota hai aur yah ek gnbhir bimaari bhi hai। saradarad ya kisi bhi tarah ke saradarad men jaladi elopaithik darad nivaarak dava khaana sehat ke lie nukasaanadeh hota hai, kayonki jayaada pen kilar khaame se kidani aur livar daimej hote hain। elopaithik davaaon se behatar hai ki ham aise kuchh ghareloo upachaar ko aajamaaen, jisase saradarad men n siraph aaraam milata hai balaki yah jar se khatam bhi hota hai, bina koi saaid iphekata। saradarad ke ghareloo nusakhe (Home Remedies for Headache) sarason tel (Mustard Oil) saradarad men sarason tel kaaphi asaradaar hota hai। maathe ke jis hisase men darad ho raha ho us taraph vaale naak men sarason ke tel ki kuchh boonden daal dijie aur usake baad jor se smson ko upar ki taraph khimchie। isase saradarad se kaaphi raahat milegi। dhayaan rahe saradarad home par bisatar par letakar darad vaale hisase ko bed ke niche lataka kar naak men tel lena chaahie। daalachini (Cinamon) daalachimi ko paani ke saath mahin pisakar maathe par patala lep lagaame se saradarad men kaaphi raahat milati hai। lep sookh jaane par use hata lijie। tina-chaar baar lep lagaane par saradarad hona bnd ho jaata hai। pushakar mool (Pushkar Mool) pushakar mool ek kudarati jari booti hai। ise chmdan ki tarah ghisakar lep bana len aur sir par lagaaen। isake lep ko maathe par lagaane se saradarad mem kaaphi raahat milata hai। mulethi (Mulethi) mulethi saradarad men kaaphi kaam karata hai। mulethi ko pisakar chooran bana lijie। is chooran ko maak ke paas le jaakar soonghem। isase saradarad chhoo-mntar ho jaaegi। saunpha-pipala-mulethi (Saumf, Peepal and Mulethi) pipal ke patate, sontha, mulaithi aur saunph sabako pisakar chooran bana lijie। usake baad is chooran men ek chamamuch paani milaakar gaadha lep bana bana lijie। is lep ko maathe par lagaaie। saradarad khatam ho jaaegaa। masaaledaar chaay (Spicy Tea) masaaledaar chaay saradarad ke lie ek raamabaan ki tarah kaam karata hai। ise ghar men bhi aasaani se banaaya ja sakata hai। yah ek uta‍tejak pey padaarath hai jo dimaag ko sachet karata hai। chaay men thori adarakha, laung aur ilaaichi mila kar ubaal den। ho gaya garamaagaram masaaledaar chaay taiyaara। masaaledaar chaay ko garamaagaram hi pina chaahie। isase aapaka saradarad to gaayab hoga hi saath men aap tarotaaza bhi mahasoos karenge। tel maalish (Oil massage) saradarad mem tel ki maalish bahut asaradaar hoti hai। maalish se sir ki rakat dhamaniyon men rakat paravaah sahi se hone lagata hai aur saradarad turnt chhoo-mntar ho jaati hai। dhayaam rahe sir ki maalish harabal tel se hi karen aur saradarad hone par tel ko halaka garam kar lena chaahie taaki yah jaladi asar kare। ninboo paani (Lemom Water) kaaphi maatara men sharaab pine se akasar logon ko haingaovar ho jaata hai। haingaovar men kaaphi tej saradarad hota hai। aisi sathiti men minboo paami kaaphi kaam karata hai। sharaab jayaada pine se sharir men paani ki kami ho jaati hai aur minboo paani pine se sharir mem paani ki kami bhi door hoti hai aur saradarad bhi thik hota hai। Disease: baronkaaitis (Bronchitis) Description: jab shavaasanali tatha isaki shaakhaaon men snkaraman ya elaraji ke kaaran soojan aame ke kaaran shavaas snbndhi samasaya hoti hai to us sathiti ko baronkaaitis (Bronchitis) kahate hain। yah saradiyon ki ek aam samasaya hai। Symptoms: - khnsi ke saath bahut gaarha v hare rng ka balagam aana - naak bahama ya bnd hona - badan darad hona - baara-baar chhaati men jalan - bukhaar ya thnd lagana - lagaataar kaaphi der hona - sns phoolana - sns lete samay chhaati men gharagharaahat ki aavaaj hona Reasons: - sine men sathit shavns nali aur usaki shaakhaaon men baara-baar home vaala inphekashana। - nayoomoniya bhi baronkaaitis ka mukhay kaaram hoti hai। - ti.bi. ka inphekashan bhi isaka ek paramukh kaaran hota hai। agar shuruaat mem hi ti.bi. inphekashan ka samuchit ilaaj ho jaae to baronkaaitis se bacha ja sakata hai। - kuchh logom men yah rog janamajaat hota hai। - isake alaava aintitaripasin maamak enjaaim ki kami, rayoometaaid auratharaaitis aur anay aatoimayoon bimaariyn bhi baronkaaitis ka kaaran banati hain। - baikatiriya ya vishaanu ka snkaramam bhi baronkaaitis ka kaaram ho sakata hain। - dhoomarapaan aur vaayu paradooshan ke kaaran bhi yah bimaari ho sakati hai। - vaayu men kisi chij se elaraji jaise paraag kan itayaadi bhi baromkaaitis ka kaaran ho sakate hain। Treatments: baronkaaitis se bachaav ke lie sharir ko thmdi se bachaana chaahie। saath hi nimam baaton ka bhi khayaal rakhana chaahie: - dhoomarapaan chhor den। - vaayu paradooshana, v dhool se bachen। - saradi aur phaloo se karen bachaava। - balagam patala rakhane ke lie khoob paani piem। - sote samay sir bisatar se uncha rakhane ke lie takie ka parayog karen। - yadi bukhaar barh jaae aur thmd lagane lage to turnt kisi chikitasak se snparak karen। Home Remedies: baronkaaitis naak aur phephare ke bich sns leme vaali nali men soojan ke vajah se hoti hai। yah paraay vaairal imphekashan se hota hai। gale men khichakhicha, knto jaisi chubhan aur darad hona isake lakashan hain। mausam men badalaav aur elaraji se bhi baromkaaitis ki shikaayat hoti hai। isamen kabhi-kabhi bukhaar ki bhi shikaayat hoti hai। baronkaaitis men kharaash ya darad home se khaana khaane, paani pine ya thook nigalame tak men takaliph hoti hai। isase nijaat paane ke lie daokatar ki madad lene se behatar hai ki kuchh ghareloo ilaaj kie jaane chaahie jo kaaphi asaradaar bhi hota hai। baronkaaitis men kharaash ke ghareloo ilaaja(Home remedies for Bromchitis) shahad (Honey) shahad men enti vaayaral aur enti baikatiriyal gun hota hai। gale men kharaash hone par shahad ya shahad vaali chaay pine se soojan kam hoti hai aur gale ko kaaphi aaraam milati hai। gale men kharaash men yah kaaphi phaayademnd hota hai। adarak (Ginger) saradi, kaph aur gale ki kharaash men adarak gale ko kaaphi aaraam pahumchaata hai। adarak men enti imphalaametari gun hota hai। adarak ka rasa, adarak ki chaay pine ya adarak choosane se gale ki soojana, kharaash men kaaphi aaraam milata hai। harabal chaay (Herbal Tea) kaali miracha, tulasi v laumg se bani chaay pine se gale men kharaash se nijaat milati hai। in kudarati jari-bootiyon se bani garam chaay ki chusakiyon se gale ko kaaphi raahat milati hai। vaise harabal chaay kai bimaariyon mem bhi kaam aata hai। haladi (Turmeric) thori si haladi daalakar doodh men ubaal len। doodh tab tak ubaalen jab tak haladi pak na jaaen. phir ise kap men lekar chaay ki chusakiyn lete hue pien। isase gale ke darad men aur kharaash men kaaphi raahat milegi। garaara (Gargil) gale mem kharaash ki shikaayat hone par garam paani men namak daalakar garaare karen। namak mila garam paani aapake gale mem inphekashan ki vajah se aai soojan ko kam karata hai aur aaraam pahunchaata hai। behatar hoga ki jaladi raahat ke lie aap har tin ghnte mem garaare karen। taral padaarath (Liquid) aap thori-thori der men kuchh garam taral padaarath lete rahen। kuchh bhi nahin to aap thori-thori der men garam paani pite rahen। isase aapake gale ki sikaai hogi aur aapako aaraam milegaa। lahasun (Garlic) lahasun men enti-baayotik aur enti vaayaral gun hote hain। gale ki soojan aur kharaash men yah kaaphi asaradaar hota hai। lahasun ke do-tin tukare ko paani ke saath chaba kar subah khaaen ya phir doodh mem ubaal kar bhi pi sakate hain। yookilipatas tel (Eucalyptus Oil) gale ki kharaash men bhaap lena kaaphi phaayademnd hota hai। garam paani men agar yookilipatas ke tel ko mila kar bhaap len to yah kaaphi asaradaar hota hai। gale ki soojan aur kharaash ko kam karata hai। Disease: ibola vishaanu rog (EVD) (Ebola) Description: ibola vaayaras rog ya ibola hemoraahaijik bukhaar ibola vishaanu ke kaaran hota hai। ibola vishaanu rog (EVD) ya ibola hemoraahaijik bukhaar (EHF) men sharir men nason se khoon baahar aana shuroo ho jaata hai, jisase sharir ke ndar rakatasaraav shuroo ho jaata hai aur isase 90% rogiyon ki maritayu ho jaati hai। Symptoms: - aarnbhik lakashan mem javara, phunasi, sar darada, michali, ulati aur pet men darada, poore sharir men gathiya ka darada, gale mem darada, dasat sakata hai - is rog ka inkayoobeshan piriyad (Incubatiom Period) ek haphate ka hota hai। usake baad rogi mem aarnbhik lakashan najar aate hain - jananng mem soojan hoti hai - tavacha men darad ka anubhav hota hai - netarashaleshamalaashoth (knjengavaaitisa) hai - poore sharir par phunshiyon najar aane lagati hain - munh ka taalu laal ho jaata hai - munha, kaana, naak se rakatasaraav hota hai - rog ke vikasit avasatha men yah lakashan bhi najar aate hai Reasons: ibola se bachaav ka sabase behatar aur ekamaatar upaay hai isase parabhaavit rogi ke samaparak men aane se bachanaa। kisi rogi ke snparak men aame se yah rog aur teji se phailata hai। Treatments: ​ibola ka abhi tak koi thos ilaaj nahin mila hai। bachaav hi is bimaari ka sabase behatarin upaay maana jaata hai। abhi tak ibola se piditon ke kes men niman kadam uthaae jaate hain: - is bimaari ke lie koi vishishat upachaar nahin hai; smkaramit logon ki sahaayata ki koshishon mem unahen oral rihaaidareshan therepi (pine ke lie thoraa-sa mitha aur namakin paani denaa) ya intaraavenas phaludas dena shaamil hai। - akasar is vaayaras ke snkaramit hone vaale 50% se 90% tak log maut ke shikaar ho jaate haim। - isake lie tika vikasit karane ke parayaas jaari hain; haalnki abhi tak aisa koi tika maujood nahin hai। Disease: loo lagana (Heat Stroke) Description: garami men sabase bari samasaya hoti hai loo laganaa। ngareji bhaasha men ise hit satarok (Heat Stroke) aur sanasatarok (Sun Stroke) bhi kahate haim। garami men uchach taapamaan men jayaada der tak rahane se ya garam hava ke jhonkon se snparak mem aane par loo (Loo) lagane ka dar adhik hota hai। Symptoms: - mkhen bhi jalati hain - isase achaanak behoshi v ntath rogi ki maut bhi ho sakati hai - bukhaar kaaphi barh jaata hai - baladapareshar bhi lo ho jaata hai aur livar - kidani mem sodiyam potaishiyam ka sntulan bigar jaata hai। aise mem behoshi bhi a sakati hai। isake alaava lo bipi , baren ya haarat satarok ki sathiti bhi ban sakati hai - loo lagane par sharir men garami , khushaki , siradarad , kamajori , sharir tootana , baar - baar munh sookha.na , ulati , chakakar , tej bukhaar sns lene men takaliph , dasat aur kai baar nidhaal ya behoshi jaise lakashan najar aate hain। loo lagane par pasina nahin aata - sharir ka taapamaan ekadam barh jaata hai। akasar bukhaar bahut jayaada masalan 105 ya 106 digari phaoranahaait tak pahunch jaata hai - haath aur pairon ke taluon men jalana-si hoti rahati hai Reasons: loo lagama ke kaaran (Heat Stroke Causes) loo lagane ke jokhim (Risk Factors of Heat Storkes) loo lagane ke kaaran dimaag aur ntarik ngom ko kashati pahunch sakati hai। vaise to loo ka shikaar akasar pachaas se upar ki umar ke log hote hain lekin kai savasath khilaari bhi isaka shikaar aasaani se ho jaate hain। kam umar ke logon men sentaral naravas sisatam vikasit ho raha hota hai to jayaada umar ke logon men dooshit hota hai, jisake kaaran in donon ko hi loo ka khatara sabase jayaada rahata hai। loo lagane ke dauraan vayakati ko sharir men paani ki kami yaani dihaaidaraishan ki shikaayat bhi hone lagati hai। hit satarok ka turnt ilaaj na karaane par masatishaka, haridaya, gurade aur mnsapeshiyon ko nukasaan pahunch sakata hai। kai sathitiyom men mariz ki maritayu bhi ho sakati hai। garami men vibhinan davaaiyon ka sevan karane vaale vayakatiyon ko bhi loo lagane ka dar hota hai। aisi davaaen jo rakat Description: miragi ek aisa rog hai, jisamen vayakati achaanak jamin par gir kar paraayh aradadh moorachhitaavasatha men rahata hai। rogi ko isaka pooravaabhaas bhi nahin hotaa, ki use miragi gun rakhati hai। baraph parabhaavit kashetar men rakat parisncharan (blood circulation) duroosat karati hai jisase tavacha ke kas jaate hain aur tavacha par maujood gndagi aur tel saaph ho jaata hai। upachaar ke lie rooi ko nimboo ke ras mem bhigokar parabhaavit sathaan par lagaaen ya daalachimi paaudar men ninboo ke ras ki kuchh boonde milaakar raat men parabhaavit sathaan par lagaakar so jaaen। subah gunagune paani se chehara saaph karen। toothapesat (Toothpaste) munhaasom ke ilaaj men toothapesat bhi bahut kaaragaar upaay hai। lekin isake lie saadhaaran toothapesat ka hi isatemaal karana chaahie। jel vaale toothapesat ka isatemaal karane se bachen। baraph se munhaason ko sek kara, parabhaavit sathaan par aadhe ghnte ke lie toothapesat lagaakar chhor den। satim (Steam) satim lene se bhi chehare ke munhaase khatam hote hain। jab chehare par bhaap li jaati hai to rom chhidar khul jaate hain, jisase tavacha khul kar sns leti hai aur is par maujood gndagi aur tel saaph ho jaate hain। (Sulphar) bhi munhaason ko jaladi thik karane ke lie upayogi hai। upachaar ke lie lahasun ki kali ko do tukarom men kaatakar munhason par ragaren aur pnch minat ke lie chhor den। usake baad chehara dho len। beking soda (Baking Soda) beking soda chehare ka atirikat tela, gndagi aur marit tavacha koshikaaon ko hataame men madad karata hai। nimboo ke ras ke saath beking paaudar lekar misharan (Honey) shahad bhi munhaason ko jalad se jalad thik karane ka gun rakhata hai saath hi, yah entibaayotik davaaon ka bhi ek satarot hai, isalie isamen baikatiriya ko maarane ki bhi kashamata hoti hai। (Cucumber) khira mem maujood poteshiyam ke kaaran khira lagaane se tavacha ko thndak milati hai। khira men vitaamin e, i aur si bhi maujood hote hain। upachaar ke khira ko pisakara, use chehare par phes maasak ki tarah lagaaen aur takaribam 15 minat baad chehara dho den। isake alaava papite men shahad milaakar bhi chehare par lagaaya ja sakata hai। daalachini paaudar (Cinnamom Powder) daalachini thik hote hain। daalachini ke saath shahad milaakar bhi chehare par lagaaya ja sakata hai। Disease: gnjaapan (Baldness) Description: purushom men gnjaapan (Baldness) ek aam samasaya hai। daraasal gnjaapan ek parisathiti hai jisamen purushon ke sir par ya to kahin baal mahin hote hain ya phir kam baal hote hain। gnjaapan ko chikitasakiy bhaasha men elipisiya (Alopecia) kahate hain। Symptoms: - enimiya hone par - enaabolik steroids goli khaane se Treatments: gnjaapam ke saamaamay upachaar (General Treatmemts for Baldness) - baalon ke lie dahi kmdishanar ka kaam karata hai। yah baalon ke ki masaaj karem। - arahar ki daal ko pis kar pesat bana len। is pesat ko sir ke parabhaavit kashetar men lagaaen, jalad hi asar dikhame lagegaa। - gnjepan se bachane ke lie arndi ke tel ko sir men laga kar achachhi tarah se masaaj karen। - baalon ka jharana Home Remedies: baalon ke jharane ko rokane ke lie to hama-aap laakhon jatan karate hain, magar gnjaapan ko ntim niyati maan kar koi upaay karama hi chhor dete hain। ham maanate hain ki isaka ek hi upaay hai – heyar taraasapalmt ya phir sarajari। aapako itani jaladi niraash hone ki jarurat nahin hai। heyar taraasapalmt ya phir sarajari men laakhon rupaye kharach karame se behatar hai ki agar aap kuchh ghareloo aur kudarati nusakhom (Herbal and Home Remedies for Baldmess) ko aajamaaemge to snbhav hai regisataan men bhi darakhat ug aaen। aaie jaanate hain un kudarati upaayon ke baare men jisase gnjaapan ko kaaphi had tak kam kiya ja sakata hai। 1. arndi ka tel (Castor Oil) arndi ka tel gnjaapam ko door karane ka sabase kaaragar dava hai। yah ek aadararak yaani maosacharaaijing ejent ki tarah kaam karata hai। yah baal aur tavacha ki kai aur samasayaaon men kaam karata hai। gnjepan ko bhagaane ke lie aapako bas aur kuchh mahin ki daal (Toor Daal) gnjepan ki ilaaj ke lie arahar ki daal bhi besat hai। arahar ki daal ko pis kar pesat bana len। is pesat ko sir ke parabhaavit kashetar men lagaaen, jalad hi asar dikhane lagegaa। 3. ailovera jel (Aloe Ver Gel) ailo vera ek harabal paudha hai aur yah baal aur tavacha ke lie kaaphi hi parabhaavakaari dava hai। ailo vera jel baalom ke garoth men kaaphi kaam karata hai। gnjaapan karane men kaaphi kaam karata hai। baalon ko jharane-girame se bhi rokata hai। baalon men dahi ka maasak lagaaem kaaphi behatar natije aaenge। Disease: dihaaidareshan (Dehydration) Descriptiom: dihaaidareshan yaami nirajalikarana। manushay sharir men paani ke kam ho jaane ki avasatha ko dihaaidareshan (Dehydration) kahate hain। vaijanyaanik bhaasha men dihaaidareshan ko haaipohaaidaraishan (Hypohydration) kahate haim। sharir men paani ki kami (Pami ki Kami) ke kaaran sharir se khanij padaarath jaise ki namak aur shakakar kam ho jaate hain। dihaaidaresham ke dauraana, sharir ki soojan ho jaati hai aur khaana nigalane men dikakat hoti hai। - sharir se pndarah paratishat se jayaada darav khatam hone par insaan ki maritayu bhi ho sakati hai। - dasat ke kaaram sharir men hue dihaaidareshan se manushay ki maritayu ke aasaar jayaada hote haim। gnbhir dihaaidareshan (Pani ki Kami) ki vajah se manushay ka baren daimej yaani usake masatishak ko haani bhi pahunch sakati hai। saath hi haaipovolemik shaok ka khatara bhi rahata hai jisamen sharir ke kai ngom ko haani pahunch sakati hai। - yadi aapako chakakar a rahe haim, ya aap kisi bhi kaaray ko karane men khud ko asamarath pa rahe hain to aise samay mem daokatar ko dikhaana behad aavashayak hota hai। do din se jayaada kabaj ya bukhaar rahane par turnt daokatar se samaparak karen। Treatments: dihaaidareshan ke upaay (Treatment for Dehydration) - jitana ho sake jayaada se jayaada paani pien। - navajaat bachachon mem dihaaidaresham ke upachaar (pani ki kami k ilaj) ke lie bachache ko mn ka doodh v paani rahen। - doodha, kaophi, pharoot joos jaise padaarathon ka sevan karane se bachen। - ilekatarolaaitas se yukat saporatas darinkas ka sevan avashay karen। Home Remedies: aapake sharir ki har koshika thik dhng se kaam kare isake lie aukasijan (Oxygen) ke saath saath paami ki bhi aavashayakata hoti hai। jab sharir men paani ki kami hoti hai to yah sathiti dihaaidareshan ya nirajalikaran kahalaati hai। munh sookha lage, honthon par papari jam jaae, thakaan ho, taoyalet kam jaana ho, chakakar aaen to imahen dihaaidareshan ke paraarnbhik lakashan samajhakara, pey padaarath adhik maatara men lena shuroo kar dena chaahie। dihaaidareshan ki samasaya ko gnbhirata se n lene par isake ghaatak parinaam ho sakate hain। aaie aapako bataate hain ki dihaaidareshan ki samasaya ko ghareloo musakhon se kis tarah thik kiya ja sakata hai। dihaaidareshan ke lie ghareloo nusakhe (Home Remedies for Dehydration) paani pine ki maatara barhaaen (Increase Water Intake) dihaaidareshan se nipatane ka sabase pahala kadam hai ki paani ki maatara badhaaen। poore din men takariban das gilaas paani pina bahut jaroori hai। yadi aapako payaas n bhi lag rahi ho tab bhi paani jaroor pien। saada paani pina achachha m lag bhuna jira daalakar bhi khaaya ja sakata hai। rasile phal aur sabajiym (Watery Fruit and Vagetable) yadi dihaaidareshan ki shurooaat hai to rasile phal aur sabajiyon ke sevan se bhi aaraam snbhav hai। do kele khaae ja sakate hain ya kele ki samoothi banaakar bhi pi ja sakati hai। naariyal paami (Coconut Water) naariyal paani ka ek gilaas dihaaidareshan se nipatame men kaaphi kaaragar hai। naariyal to is paani ko chhaanakar gunaguma rahane tak thnda karen aur isamen shahad milaakar pien। savaad barhaame ke lie minboo ka ras bhi milaaya ja sakata hai। Disease: ghamauriyn (Prickly Heat) Description: ghamauriyon ko mgareji men parikali hit (Prickly Heat) kahate hain। garamiyon ke mausam men ghamauriyn hona aam baat hai। garami ke mausam men sharir se pasina adhik maatara men bahata hai। yadi samay rahate is pasine ko saaf na kiya jaae to yah sharir ki tavacha men hi sookh jaata hai jisake kaaran pasine ki garmthiyn bnd ho jaati hain aur sharir men ghamauri hone lagati hain। Symptoms: - sharir men khujali hona - sharir men jalam ya knte si chubhan mahasoos hona - sharir par laala-gulaabi, chhote daanon ka ubharana - adhik pasina aana - kaparon se chubhan hona - thakaavat mahasoos hona Reasons: ghamauri ke dauraan sharir men khujali, halaki soojam aur chubham mahasoos hone lagati hai। ghamauri ke daane dhoop ke sidhe snparak men aane se barh jaate hain। aamataur par ghamauri kuchh dinon men apane aap sahi ho jaati hai lekin kuchh logon men yah haphaton aur mahinon tak ke lie ho sakati hai। isalie ek haphate tak ghamauri ke thik na hone par daokatar se jaroor paraamarash lena chaahie। ghamauri (Prickly Heat) ke kaaran logon men thakaavat (Heat Exhaustion) aur dhoop men chirachiraahat ki shikaayat bhi hoti hai। ghamauri ke kaaran loo lagama ka khatara bhi paida ho sakata hai। ghamauriym bhi kai parakaar ki hoti hain jaise milieriya karisatalaain (Miliari Crystallina), milieriya roobara (Miliari Rubra) aur milieriya paraophnda (Miliari Profunda)। milieriya paraophunda men sabase adhik khatara rahata hai aur ise vaailadaphaayar (Wildfire Rash) bhi kahate hain। Treatments: ghamauriyon se bachaav ka sabase behatar upaay hota hai garami se bachakar rahamaa। isake alaava ghamauriyon (Ghamoriyan) se bachaav ke kuchh aham upaay niman hain: - sinthetik phaibarik se bane vasataron ko na pahanen। - sooti aur dhile dhaale kapare pahanen। - khoob paani pien aur nahaaen। - baahar se ghar lautane ke kuchh der baad sanaan karen। - sharir ke hisason ko taaza hava lagane den। - masaaledaar bhojan se bachen। saada bhojam hi khaaen। - baarish ke paani se sanaan karane se sharir par nikali phunsiyn aur daanen door hote hain। - rojaana subah nim ki chaara-pnch patatiyn chabaaen। - sharir par mulataani mitati ka lep lagaaen। - nim ki patatiyon ko paani men ubaalakar is paani se sanaam karen। - naariyal ke tel men kapoor milaakar is tel se poore sharir ki maalish karen। - kailaamaain loshan ka parayog karen। - gile sharir par paaudar na lagaaen। jaroorat se jayaada paaudar ka parayog karane se bhi bachen। Home Remedies: garamiyon mem ghamauriyon ki samasaya aam hai। jayaada pasina aane ya garami men rahane par baron, bachachom, yahn tak ki navajaaton (Infants) men bhi ghamauri ki samasaya ho jaati hai। ghamauri hone par chhote-chhote chubhane vaale daanem pitha, garadan tatha sharir ke anay hisason par nikal aate hain। kai baar baikatiriyal inphekasham (Bacterial Infection) aur sharir ka vajan jayaada hone se bhi ghamauri nikalame ki samasaya hoti rahati hai। yoon to mausam men badalaav hote hi ghamauri ki samasaya khud b khud thik ho jaati hai lekin kai dapha samasaya itami barh jaati hai ki mausam men badalaav hone tak ka samay kaatana bhi mushakil hota hai। aise men kuchh ghareloo upachaaron se ghamauriyon se nijaat snbhav hai। ghamauriyon se raahat ke lie ghareloo nusakhe (Home Remedies for Prickley Heat) otamil (Oatmeal) ghamauriyon se nijaat ke lie otamil bahut barhiya nusakha hai। otamil se ghamauriyon men hone vaali jalan (inflammation), chubhan aur khujali (itching) se raahat milati hai। upachaar ke lie thnde paani se bhare hue tab men ek kap otamil daalen। jab tak paani doodhiya rng ho tab tak intajaar karen aur is paani men takariban aadha ghnta baithen। is upaay ko har roj do baar karen। thnda upachaar (Cold Compress) ghamauri parabhaavit sathaan par thndi sikaai karane se bhi turnt aaraam milata hai। baraph ke kuchh tukaron ko kapare men lapetakar parabhaavit sathaan par sikaai karen। lagaataar takariban 10 minat tak aisa karen। har chaar se chhah ghnte par aisa karen। khujali tatha jalan se bhi raahat milati hai। Disease: sakaravi (Scurvy) Description: yah rog bhojam men vitaamin si (Vitamin C) jise esakorabik esid (Ascorbic acid) bhi kaha jaata hai, ki kami se snpooran vitaamin mil saken। -dhoomarapaan ko chhorama Home Remedies: sakaravi rog vitaamin si se jura hua hai। vitaamin si (esakorabik esid or Ascorbic Acid) ki kami hone par sakaravi rog hota hai। (Details of Premature Ejaculation in Hindi) achachhe yaunn snbndhon ke lie jaroori hai ki donon hi paaratanar sntushat ho paaen aur charam ko paraapat karen, lekin shighar patan (Sighr Patam) ki samasaya ke chalate purush samay se pahale hi sakhalit ho jaata hai aur mahila saathi ko yaun sntushati nahim mil paati। medikal saains ki bhaasha men kaha jaae to, intarakoras aaramabh hone ke 60 seknd ke ndar hi agar puroosh ka viraya-sakhalit ho jaae to ise shigharapatan (Premature Ejaculation) kaha jaata hai। Reasons: shigharapatan ya parimecha‍yor ijaikuleshan shigharapatan ke kaaram (Causes of Premature Ejaculation) shigharapatan ke kai kaaran jaise- galat tarike se hasatamaithuna, tanaav ya chintaa, masatishakiy rasaayanon ka asuntalan ya kharaab khaana-paan v jivanashaili aadi khushahaal banaaya ja sakata hai। shigharapatan ke kai anay kaaran ho sakate hain jaise - barhati umar tatha parosa‍tet ki samasa‍ya aadi। saath hi dara, asurakashaa, chhupakar sekasa, shaaririk v maanasik pareshaani bhi is samasaya ka ek kaaram ho sakati hai। isake kaaranon ki sahi jaanakaari homa jaroori hota hai। shigharapatan ke jokhim (Risks of Premature Ejaculation) shigharapatan ka rogi sa‍vabhaav men chirachira ho jaata hai, use siradarad v tanaav jaisi shaa‍ririk samasa‍yaaen bhi ho sakati haim। kai baar dekha jaata hai ki shigharapatan se garasit vayakati ki kuchh samay ke baad sekas men aroochi bhi hone lagati hai v shaaririk durabalata bhi ho sakati hai। shigharapatan ka ilaaj samay par n kie jaane athava isaka thik parakaar se ilaaj m kie jaane par rog gnbhir roop le sakata hai। shigharapatan (Premature Ejaculation ) ke kisi bhi satar par purush apani sakhalan kariya ko niyntarit nahin kar paate hain, jis kaaran ve apane utathaan ko bamaane mem asaphal (Erectile Dysfunction) rahate hain aur us vakat viray ko sakhalit hone se rok nahim paate jab virayapaat nahim karana chaahie। Treatments: shigharapatan ya parimecha‍yor ijaikuleshan ke upaay (Remedies of Premature Ejaculation in Hindi) shigharapatan ke kaarana, parakaar v satar ke aadhaar par isaka upachaar bhi alaga-alag ho sakata hai। yog v ekasarasaaija, kuchh vitaamin v jari-bootiyon, aadi ki madad se is samasaya ko door kiya ja sakata hai। snsarag ke bicha-bich men uraja deme vaale tarala, jaise galookoja, joosa, doodha, aadi ka sevan karane se bhi aaraam milata hai । shigharapatan ka desi upachaar (Home Remedies of Premature Ejaculation) kai log maanate hain ki shigharapatan (Premature Ejaculation​) ke desi upachaar ke taur par kaunch ke bija, saphed moosali aur ashavagndha ke Goiter im Hindi) 1. namaka- khaame men hamesha aayodin vaala namak khaame se ghengha rog mem bahut laabh milata hai। 2. karajani- goonja ya karajani ki jar aur bij se nikaala hua tel lagaame se aur gale ke anadar gharashan karane se ghengha rog shnt hota hai। 4. pipala- pipal aur thoohar ka lep karane se medaj ghengha (motaape ki vajah se gale ki gnthe) thik ho jaati haim। 5. devadaaroo- devadaaroo aur inadaraayan ko ek saath pisakar lep karane se kaphaj ghengha thik ho jaati hai। 6. arndi- arndi ki jar ko pisakar chaaval ke paani men milaakar subaha-shaam lep karame se ghengha rog thik ho jaata hai। 7. samudaraphala- samudaraphala, sahajan ke bij aur dashamool ki saari aushadhiyon ko sil par pisakar halakaa-halaka garam lep karane se vaataj galagnd yaani ghengha (gais ki vajah se gale ki gnthe) rog thik ho jaata hai। 8. amalataasa- amalataas ki jar ko baarik pisakar paani men milaakar galagmd (ghenghaa) tatha gmdamaala (gale ki gnthe) par lep karane se donon rog thik ho jaate hain। 9. lauki- lauki ke pake hue phal men paami bharakar ek sapataah tak rakhe rahane den। usake baad pine se ghengha rog samaapat ho jaata hai। 10. laal arndi- laal arndi ki jar ko pisakar chaavalon ke paani men milaakar lep karane se ghengha rog thik ho jaata hai। 11. soorajamukhi- soorajamukhi ki jar aur lahasun donon ko pisakara, tikiya banaakar gale par bndhane se ghengha phoot jaata hai aur bahakar saaph ho jaata hai magar isase darad bahut hota hai। Disease: motaapa (Obesity) Description: sharir ke ndar asaamaanay roop se jama vasa hi obesiti (Obesity) hai। saamaanayataur aapako dubala nahin kar sakataa, isalie smyam rakhen aur bataae gae nusakhom ko apanaaen। isase aap do se tin mahinon men hi apana vajan kam kar sakate hain। motaapa ya vajan kam karane ke ghareloo nusakhe (Home Remedies for Obesity) shahad aur adarak ka ras (Honey and Ginger Juice) shahad aur adarak ko milaakar khaane se vajan teji se kam hota hai। shahad men pharakatoj ki uchach maatara hoti hai jahn atirikat vasa ko jalaane ka kaam karati hai vahin adarak bhi sharir ki vasa ko pighalaane ka kaam karata hai aur paraakaritik bhookh lagane ki kariya ko banaae rakhata hai। upachaar ke lie do misharan subah khaali pet aur raat ko sone se pahale pien। ek mahine se pahale hi aap khud ko halaka mahasoos karane lagenge। ninboo, shahad aur kaali mirach (Lemon, Honey and Black Pepper) ninboo, chamamach shahada, ek chhoti chamamach kaali mirach aur chaar bari chamamach ninboo ka ras milaaen। har roj subaha-subah is tarah ke paani ko pine se jalad hi vajan kam hone lagegaa। ber ki patati (Indiam Plum Leaves) ber ki patatiyon men vasa ko kaatane ki shakati hoti hai। upachaar ke lie ber ki patatiyon ko raatabhar paani men bhigaakar subah subah chabaakar khaaen। aisa karane se ek mahine khujali se nijaat ke ghareloo nusakhe (Home remedies for Itching) 1. naariyal ka tel (Coconut oil)- tavacha ke shushak hone ya kisi kire ke kaatane se, khujali kisi bhi kaaran se ho, naariyal ka tel behad phaayademnd hota hai। naariyal ke tel ko khujali vaale sathaan par lagaakar halake haath se maalish karem। itana hi nahin naariyal tel ko poore sharir par bhi lagaaya ja sakata hai। 2. petaroliyam jaili (Petroleum jelly)- yadi tavacha behad snvedanashil (semsitive skin) hai to khujali se mijaat ke lie petaroliyam jaili behad achachha upaay hai। isamen koi bhi rasaayan nahin hota aur tavacha par behad parabhaavi bhi hoti hai। isake isatemaal se n keval khujali balaki tavacha ki anay samasayaaen bhi hal ho jaati hain। 3. ninboo (Lemon)- nimboo mem vitaamim si (vitamin c) uchach maatara men paaya jaata hai। khujali se nijaat ke lie ninboo behad achachhe upaayon men se ek hai। ninboo men maujood volaataail (volatile) tavacha ki soojan aur jalan ko door karate hain। parabhaavit tavacha par ninboo ke ras ko rooi ki sahaayata se lagaaya ja sakata hai। 4. beking soda (Baking soda)- tim hisase beking soda men ek hisasa paani milaakar ek pesat bamaayen। is pesat ko parabhaavit sathaam par lagaane se khujali ki samasaya se raahat milati hai। lekin tavacha kati-phati ho to beking soda lagaane se bachana chaahie। 5. tulasi (Basil)- tulasi men thaayamaola, yoojinaol aur kainphar uchach maatara men hote hain jo khujali aur jalan se raahat dete hain। tulasi ki kuchh patatiyon ko achachhi parakaar dhokara, parabhaavit sathaan par ragarame se khujali aur jalan se raahat milati hai। 6. seb ka siraka (Apple cider vinegar)- seb ke sirake ka isatemaal roosi se mijaat ke lie kiya jaata hai, usi parakaar khujali men bhi yah laabhadaayak hai। seb ke siraka mem entisepatik aur entiphngal gum hote hain jo ki tavacha snbndhi samasayaaon se nijaat dilaate hain। seb ke siraka men rooi ko bhigaakar parabhaavit sathaan par lagaame se khujali ki samasaya se raahat milati hai। 7. elovera (Aloevera)- elovara maoishacharaaijar se bharapoor hota hai jisase rookhi tavacha se hone vaali khujali men yah asarakaari hai। elovera jel parabhaavit tavacha par lagaane se khujali, jalan aur soojan door hoti hai। tavacha par elovera lagaane ke lie isaki ek patati ko chaakoo se bich se chir kar usake mdar se jaili ko baahar nikaalen aur sharir par halake haathom se masaaj karen। 8. mim (Neem)- nim ki patatiyon ko paani men daalakar ubaalen। isake baad is paani ko gumaguna rahane par nahaayen। mim men paraakaritik taur par emtisepatik gun hote hain jo khujali ko door karate hain। isake alaava yadi rakat men kisi parakaar ki ashudadhi ke kaaran khujali hoti hai to subah subah nim ke chhote ya kachache patate chabaayen। mibauri chabaane se bhi rakat saaph hokar khujali door hoti hai। Disease: gale men darad (Throat Ache) Description: gale men darad (Throat ache) saamaamay saradi ka snket bhi ho sakata hai aur vokal korad men inphekashan ya satarep tharot (strep throat) jaisi balagam mem khoon a raha ho to ise najarndaaj nahin karana chaahie। Disease: javaaint pena- jorom men darad (Joint Paim) Descriptiom: javaaint pena- joron men darad Symptoms: - joron ko morane men doodh se hadadiyon ko kailashayim aur vitaamin di milata hai jisase hadadiyn majaboot banati hain। yadi doodh pasnd n ho to doodh se bane anay khaaday padaarath jaise panira, dahi aadi bhi khaae ja raahat ke lie achachha vayaayaam hoti hai। Home Remedies: joron ka darad (Joint Pain) sharir ke kisi bhi bhaag mem ho sakata hai, ghutane, kndhe ya kamara। kai baar gathiya jorom ke darad ka kaaran (Stress) Description: kisi baat se pareshaana, aahat ya dukhi hokara, vayakati ka man se gahan udaas hona hi tamaav hai। tanaav man se snbndhit hai। tanaav (Stress) ek tarah ka davnd hai jo sntulam saath sochata rahata hai। saamaanay baahari kaaran (Common External Reasons) - jivan men koi bara nakaaraatamak badalaav - sakool ya kaolej men kisi bhi tarah ka koi dabaav - rishaton men daraar - sahaayak hai। Disease: esiditi ya amalapitat (Acidity) Description: esiditi (Acidity) Symptoms: - kabhi-kabhi chhaati men darad ho sakata hai। - khatati dakaaren aanaa, - khaana ya khatata paani (esida) munh men a jaanaa, - chhaati men jalan hona - pet men gais banana - matali aur ulati Reasons: kaaran (Cause of Acidity) ham jo bhi khaate hain, usaka paachan (Digestion) behad jaroori hota hai। bhojan ke paachan ke lie aamaashay men kai tarah ke paachan rasaayanon ka sataraav hota hai jaise ki haaidarokalorik esid (Hydrochloric acid) aur pepasin (Pepsin)। saamaanay roop se yah donon lie methi ke daanon ko paani ke saath milaakar pesat bana len। is pesat ko ek gilaas chhaachh men milaakar pien। isase pet ka darad bhi thik hoga aur gais se bhi raahat milegi। saath hi, esiditi bhi khatam hogi। savaad barhaame aur behatar parinaam ke lie is chhaachh men kaala namak aur kaali mirach bhi milaai ja sakati hai। seb ka siraka (Apple Cider Vinegar) seb ka siraka bhi esiditi ko thik karane ka aasaan tarika hai। upachaar ke lie ek kap paani men do chamamach kachacha seb ka siraka milaakar din mem do baar pien। khaana khaane se pahale bhi ise piya ja sakata hai। laung (Cloves)
