men rakhakar chabaaen। saunph ke saath mishari bhi milaai ja sakati hai। aisa karane se esiditi se raahat milati hai। Disease: elaraji (Allergy) Description: elaraji (Allergy) kisi bhi chij ke parati atisnvedanashil hona hi elaraji hai, jise savaasathay ki bhaasha mem etopi (atopy) bhi kahate hain। elaraji kisi se bhi ho sakati hai, mausam men badalaav se, kisi khaane ki chij se, paalatu jaanavar se, dhool se, dhuen se, saumdaray parasaadhanon se ya davaaon aadi se। elaraji men sharir ka imayoon sisatam kuchh khaas chijon ko savikaar nahin kar paataa। in chijon ke parati imayooniti ayogay tarah se paratikariya deti hai। imayooniti davaara di jaane vaali paratikariya hi elaraji hoti hai। yoon dekha jaae to adhikatar elaraji khataranaak nahin hoti lekin kabhi kabhi samasaya gnbhir ho jaati hai। elaraji ko roka ja sakata hai, lekin isake lie elaraji paida karane vaale kaaramon se poori tarah door rahana hogaa। yoon to elaraji phailane vaali bimaari nahin hai phir bhi yadi kisi ko naak bahane aur nkhom se paani aane vaali elaraji ho to usase snparak bamaakar rakhane men hi behatari hai। snbhav ho to usake davaara isatemaal kie gae saamaan ko bhi isatemaal n karen। Symptoms: - nkh men khujali homa aur nkh ka laal ho jaana - nkh se paani aana - egajima aur garamiyon men bukhaar - gale men khujali homa - tavacha par khujali hona - tavacha par pitat uthana - tavacha par laal chakatate aur daane hona - naak ke ndar baara- baar daane nikalana - naak men baara-baar khujali hona - maak se paani aana Reasons: elaraji ke kaarana- (cause of allergy) 1. dhool (Dust) dhool ke kan bahut chhote jiv hote hain jo hamaare- aas paas ki jayaadaatar vasatuon par rahate hain। yah kan uchach aadarata men panapate haim jo marit tavachaa, baikatiriya aur phngas aadi se apana khaana paraapat karate hain। 2. kit (Insect) kiton se elaraji vaale logon ko kiton ke kaatame se dnk lagane se tavacha ekadam laal hokar phool jaati hai। itana hi nahin unahen ulati, chakakar aana aur bukhaar bhi ho sakata hai। 3. khaana (Food) kuchh logon ko rojamarara mem khaayi jaane vaali chijon se bhi elaraji hoti hai, jaise moongaphali, doodh aur nda aadi। khaaday padaarath se elaraji vaale logon ko khaane ke baad ji michalaane, sharir men khujali hone ya daame mikalane ki samasaya ho sakati hai। 4. rabar (Latex) rabar se bana koi bhi utapaada, elaraji ka kaaran ho sakata hai। kuchh logon ko rabar se bane utapaad bhi nukasaan pahunchaate hain, jaise dasataane, kndoma, medikal upakaran aadi ke isatemaal se jalana, maak bahanaa, chhinkamaa, sns ki ghabaraahat aur khujali ki samasayaaen ho sakati hain। 5. khushaboo (Fragramce) achachhi khushaboo bhale achachhi lagati ho lekim yah bhi kuchh logon ki elaraji ka kaaran ho sakati hai। paraphayooma, khushaboo vaali momabatatiyn, kai tarah ke bayooti paraodakat aadi ki khushaboo se sir darada, ji michalaane aur naak ki elaraji ho sakati hai। 6. jaanavar (Pets) paalatu jaanavar bhi kai logon ki elaraji ka kaaran hote hain। jaanavaron ke baala, unake munh se nikalane vaali laara, roosi aadi se kai gnbhir pareshaamiyn ho sakati hain। 7. ghaas (Grass) kai baar ghaasa, per aur phool bhi elaraji ka kaaran hote hain। yah sab mausami elaraji ka kaaran hote hain, jinase khujali, nkhon men jalama, lagaataar chhimk aana aur khujali aadi ki samasaya ho sakati hai। Treatments: elaraji se nijaat paane ke lie upaay (Tips to Prevent Allergy) - dhoola, dhuna aur gndagi se bachakar rahen। - kuchh davaaon jaise esapirima, nimusalaaid aadi ke sevan men saavadhaami baraten। - khatati chijon, jaise achaar aadi ka isatemaal kam karen। - aise khaaday padaarath jinahen khaane se elaraji hai, unahen n khaaem। - gndagi se elaraji vaale logon ko samaya-samay par chaadara, takiye ke kavar aur parade aadi badalate rahane chaahie। Home Remedies: dhool (Dust), gndagi (Dirt), mausam men parivaratan (Climate change), silana, aadi kuchh aise kaaran hain jinase vayakati ko elaraji (Allergy) ho sakati hai। parayaavaran men maujood chijon ke lie alaga-alag snvedanashilata hoti hai jisake chalate hamaara sharir paratikariya karata hai। aise men vijaatiy padaarathon ki sharir men asavikaarata elaraji hai। kuchh logon ko khaane ki chijon se elaraji ho sakati hai। adhik chhinken aanaa, sns lete samay aavaaj honaa, sharir men kisi tarah ki soojana, khujali, chakakar aanaa, ji ghabaraanaa, pet men maror hona aadi elaraji ke kuchh lakashan hain। aaie aapako bataate hain elaraji se bachane ke kuchh ghareloo upaae (Home remedies of Allergy): 1.shahad (Honey)- shahad sharir ki rog paratirodhak kashamata ko barhaata hai। rojaama do chamamach shahad ka isatemaal sharir ko kaaphi laabh pahunchaata hai। ek gilaas gunagune paani men shahad mila kar pine se ya doodh men shahad mila kar pime se kaaphi laabh pahunchata hai। 2. seb (Apple)- rojaana ek seb khaane se imayoon sisatam (immune system) behatar hota hai aur aap elaraji se door rahate hain। seb ka joos bhi piya ja sakata hai। 3.haladi (Turmeric)- elaraji se bachaane men haladi bhi kaaphi parabhaavashaali hai। haladi men taakatavar enti aukasidemt paae jaate hain jo elaraji se larane men madad karate hain। ek gilaas garam doodh men ek chamamach haladi milaakar pine se kaaphi laabh pahunchata hai। 4. lahasoon (Garlic)- lahasoom bhi ek enti elaraji khaaday padaarath hai jise apani daait men shaamil karana aavashayak hai। yah ek enti baoyotika, enti aukasident aur imayooniti barhaame vaala khaaday padaarath hai। lahasoon ko sabaji men daalakar ya subah khaali pet ek do kali paani ke saath nigalane se kaaphi phaayada hota hai। 5.ninboo (Lemon)- nimboo men uchach maatara men vitaamin si aur enti aukasident paaya jaata hai। ninboo imayoon sisatam barhaata hai aur elaraji se door rakhane mem kaaphi phaayademmd saabit hota hai। 6. adarak (Ginger)- adarak ke sevan se sns ki bimaari mem aaraam milata hai। aise mem yah asathama se snbndhit elaraji men kaaphi aaraam pahunchaata hai। rojaana adarak ka sevan karame se elaraji se raahat paai ja sakati hai। daokatar ki salaah par adarak ke sapaliment bhi lie ja sakate hain। 7. garin ti (Green tea)- garin ti men maujood entiaukasidentas sharir ki rog paratirodhak kashamata ko barhaate hain। isamem maujood thiyaanin bhi elaraji se bachaane men madad karata hai। yadi kisi ko garin ti pasnd n ho to balaik ti bhi pi ja sakati hai। 8. baadaam (Almond)- baadaam men vitaamin bi, i, maiganishiyama, jinka, seleniyam (selenium) tatha anay savaasathayavaradhak vasa paai jaati hai। jis kaaran yah tamaav se to raahat dete hi hain saath hi elaraji se bachaane men bhi madad karate hain। rog paratirodhak kashamata ko tej kar sharir aur dimaag ko majabooti dete hain। baadaam ko bhoon kar ya kachacha bhi khaaya ja sakata hai। yadi aise khaana snbhav n ho to baadaam ka paaudar banaakara, doodh ke saath khaaya ja sakata hai। Disease: motiyaabinda- keterekat (Cataract) Description: keterekat ya motiyaabind (Cataract) motiyaabind nkh ke lens men ubhara saphed rng ka dhababa hai, jo ki nkh ki darishati ko parabhaavit karata hai। motiyaabind hone se vayakati ko koi bhi vasatu dhundhali najar aati hai। motiyaabind jayaadaatar bujuragon ko hota hai। motiyaabind keval ek nkh ya donon nkhon men bhi ho sakata hai, yahn tak ki yah ek nkh se doosari nkh men bhi phail sakata hai। Symptoms: - nkhon ke lens par saphed parat ka jamama - ek mkh se do chijen najar aana - kai dapha halaki roshani bhi bahut tej paratit hona - kisi bhi vasatu ka rng halaka najar aana - koi bhi vasatu dhundhali najar aana - chashame ka nnbar baara-baar badalana - tej roshani se pareshaani hona - raat ki laait men chhalale numa aakariti najar aana - raat ko gaari chalaane men dikakat hona - shaam hote hi nkhon ki roshani aur bhi kamajor hona Reasons: nkh ke ndar ka lens kaimare ki tarah kaam karata hai। yahi retina par laait ko phokas karata hai jisase chijen saaph najar aati hain। lens paani aur parotin se milakar banata hai। parotin is tarah se lens ke saath juri rahati hai ki yah lens ko saaph rakhati hai jisase ki roshani aara-paar ja sake। umar barhame ke saath kai baar kuchh parotin ek jagah ikatathi ho jaati hai aur lens ke ek hisase par jama ho jaati hai। aise men motiyaabind mkh ke lems men atayadhik parotim ke banane ke kaaran hota hai jo lens ko dhundhala bana deta hai। yah lens ke jarie roshani ko poori tarah jaane nahin deta jisase nkh se saaph dikhaai nahin detaa। aise men sabhi nae lens selasa, lens ke baahar ki or jama ho jaate haim jabaki sabhi puraane lens selasa, lens ke bichon bich ek jagah ikatatha ho jaate hain, jise motiyaabind ya keterekat kahate hain। motiyaabind hone ke anay kaaran (other reason & causes of cataract) - nkhon men kisi tarah ka anay rog honaa, jaisa galookoma aadi - janamajaat nkh mem motiyaabimd hona - daayabitij hona - sharir men kisi pareshaani, jaise asathama ke lie sateraoid lena - achaanak se tej roshani ke snparak men aane se ya lagaataar tej roshani men rahane se - dhoomarapaan ya sharaab aadi ka jayaada sevan karane se Treatments: motiyaabimd ke upaay (tips to prevent cataract) - dhoop ya tej roshani se khud ko bachaaen, nkhon par chashama aur sir par topi paham ke rahen - kisi bhi tarah ka koi nasha n karem - paushatik khaana khaaen - samaya-samay par mkhom ki jnch karavaaen - tanaav se door rahen - daayabitij niyntaran men rakhen Home Remedies: jab nkhon ki baat ho to samasaya ko gnbhirata se lena chaahie, kayomki yadi nkhon ki roshani ek baar chali gai to dobaara mahin paai ja sakati। motiyaabind (Cataract) bhi aisi hi gnbhir samasaya hai, jisamen nkhon ke lens par ek dhababa (spot on the eye lens) a jaata hai। jisase aap jo bhi chij dekhate hain vah aapako dhundhali najar aati hai aur vahn aapako dhababa jaisa najar aata hai। yoon to motiyaabimd ko sarajari ke davaara hataaya ja sakata hai lekim kuchh ghareloo nusakhon ki madad se bhi motiyaabind ka ilaaj snbhav hai। yadi shurooaat men sachet hokar yah apamaae jaaen to snbhav hai aapako sarajari ya auparesham m karavaana pare। motiyaabind ke lie ghareloo nusakhe (Home Remedies for Cataract) lahasun (Garlic) lahasun ke asnkhay savaasathay laabh hain aur yah nkhon ke lie bhi samaan roop se laabhakaari hai। lahasum ki do se tim kaliyn (2 to 3 clove) rojaama khaane se nkhon se ekadam saaph dikhaai dene lagega aur kuchh hi dinon men dhababe ki shikaayat door ho jaaegi। paalak (Spinach) paalak khaane se motiyaabind kaaphi had tak thik ho jaata hai। paalak men bita kairotin (Bet Carotene) or entiaukasident (Antioxidents) gun hote hain। paalak ko rojaana khaane se nkhon ka motiyaabimd kuchh din men hi khatam ho jaata hai aur mkhen pahale jaisi ho jaati hain। doodh aur baadaam (Milk and Almond) motiyaabind se pareshaan logon ki nkhen jayaadaatar laal rahati hain aur samasaya se nipatana aur bhi mushakil hota hai। aise men doodh aur baadaam nkhon ko laabh dete hain। upachaar ke lie baadaam ko raat bhar doodh men bhigaakar chhor den। is doodh ko subah chhaanakar isaki boonde mkhon men daalen aur baadaam ko chaba kar kha len। garin ti (Green Tea) garin ti se nkhon ki roshami tej ho sakati hai। garim ti saamaanay nkhom ki samasaya men bhi laabhakaari hai। rojaana tin se chaar baar garin ti pine nkhon ko savaasathay laabh hota hai। garin ti men maujood entiaukasident (Antioxidemt) nkhom ko nai taajagi dete hain। kachacha papita (Raw Papaya) kachache papite men papen (Papain) maam ka enjaaim hota hai jo ki parotin (Protiem) ke paacham men sahaayak hota hai। motiyaabind se pareshaan logon ko parotin ko pachaame men dikakat aati hai, aise men kachacha papita motiyaabind se garasit logon ko laabh deta hai। kachacha papita rojaana isatemaal karane se nkhon ke lens nae jaise chamakame lagate hain। vitaamim si (Vitamin C) motiyaabind ke ilaaj men vitaamin si mahatavapooran bhoomika nibhaata hai। vitaamin si ke sevan se motiyaabind snrachamaaon ko roka ja sakata hai। aahaar men aise khaaday padaarathon ko isatemaal karen, jinamen vitaamin si jayaada se jayaada ho। isake alaava vitaamin si sapaliment (Vitamin C Suppliment) ke roop men bhi liya ja sakata hai। kachachi sabajiyn (Raw Vegetables) kachachi sabajiyn nkhon ke lie chamatakaar ka kaam kar sakati hai। kachachi sabajiyon men poshak tatav aur vitaamin e (Vitamin A) ki uchach maatara hoti hai jo ki nkhon ke savaasathay ke lie jaroori hai। apane dainik aahaar men kachachi sabajiyom ko isatemaal karane se motiyaabind ke saath hi nkhon ki anay saamaanay samasayaaon se bhi nipata ja sakata hai। kachachi sabajiyom ko salaad ke roop men jitana snbhav ho khaaen। jaamum (Bilberrys) jaamun se motiyaabind poori tarah nahin hatata lekin darishati ki asapashatata ko jaamun khaane se thik kiya ja sakata hai। jaamun men enthosaayanosaaidas (Anthocyanosides) tatha phalevamaaidas (Flavonoids) kaaphi adhik hote hain jo ki retima (Retima) aur nkhon ke lains (Eye Lens) ki rakasha karate hain। Disease: saradi aur kaph (Cough And Cold) Description: saradi aur kaph (Cough and Cold) naak bah rahi hai, ya bnd hai jisase ki sns leme men takaliph ho rahi hai, gale men darad mahasoos ho raha hai ya gale men chubhan aur chhila (scratchy throat) jaise mahasoos ho raha hai aur khnsi ke saath balagam (muscus) pareshaan kar raha hai to samajh lijie aap saradi- jukaam aur kaph se pareshaan hain। Symptoms: - nkhon se khoob paani aana aur jalan hona - aavaaj bhaari hona - khaane men savaad aur khushaboo mahasoos n hona - gala chhila hua ya darad mahasoos homa - chhink aana - naak ka bnd homa - naak se khoob paani girana - naak se gale ki or balagam ka girana - mnsapeshiyon men darad ya khinchaav hona - sir bhaari mahasoos hona ya halaka darad hona Reasons: kaarana- (Cause of Cough and Cold) saradi hinovaayaras (rhinovirus) se phailati hai jo ki 10 se 40 paratishat tak saradi ko sharir men paravesh karaata hai। vahin koronaavaayaras (coronavirus) lagabhag 20 paratishat saradi ke lie jimamedaar hota hai। inake alaava resapiretari sinsitaayal vaayaras (respiratory syncytial virus) aur pairaainphalooenja vaayaras (parainfluenz virus) 10 phisadi tak saradi ke lie jimamedaar hote hain। saradi, smkaraman se bhi phailati hai। ek snkaramit vayakati ya usake davaara isatemaal kie gae saamaan ke snparak men aane se doosare ko bhi saradi ki samasaya ho sakati hai। yah vaayaras sharir ke ndar pahunchakar vayakati ki rog kashamata ko parabhaavit karate hain aur kaaphi maatara men balagam banaana shuroo kar dete hain, jisase gala aur naak poori tarah parabhaavit ho jaate hain। itana hi nahim snkaramit vayakati ke chhimkane (sneezing), usase haath milaame se bhi saradi ke baikatiriya doosare vayakati ko parabhaavit kar sakate hain। saradi aur kaph ke lie kai anay kaaran (Other causes of Cough and Cold) - kamare men silan ya ghutan ho - tej dhoop se aane ke baad turnt thnda paani pina - sharir ki paratirodhak kashamata kamajor hona - bahut tej paraphayoom ya tel ka isatemaal - auphis ya ghar ke baahar bina haath saaph kie khaanaa-pina Treatments: saradi se raahat ke lie tipas (Tips to prevemt cough and cold) - aaraam karem, khoob pey padaarath len aur savaasathayavaradhak khaama khaaen। - yadi bukhaar ya sharir men darad ho to pairaasitaamaol li ja sakati hai। - naak par baam ya baajaar men maujood sapare ka isatemaal kiya ja sakata hai। isase bnd naak khulegi aur raahat milegi। - garam paani men namak daal kar garaare karate rahen। - khaane-pine se pahale apane haath achachhi tarah dhoen। - snkaramik vayakati ke snparak men n aaem, jaise ki haath milaane ki jagah namasate ki ja sakati hai। - yadi aap khud snkaramit hain to bhir vaali jagahon par jaane se bachen aur apani chijen jaise roomaal aadi doosarom se door rakhen। - thndi aur baahar ki chijen khaane se parahej karen। Home Remedies: mausam men parivaratana, sarada-garam hone ya paradoosham aur elaraji (Allergy) ya snkaraman (Infection) ke kaaran saradi-khnsi ki samasaya ho jaati hai। kai baar snkaraman bhi isaka kaaran hota hai। aaie jaanate hain, saradi khnsi se bachaav ke ghareloo nusakhe (Home Remedies for Cough and Cold): 1. haladi (Turmeric)- aadha kap garam paani ko ubaal len phir usamen ek chamamach kaali mirach paaudar (black pepper powder), ek chamamach haladi paaudar aur ek chamamach shahad milaaen। ab is misharan ko do se tin minat tak ubaal len aur niyamit taur par kaarhe ki tarah pien। 2. adarak (Ginger)- adarak ko ghisakar ya chhote-chhote tukaron men kaatakar ek kap paani men daalakar ubaal len। din bhar men tin se chaar baar is ghol ko pien। shahad aur ninboo ko adarak ke ras men milaakar pine se bhi kaph ki shikaayat door hoti hai। 3. ninboo (Lemon)- ek chamamach shahad men do chamamach ninboo ka ras milaakar garam kar len। din bhar mem kai baar is ghol ko dava ki tarah lete rahem। 4. lahasun (Garlic)- laung ke tel aur shahad men lahasun ki do se tin kali ko pis kar mila len। din bhar mem kai baar thori thori maatara men isaka sevam karate rahen। 5. payaaj (Onion)- ek chamamach shahad mem aadha chamamach payaaj ka ras len aur isako milaakar din bhar men kam se kam do baar avashay sevan karen। kaph aur gale ki kharaash se raahat milegi। 6. garam taral padaarath pien (Drink warm liquids)- garam paani pien ye gale ki soojan (throat sweeling) ke lie phaayademnd hai। aap chaahen to koi amay garam padaarath bhi pi sakate hain। 7. shahad (Honey)- shahad gale ko aaraam pahunchaane ke lie ek paarnparik upaay hai। ek gilaas garam paani mem shahad aur ninboo ka ras milaakar din men tin baar pime se khnsi se raahat milati hai। 8. seb ka siraka (Apple cider vinegar)- seb ka siraka har tarah ki khnsi ke lie achachha hai। 2 bara chamamach siraka 10 tola paani men milaakar garam karen। isamen ek chamamach shahad daalakar pien। khnsi men raahat paane ka kaaragar upaay hai। 9. tulasi ke patate aur shahad (Honey and basil leaves)- dhule hue tulasi ke kuchh pataton ko koot kar usaka ras nikaalem aur usame shahad milaaen। ab ise chamamach men garam karake din men 3-4 baar lem, is ghareloo upaay se khnsi men jaladi aaraam milata hai। Disease: titanas (Tetanus) Descriptiom: titanas (Tetanus) manushayon ke ghaav (Wound) men snkaraman hone se titanas hota hai jisaka kaaran kalosataridiyam titaami baikatiriya (Clostridium Tetani Bacteria) hai। yahi jivaanu ghaav ya chot mem vish paida karata hai jisase titanas ho jaata hai। dhire-dhire yahi jahar poore sharir men phailane lagata hai jisase sathiti ghaatak ho jaati hai। titanas ke kaaran kai baar vayakati ki maritayu bhi ho sakati hai। titanas men sharir ki mnsapeshiyon men ainthan mahasoos hoti hai aur rook rook kar darad hota hai। haalnki kisi chot ke lagane ke baad yadi turnt titanas ka tika lagavaaya jaae to isase hone vaali pareshaamiyon se bacha ja sakata hai। Symptoms: - uchach rakatachaap - garadan mem ainthan hona - chirachiraapan - chehare ki mnsapeshiyon ka jakar jaana - jabare ka bnd ho jaana - nigalane men dikakat hona - pasina khoob aama - mnsapeshiyon men ainthan aur akaran mahasoos hona - sns lene men takaliph hona - hariday gati ka tej homa Reasons: titanas ka kaaram (Cause of Tetanus) kalosataridiyam titaani (Clostridium Tetami)chhar ke aakar ka jivaanu hai jo duniya bhar men mitati men paaya jaata hai। kalosataridiyam titaani titanas rog ke lie jimamedaar jivaanu hai। yah baikatiriya do roopon men paaya jaata hai, pahala doramnt ya nishakariy roop men doosara sakariy roop men jo jivaanuon ki smkhaya ko aur bhi barha deta hai। kisi bhi tarah ki chot men titanas ho sakati hai। - ghaav se - sarajari men - parasav ke dauraan - koi phora home par - sui ya injekashan se nasha karane vaalon ko - kisi puraane jng lage lohe se chot lagane se Treatments: titanas se bachane ke lie tipas (Tips to Prevent Tetanus) - koi bhi aisa ghaav jisase tavacha phat gai ho, use turmt paani aur saabun se saaph kiya jaana chaahie। - ghaav ko kabhi khula n chhoren। khule ghaav ke snkaraman ka khatara jayaada hota hai। - yadi ghaav se khoon bah raha ho to to us par sooti aur sookha kapara bndhen। - rakat ko rokane ke lie ghaav ke upar dabaav daalen, jisase rakat bahana rook jaae। - ghaayal vayakati ko turmt titanas ka tika lagavaana chaahie। titanas ke anay upachaar (Treatment of Tetanus) - ghaav ko garam paani se dhoen aur koi emtisepatik karim ya paaudar lagaaen। - taarapim ke tel se sharir ki maalish karen, isamen paira, jabare aur garadan par halake haath se dabaav daalate hue maalish karen। - ghaav ke upar tel ko garam karake usamem haladi milaakar lagaaen - momabatati ke mom ko pighalaakar bhi ghaav par lagaaya ja sakata hai - kate sathaan par nim ka tel lagaane se bhi titanas ka dar nahin rahata Disease: moch (Sprains) Description: moch (Sprains) sharir ke jor ke ligaament (ligamemt) ya sanaayu jab kisi chot ke kaaran jaroorat se jayaada khinch jaate hain to is avasatha ko moch (Sprains or Moch) kaha jaata hai। jayaada khinchaav ke kaaran peshiyon ke phaaibar phat jaate hain aur ligaament men ghaav ho jaata hai। ligaament ek hadadi ko doosari hadadi se jorane (connect) ka kaaray karate hain। Symptoms: - chot vaali jagah par asahaniy darad - chot vaali jagah par sunanapan hona - parabhaavit sathaan ko morane ya chalaane men pareshaani hona - parabhaavit sathaan par nila ya kaala dhababa aana - parabhaavit sathaan par soojan aana - bina sahaare ke chalane phirane men dikakat hona Reasons: moch ke kaarana- (Causes of Sprains) moch sharir ke alaga-alag hisason men alaga-alag kaaranon se a sakati hai। moch saamaanay ya karonik bhi ho sakati hai। 1. enkal mem moch (Ankle Sprains)- unchi-nichi jagah par chalane ya daurane se enkal men moch a sakati hai। kai baar haai hil pahanane se pair achaanak se murata hai, yah bhi pair men moch ka kaaran ho sakata hai। 2. ghutane men moch (Knee Sprains)- bhaagate- bhaagate achaanak gir jaane ya koi bhaari vasatu uthaakar chalane se ghutanon men moch a sakati hai। kai baar chalate chalate achaanak ghutana mur jaata hai। yah bhi ghutane men moch ka kaaran ho sakata hai। 3. kalaai men moch (Wrist Sprains)- girane ke dauraan haath ke murane, kisi ke davaara haath ko galat tarike se khinchane, khel ke dauraan aadi sathitiyon men kalaai men moch a sakati hai। 4. kamar men moch (Waist Sprains)- kai baar sirhiyn charhane utarane men dikakat hone yaa, kisi unchi jagah se kamar ke bal girane se ya jaroorat se jayaada bhaari chij ko jhukakar uthaane se kamar men moch a sakati hai। 5. ngoothe men moch (Thumb Sprains)- kai tarah ke khel khelane ya kahin ngootha dab jaane ke kaaran chot lagane se ngoothe men moch a sakati hai। 6. garadan men moch (Neck Sprains)- achaanak se garadan men jhataka lagane, jayaada uncha takiya lagaane, kisi parakaar se garadan men chot lagane ki sathiti mem garadan men moch a sakati hai। anay kaaran (other causes & reason of sprains) - kai baar vayaayaam karane se pahale vaaramaap n hona aur achaanak se kathin vayaayaam shuroo kar dena bhi moch aane ka kaaram ho sakata hai। - pair men paraopar phutaviyar n hone se bhi pair ke murane ya chot lagane ka khatara barh jaata hai jisase moch ki snbhaavana rahati hai। Treatmemts: moch se nijaat ke lie upaay (Treatment of Sprain Pain) - moch se nijaat ke lie parabhaavit sathaan par chane bndh den। in chamom ko baara- baar bhigaate rahen। jaise jaise chane phoolenge, moch thik hoti jaaegi। - moch vaale sathaan par ernd ke pataton ko halaka sa senk kar us par sarason ka tel lagaakara, parabhaavit sathaam par bndh den। - til ke tel mem aphim milaakar moch vaale sathaan par bndh den। - moch vaale sathaan par haladi, choona aur shahad ko milaakar lagaane se chot thik ho jaati hai। - moch se nijaat ke lie tejapatata aur laumg ko pisakar lep lagaaen। - sarason ke tel men ajavaayan aur lahasun ko garam karake, is tel se moch vaale sathaan ki maalish karen। - paan ke patate par sarason ka tel lagaakar use halaka garam karen aur moch vaale sathaan par bndhen । - tulasi patatom ke ras men sarason ka tel milaakar parabhaavit sathaam par lagaaen। turnt aaraam milegaa। - akharot ke tel se maalish karane par bhi chot mem aaraam milata hai। - mamak ko garam karake, kisi mote kapare mem bndhakara, chot vaale sathaan par bndh den। aaraam milegaa। - namak aur haladi ko milaakar chot vaale sathaan par lagaane se bhi aaraam milegaa। - paan ke patate ya aam ke patate par tel lagaakara, us par namak lagaaen aur garam karake chot vaale sathaan par bndh den। aisa karane se bhi moch thik ho jaaegi। - moch aur soojam men elovera lagaane se bhi aaraam milata hai। Home Remedies: umchi eri ke joote-chapapal pahanane, pair umche niche parane, vayaayaam bahut jayaada ya galat tarah se karane, bahut jayaada chalane, galat tarah se uthane baithane aadi aise kuchh kaaran hain, jinase sharir men moch (sprain) ki sathiti ban jaati hai। kai dapha darad asahaniy bhi ho sakata hai aur parabhaavit jagah par laal ya nila nishaan aur soojan bhi a sakati hai। yadi khinchaav ki pareshaani ho to pairom ko thanad se bachaayen aur aise kapare ka chumaav karen jo thanad ke dinon men aapake pairon ko hava n lagane den। aaie jaanen moch se raahat ke ghareloo upaay (Home remedies for sprain): 1. garam aur thnda senk (Hot amd cold compress)- sharir ke darad vaale hisase par karam se garam aur thnde paami ka sek karen, ye tanaavagarasat mmsapeshiyon ko aaraam pahunchaaegaa। ise kai tarike se kar sakate hain jaise ki tauliye ko garam paami men dubaayen aur tanaavagarasat mnsapeshi par laga sakate hain। tanaavagarasat mnsapeshi men aaraam ke lie gunagune paani se nahaaya ja sakata hai ya bhaap le sakate hain। baraph lagaakar bhi aaraam pa sakate hain। 2. mnsapeshi ko khinchana (Stretch your muscle)- din paratidin ki saamaanay shaaririk parakariya ke liye jaane se pahale, mnsapeshiyon ko khinchana mahatavapooran hota hai। isake lie halaki halaki satareching karen। agar aapako raat men sote samay pairon men khinchaav hota hai, to achachha hoga ki aap mnsapeshiyon ko khinchane ka abhayaas karen। 3. taral padaarath lete rahen (Take enough liquid)- taral padaarath ke saath paani ko niyamit ntaraal par lekar sharir men nami banaayen rakhen। 8 gilaas paani pine ke saath aapako phalon ka joos bhi pina chaahiye। parayaapat maatara men taral lena aapake mmsapeshiyon men kam maror paida karega aur aaraam degaa। 4. kela (Banana)- kele men parayaapat maatara mem potaishiyam hota hai। yah sharir ke liye behad achachha hota hai। agar maashate ya bhojan ke baad paratidin ek kela khaate hain to yah mnsapeshiyom ko maror se door rakhega aur khimchaav se raahat degaa। 5. garam paid se sikaai (Hot pad)- ek samay aisa tha jab log garam paani ko paid par daalakar phir isatemaal karate the aur sharir par lagaakar sabhi parakaar ke darad se door rahate the। lekim ab baazaar men bijali se chalane vaale garam paid maujood hain। in paid se sikaai karane se mnsapeshiyon ka khinchaav door hota hai aur darad se raahat milati hai। 6. maalish (Massage)- parabhaavit hisase ki maalish karana bhi behad raahat deta hai। kisi bhi tel ko thora gumaguna karake, usamen lahasun ki kuchh kaliyn daalen। kuchh der is tel ko aur garam karen aur gunaguna rahane par parabhaavit hisase ki halake haathon se maalish karen। kuchh hi der men pairom men khinchaav kam hoga aur darad men bhi aaraam milegaa। Disease: niman rakatachaap ya lo baladapareshar (Low Blood Pressure) Description: niman rakatachaap ya lo baladapareshar (Low Blood Pressure) lo baladapareshar ya niman rakatachaapa, aukasijan (oxygen) ko dimaag tak jaame se rokata hai। keval aukasijan hi nahi balaki anay poshak tatav bhi dimaag tak nahin pahunch paate। baladapareshar ko savaasathay ki bhaasha men haaipotemshan (hypotension) ke naam se jaanate hain। yoom to lo baladapareshar koi bimaari nahin hoti lekin yah sharir men panap rahi anay gmbhir bimaari ka snket hoti hai। aise men jab kisi ke sharir men rakata-paravaah saamaanay se kam ho jaata hai to use miman rakatachaap ya lo balad pareshar kahate hai। naaramal balad pareshar 120/80 hota hai। aise men dila, kidani, phephare aur dimaag nshik roop se ya poori tarah se kaam karana bhi bnd kar sakate hain। Symptoms: - nkhon ke aage ndhera chhaana - ulati aur daayariya - garadan ka akar jaana - chakakar aana - chhaati mem darada, sms phoolana - haathon aur pairon ka thnda hona - hariday men misad bitas mahasoos ki jaati hai Reasons: balad pareshar kam hone ke kaaran (causes of low blood pressure) 1. dil ki bimaari (heart disease)- baladapareshar kam homa dil ki gnbhir bimaari se jura hota hai, dil ki bimaari se haarat ki mnsapeshiyn kamajor ho jaati hain, jisase haarat parayaapat khoon ko pamap nahin kar paata aur hamaara bipi lo rahane lagata hai। dil ke marijon aur enimiya ke rogi lo bipi ko lekar saavadhaan rahen। 2. aarathosatetik haaiparatenshan taaip (arthostetic hypertension type)- isamem marij ko khare hone par chakakar aate hain, kayonki usaka balad pareshar ekadam se 20 paoint niche a jaata hai। yah naravas sisatam par aadhaarit hota hai। lekin kai baar davaaon ke saaid iphekat se ya elaraji se bhi ho sakati hai। 3. khoon ki kami tatha anay ka (less blood and other reasom)- sharir ke ndarooni ngon se khoon bah jaane ya khoon ki kami se, khaane men paushatikata ki kami ya aniyamitata se, phepharon ke ataik se, haarat ka vaolav kharaab ho jaane se, lo bipi ho sakata hai। achaanak sadama lagane, koi bhayaavah darishay dekhane ya khabar sunane se bhi lo bipi ho sakata hai। isake alaava (other reason & causes of low blood pressure) - garabhaavasathaa, haaramon asntulan jaise ki thaayaraoid ki sakariyata kam ho jaana - balad shugar davaaon ke parabhaav se - satarok tatha livar smbndhi bimaariyn - kuchh aavashayak vitaamin jaise bi12 aur aayaran ki kami Treatments: baladapareshar lo hai to kaya karen (some tips to prevemt low blood pressure) - turnt baith ya let jaaen, mutathiyn bhimchen, bndhen, kholem, pair hilaayen। - mamak aur chini vaala paani ya chaay pien। pairon ke niche do takie lagaakar leten। - jo log pahale se haai bipi ki dava kha rahe haim, ve dava khaana bnd kar dem। - kam se kam aath gilaas paani aur anay pey roj pien। - bhojan men kaarabohaaidaret ki maatara kam kar den। - in sab ke alaava turanat daokatari salaah len। Home Remedies: - miman rakatachaap se pirit log namak jayaada khaaen - lagaataar chakakar a rahe hon, to paani jayaada pien - ek kap shakaraknd ka joos din men do baar pien - mitati ke baratan men raatabhar kishamish bhigaakar rakhem। subah kishamish chabaakar khaaen aur paani pi lem - subah khaali pet tulasi ke patate ke ras men shahad milaakar khaaen - raat men baadaam bhigaakar rakhen, subah in baadaam ke chhilake utaarakar pis len aur doodh ke saath ubaalen। is doodh ko gunaguna pien। Disease: saphed baala- gare heyar (Grey Hair) Description: saphed baala- gare heyar (Grey hair) umar ke saath baalon ka saphed hona paraakaritik hai lekin kai baar kam umar men hi baal saphed hone lagate hain। aisa kai baar haaramonal garabari, badalati laaiphasataail aur paradooshan vaale maahaul ke kaaran bhi ho sakata hai। maujooda samay men tinej men hi bachachon ke baal saphed hone lagate haim। Symptoms: - umar se pahale baal saphed ho jaana - baal naajuk hona - baal patale ho jaana - baalon ka tekasachar kharaab hona Reasons: kaarana- (Cause of Grey Hair) melaamin ke aadhaar par hi baalom ka rng kaalaa, saphed ya bhoora hota hai। jinake baalon men melaamim ki kami hoti hai umake baalon ka rng halaka hota hai jinake baalom men melaanin jayaada hota hai unake baal kaale hote hain। jin logon ke baal saphed ho jaate hain unake baalom men melaanin khatam ho jaata hai। melaanin pigament baalon ke phaolikal men rahata hai। kuchh maamalon men thaoiraaida, animiya ya aanuvnshik kaaranom se bhi baal saphed ho sakate hain। baal safed hone ke anay kaaran (Other Reasons & Causes of Gray Hair) - vitaamin bi, aayaran aur kaopar tatha aayodin jaise tatavon ki kami se baal saphed hote hain। jin logon ke khaane men in minaral ki kami hoti hai unake baal samay se pahale saphed hone lagate hain। - aise vayakati jo bahut jayaada gusasail hote hain ya bahut jaladi tanaav men aate unake baal bhi jaladi saphed hone lagate hain। - kuchh vayakatiyon men umar se pahale baalon ka saphed homa aanuvnshik hota hai। - bahut lnbe samay tak kisi bimaari se pirit rahame ya jaladi jaladi bimaar parane vaale logon ke baal bhi umar se pahale saphed hone lagate hain। - baalon ki dekhabhaal thik parakaar se n ki jaae ya baalon ki saphaai ka dhayaan n rakha jaae to bhi baal umar se pahale saphed hone lagate hain। - bahut jayaada rasaayan vaale shainpoo ya baalon ke utapaad jaise ki heyar kalar ya jel aadi isatemaal karane vaale logon ke baal bhi jaladi saphed hone lagate hain। - bahut jayaada paradooshan vaale maahaul ya dhoop men rahane se bhi baalom ka rng urane lagata hai। Treatments: baalon ko kaala karane ke lie upachaar (Tips & Remedies to prevent gray hair) - kachache papite ka pesat sir par takariban 10 minat lagaakar rakhen। aisa karane se kuchh hi dinon mem baalon ka jharana rookega saath hi baal kaale bhi honge। itana hi nahin baalon se dendaraph bhi khatam hogaa। - baal dhone ke lie kemikal shainpoo ka isatemaal bnd karen, isaki jagah besan aur doodh ya dahi ka isatemaal karen। aisa karane se baalon ka paraakaritik rng bana rahegaa। - baal dhone ke lie nvala paaudar aur minboo ka isatemaal karen। shikaakaai aur ritha milaakar ghar par hi shainpoo bhi banaaya ja sakata hai। - sir men laal payaaj ko pisakar usaka ras lagaaen। aisa karane se bhi saphed baal kaale hone lagate hain saath hi baalom ka jharama bhi bnd ho jaata hai। - dahi mem kaali mirach aur ninboo ka ras milaakar sir ki tavacha aur baalon par lagaaen। takariban aadhe ghnte baad baal dho den, aisa karane se baal kaale hone lagenge। - desi ghi bhi saphed baalon ko kaala karane ka saral upaay hai। tel ki jagah desi ghi se baalon ki masaaj karem। - nvale ka parayog khaane men bhi karen। nvala khaame se bhi baal kaale hote hain। Home Remedies: aajakal umar se pahale hi baalon ka pakana ya saphed hona aam samasaya banati ja rahi hai। baalon ki thik se dekhabhaal n ho paane aur paradooshan ke kaarana, hamaare baal asamay hi saphed ho jaate hain। baalon ko kalar karana is samasaya ka koi upachaar nahin hai lekin kuchh ghareloo upachaar aajamaakar aap apane baalon ko saphed hone se rok sakate hain। jaanie saphed baalon ko kaala karane ke ghareloo nusakhe (Home Remedies for Grey Hair) 1. payaaj ka ras (Onion juice)- kuchh dinon taka, nahaane se 1/2 ghnta pahale rojaama sir men payaaj ka pesat lagaaen। isase baal kaale hone lagenge। 2. kachacha papita (Raw papaya)- sapataah mem kam se kam 3 din das minat tak kachache papite ka pesat sir men lagaaen। isase baal nahin jharenge aur kaale bhi hone lagenge। 3. naariyal tel (Coconut oil)- bharingaraaj aur ashavagndha ki jaren baalon ke lie varadaan maani jaati hain। inaka pesat naariyal ke tel ke saath baalon ki jaron mem lagaaen aur 1 ghnte baad gunagune paani se achachhi tarah se baal dho len। isase bhi baal kaale hote hain। 4. ninboo ka ras (Lemon jiuce)- ninboo ke ras men nvala paaudar milaakar use sir par lagaane se bhi saphed baal kaale ho jaate hain। 5. desi ghi (Desi ghee)- paratidim shudadh ghi se sir ki maalish karane se bhi saphed baal kaale hote hain। 6. adarak (Ginger)- adarak ko kadadookas kar shahad mem mila len। ise baalon par kam se kam sapataah mem do baar niyamit roop se lagaaen। baalon ka safed hona kam ho jaaegaa। 7. jaitoon ka tel (Olive oil)- jaitoon ke tel ko halaka garam karen। isamen 4 garaam kapoor milaakar is tel se maalish karen। isaki maalish se kuchh hi samay men roosi khatam ho jaaegi aur baal bhi kaale rahenge। 8. mvala (Aamla)- nvale ke paaudar men ninboo ka ras milaakar use niyamit roop se lagaaen। shainpoo ke baad nvala paaudar paani men gholakar lagaane se bhi baalon ki kndishaning hoti hai, aur baal bhi kaale hote hain। nvala kisi na kisi rup me sevan bhi avashay karate rahen। 9. til ka tel (Sesame oil)- saradiyon men til adhik se adhik khaaen। til ka tel bhi baalon ko kaala karane mem madad karata hai। 10. kaali mirach (Black pepper)- aadha kap dahi men chutaki bhar kaali mirach aur chamamach bhar ninboo ras milaakar baalon mem lagaae। 15 minat baad baal dho len। saphed baal phir se kaale home lagenge। 11. menhadi (Henna)- lohe ki karaahi men ek katori mehndi paaudara, do bare chamamach chaay ka paani, do chamamach nvala paaudara, ek chamamach ninboo ka rasa, do chamamach dahi, shikaakaai v ritha paaudara, ek mda (agar aap lena chaahen to), aadha chamamach naariyal tel v thoraa-sa katatha daalakar raat ko bhigo den। ise subah baalom men lagaaen, phir do ghnte baad dho len। isase baal bina kisi nukasaan ke kaale ho jaaemge। aisa maah men kam se kam ek baar avashay karen। Disease: hadadi pharaikachar ya hadadi ka khisakana (Bone Fracture Or Dislocation) Description: hadadi pharaikachar ya hadadi ka khisakana (Bone fracture or dislocation) pharaikachar (Fracture)- hadadi ka tootana hi hadadi ka pharaikachar kahalaata hai। hadadi kai kaaramon se toot sakati hai, kahin girame se, takakar lagane se, jhataka lagane se ya achaanak se dabaav parane para। hadadi ka khisakana (Dislocation of bone) - do hadadiyn jab jure hue sathaan se khisak jaati hain to ise disalokeshan ya hadadi ka khisakana kahate haim। do hadadiyn ek jor par jaakar milati hain, lekin is jor par chot lagane ke kaaran isi jor se hadadiyn khisak jaati hain। hadadiyon ke khisakane par bhi bahut darad hota hai aur snbndhit sathaam par soojan a jaati hai। Symptoms: - asahaniy tarah se darad hona - aasa-paas ki tntarikaaon men kashati ke kaaran akaran - pharaikachar ki jagah par soojan a jaana - pharaikachar ke aasa-paas ke utakon men asathirata - pharaikachar vaale sathaan ka poori tarah se kaam bnd kar dena - behosh hona Reasons: kaarana- (Causes of bone frtacture or dislocation) pharaikachar ke kai kaaran ho sakate hain। hadadiyon ke kamajor hone ya hadadiyon se snbndhit kaimsara, sisata, ausatiyoporosis aadi home se। pharaikachar ke baad hadadi men darad ke bhi kai kaaran ho sakate hain- - hadadiyon ke aasa-paas ke narav edingasa, jo hadadi ke tootame par sakariy hokar dimaag ko darad ka snket dete hain। - hadadiyn tootane se rakatasataraav ka hona aur soojan aanaa, jisase darad hota hai। - pharaikachar hone par mnsapeshiyn sikur kar hadadi ko bachaane ki koshish karati hain, yah bhi darad ka kaaran hota hai। - aisi koi duraghatana hone par jisase hadadiyn parabhaavit hon। - hadadiyon ka pharaikachar vayakati ki umar par bhi nirabhar karata hai kayonki jayaada umar men pharaikachar ke chmses barh jaate hain। kuchh sathitiyon men asahaniy darad bhi ho sakata hai jaise- - snkaramam hone par - galat tarike se palaasatar lagaane para, bahut dhila ya bahut taait Treatments: upachaara- (Tips to prevent bone fracture or dislocation) - pharaikachar vaali jagah ki baraph se sikaai karen। soojan kam hogi aur darad se aaraam milegaa। - pirit vayakati ko poori tarah aaraam karana chaahie। snbhav ho to snbndhit jagah ko hilaane-dulaane se bachen। - garam sikaai karane se bhi aaraam milata hai। - yadi haath ya pair ki hadadi tooti ho to use umchaai par karake rakhen। - pharaikachar vaale sathaan ke aasa-paas ki jagah par maalish karen। - aadha anaanaas roj khaaem। - red mit khaane se bachen। - parijaravetiv khaana n khaaen। saavadhaamiyn- (Precautions) - kaar men baithakar hamesha sit belat pahanen। - koi khel khelate samay ya saaikil aur motarasaaikil chalaate samaya, snbndhit sephati upakaran jaroor pahanen। - yadi kisi ko ausatiporosis hai, to niyamit vayaayaam karen aur hadadiyon ko majaboot karane vaali daait len। Disease: chikan paokasa- chechak (Chickenpox) Description: chikan paokasa- chechak (Chickenpox) chechak ek vaayaral snkaraman (viral infectiom) hai jisase sharir par chhaale ki tarah daane banate hain aur unamen khujali (itching) hoti hai। chechak aise logom ko jayaada hota hai jo bimaar n parate hon ya jinahonne chechak se bachane ke lie tikaakaran n karavaaya ho। pahale ke samay men yuva hone tak har koi chechak rog se ek n ek baar jaroor parabhaavit hota tha lekin aaj ke samay men is tarah ke rogon men kami aai hai। jayaadaatar logom ke lie, chechak ek halaki bimaari hai। phir bhi, yah tika lagaaya jaana behatar hai। chechak ke tike chechak aur usaki snbhaavit jatilataaon ko rokane ke lie ek surakashit aur parabhaavi tarika hai। Symptoms: - thakaam (kamajori) mahasoos hona - bukhaara, siradarad - bhookh men kami - sharir par laala-gulaabi, chhote daanom ka ubharana Reasons: kin logon ko hota hai adhik khataraa? (Risk Factors of Chicken Pox) chechak atayadhik snkaramit hoti hai, aur yah teji se phail sakati hai। vaayaras ke daane ke saath sidhe smparak men aane se ya khnsane ya chhinkane se hava men baikatiriya phailane se doosaron ko ho sakati hai। chechak (chechak) ka khatara tab aur adhik hota hai jaba: - kisi ko kabhi chechak n hui ho। - chechak ke lie tikaakaran n karavaaya ho। - bachache jo sakool ya haosatal men snkaraman se parabhaavit hue hon। Treatments: upachaar (Treatments of Chicken Pox) - ek chamamach beking soda (baking soda) ko ek gilaas paani men gholakara, is paani ko rooi ki sahaayata se sharir par lagaaen। chechak se nijaat milegi। - chechak ke dauraan home vaali khujali se bachane ke lie otamil (oatmeal) ko paani men daalakar nahaaen। - chechak (chechak) se hone vaali khujali se bachane ke lie kailaamaain losham (calamine lotion) ko daanon ke upar lagaaen। - din men do se tin baar parabhaavit sathaan par shahad lagaaem। - chechak ko jaladi thik karane ke lie gaajar aur hare dhaniya ka soop banaakar pien। - chndan ke tel men rooi bhigaakara, parabhaavit sathaan par lagaaen। - hari matar ko ubaalakar usaka pesat bamaakara, daanon par lagaaen, aaraam milegaa। - elovera ka taaja ras nikaalakar daanon par lagaaen। tipas (Tips for Chicken Pox) - yadi chechak ke saath bukhaar bhi hai to khoob pey padaarath pien। paani, joos aur soop samay samay par lete rahen। yadi bachacha snkaramit mn ka doodh pita ho, to mn ko doodh nahin pilaana chaahie। - daanon ko n khujalaaen aur haathom ke maakhoon chhote rakhen। raat men sote samay khujalaane se bachame ke lie haathon par galavas (gloves) pahanen। - khujali se bachane ke lie sharir ko thnda rakhen। halake kapare pahanen aur garam paani se nahaane se bachen। - is baat ka bhi dhayaam rakhen ki smkaramam ghar ke doosaron sadasayon tak n phaile। snkaramit vayakati ke kapare, bisatar aadi door rakhen aur unahen ghar ke anay sadasayon ke kaparon se alag hi dhoen। Home Remedies: sharir men teji se khujali honaa, laal daane nikal aana chikan paokas ya chechak (Chicken pox) ke paramukh lakashan hain। 1 varash se lekar 10 varash tak ke bachachon men chikan paokas ka khatara jayaada hota hai। khaana-paan men hui aniyamitata chikan paokas ke phailane ka paramukh kaaran hoti hai। is dauraan naakhoom se chakataton ko hataane ki koshish nahin karami chaahie, aisa karane se yah phailata hai। chechak (Chechak) ke samay khaana-paan ka uchit dhayaan rakhana chaahie। masaaledaar aur auyali khaama khaane se bachen। chikanapaokas ke kisi marij ko kabhi esaparin nahin deni chaahie। isase usaki haalat kharaab ho sakati hai। chikan paokas hone par baahar aur bhir vaali jagah par jaame se parahej karen। ho sake to is dauraan logon se door rahen। jaanie chikan paokas se bachaav ke ghareloo nusakhe (Home Remedies for Chicken pox) niman upachaaron ko apanaakar is bimaari se raahat paai ja sakati hai: 1. jai ka aata (Oat Flour)- chikan paokas hone par sharir men bahut tej khujali hoti hai। khujali se bachane ke lie jai ke aate ko paani men milaakar sanaan karana chaahie। 2 litar paani men 2 kap jai ka aata milaakar lagabhag 15 minat tak ubaalen, pake aate ko ek kaotan ke baig men achachhi tarah se bndhakar baoth tab men daalakar nahaaen। 2. bhoora siraka (Brown Vinegar)- aadha kap bhoore sirake ko paani men daalakar nahaane se sharir men ho rahi khujali se nijaat paayi ja sakati hai। isase daanom ki soojan kam hoti hai aur daane sookhane bhi lagate hain। 3. ninboo ka ras (Lemon Juice)- ninboo ka ras pine se chikan paokas men raahat milati hai। upachaar ke lie samay samay par ek gilaas saaph paani men ninboo nichorakar pite rahen। 4. mim ki patatiyn (Margos Leaves)- nim ki patatiyon ko garam paani mem daalakar nahaane se khujali samaapat hoti hai। nim paraakaritik roop se enti baikatiriyal gunon se bharapoor hota hai। aise men chikan paokas thik karame men behad phaayademnd hai। 5. beking soda (Baking Soda)- aadha chamamach bekimg soda ko ek gilaas gunagune paani men milaaen aur is lep ko poore sharir par lagaakar sookhane dem। isase chikanapaokas jalad thik ho jaata hai। 6. seb ka siraka (Apple Cider Vinegar)- aadha kap seb ke sirake ko halake garam paani men milaakar nahaane se raahat milati hai। is paani men takariban 20 minat tak jaroor baithen। 7. vitaamin i tel (Vitamin E Oil)- vitaamina-i yukat tel ko sharir par lagaane se chikan paokas ke dauraam hone vaali khujali se raahat milati hai। 8. gaajar (Carrot)- ubale gaajar aur dhamiya khaane se chikam paokas se aai kamajori kam hoti hai। gaajar aur dhaniya ka soop banaakar pine se raahat milati hai। 9. harabal chaay (Herbal Tea)- tulasi, genda aur kaimomaail ko milaakar chaay banaaie phir usamen shahad ya ninboo milaakar pijie। is chaay ko din mem 3-4 baar pine se raahat milati hai। 10. hari matar (Green Pea)- hari matar ko paami men pakaakar isake paani ko sharir men lagaaie, isase chikan paokas ke laal chakatate samaapat hote hain। 11. adarak (Ginger)- baath tab men thnda paami len aur usamem adarak daalakar tis mimat tak chhor den। usake baad is paani men baith jaaem। isase chikanapaokas ke dauraan hone vaali khujali men aaraam milata hai। Disease: haija (Cholera) Description: haija (Cholera) haija ek snkaraamak bimaari (imfectious disease) hai, jo mton ko parabhaavit karati hai aur jisamen paani ki tarah patale dasat lag jaate hain। haija ka ilaaj samay rahate n kiya jaae to vayakati men paani ki kami (dehydratiom) ho jaati hai, jisase vayakati ki maut bhi ho sakati hai। haija dooshit paani pine ya dooshit khaana khaame ke kaaran phailata hai। aisa paani ya khaana jisamen vaaibariyo koleri baikatiriya (vibrio cholerae becteria) maujood ho, haija ka kaaran banata hai। haija (Haija) aisi jagah par jayaada phailata hai jahn, saaph saphaai ka abhaav ho, sivarayukat paani ki sapalaai ho, saaga-sabaji sivar ke paani mem ugaai ja rahi hon ya kisi ka ghar naale aadi ke paas sathit ho। haijaa, bachachon se lekar bujuragon taka, kisi men bhi ho sakata hai। garabhavati mahilaaon tatha bachachon men bhi is rog ke hone ki aashmka jayaada rahati hai kayonki unaki paratirodhak kashamata kam hoti hai। haija men vayakati ke sharir se paani ke saath kai jaroori lavana, sodiyam aur poteshiyam aadi bhi nikal jaate hain, jisase vayakati ke sharir ka rakat amaliy ho jaata hai aur vayakati ki maritayu ho jaati hai। Symptoms: - dasat ekadam patale aur chaaval ke paami jaise hona - dasat ke saath ulatiyn hona - parabhaavit vayakati ko atayadhik payaas lagana - parabhaavit vayakati ko peshaab kam aana - sharir ki mns peshiyon mem ainthan hona Reasoms: haija ka kaaran (Causes of Choler in Hindi) 1- dooshit paani, bhojana, phal ya doodh aadi ka parayog karane se। 2- rogi vayakati ke snparak men rahane se, masalana, usake saath khaane, uthane-baithane, usake davaara isatemaal kie gae kapare pahanane, usake davaara isatemaal kie gae kisi bhi saamaan ko isatemaal karane se। 3- makakhiym bhi haija (Haija) phailane ka bara kaaran hain। khule men ki gai shauch ya gndagi par baithakar makakhiyn baikatiriya lekar doosari jagahon par phaila deti hain, jisase haija phailata hai। 4- khaane ko bina dhake rakhanaa, aur use khaanaa। 5- paani ko bina dhake rakhanaa। 6- kachacha ya adhapaka bhojana, khaasakar mns khaanaa। Treatments: upachaar (Treatment of Cholera) haija ka ilaaj karane se pahale rogi ko saapha-saphaai ka vishesh dhayaan rakhama haahie। haija akasar saapha-saphaai ki kami ke kaaran bhi phailata hai। haija hone par niman upaay apanaane chaahie: - dooshit bhojana, paani ya kisi anay khaaday padaarath ka isatemaal n karen - baasi bhojan n karen - paratayek khaaday padaarath aur paani ko hamesha dhak kar rakhen - sharir men paani ki kami n hone den। - bimaari ho rahi ho to mimboo ki shiknji, dahi, chhaachha, paani tatha oaaraes aadi pite rahen - yadi vayakati ke dasat aur ulati n rook rahe hon, to use turnt asapataal le jaaem - paratayek vayakati ko haija (Haija) se snbndhit tika jaroor lagavaana chaahie - rogi ke isatemaal se snbndhit har chij ko doosare logon se alag rakhen - paani men phinaail daalakar pharash ko saaph karen, aisa karane se kitaanu mar jaate hain। Home Remedies: pey padaarath ki maatara barhaayen। paani, nimboo paani, chhaachh aadi pite rahen। ghar par oaaraes taiyaar karen, isake lie chaar kap paani men chhah chhote chamamach chini aur aadhi chhoti chamamach namak milaaen aur jitama jayaada pi saken, pien। dahi men kela milaakar khaaen। adarak ko kadadookas karake shahad ke saath milaakar khaaen। yadi shauch men khoon ke dhababe a rahe hon to adarak n khaaen। ek gilaas paami men shahada, nimboo aur namak milaakar piyen। 10 se 20 miligaraam jink ki jaroorat roj hoti hai, aise men jink ke sapaliment len। payaaj aur kaali mirach ko pisakar pesat banaaen। ise din men tin baar ek haphate ke lie khaaen। laung daalakar paani ko ubaalen aur chhaanakara, is paani ko pien। dahi men methi paaudar aur jira paaudar daalakar khaaen। ninboo ke ras men kachachi haladi ki jaren 2 ghnte ke lie bhiga kar rakhen aur baad men pisakar ek kntenar men rakh lem। ek kap paani men is pesat ki kuchh maatara ko paani aur shahad milaakar pien। Disease: jaraman mijalas ya roobela (German Measles) Description: jaraman mijalas ya roobela (German measles) naaka, sns ki nali aur phepharom se snbndhit snkaraman ko roobela kahate hain। yah ek tarah ka khasara hai jise roobiyola ya jaraman mijalas ke naam se bhi jaana jaata hai। yah behad snkaramit hota hai aur teji se ek vayakati se doosare vayakati men phail jaata hai। snkaramit vayakati ke snparak men aane se yah teji se doosare vayakati ko bhi snkamit kar chhote bachache, garabhavati mahilaaen ya aisa koi bhi vayakati jisaki imayooniti kam ho, roobela ka shikaar ho sakata hai। roobela se pirit vayakati men kai jatilataaem bhi ho sakati haim, khaasakar aratharaaitis ke lakashan aana Treatments: tipas (Tips to Prevent German Measles) - sharir ko poori tarah se aaraam den। - dosaton, sahakaramiyon, khaasakar garabhavati mahilaaon ko apani bimaari ke baare men bataaen aur khud se door rahane ki salaah den। - aise logom se bhi door rahen jinaki imayooniti kamajor ho। - snkaramit vayakati apane isatemaal ki sabhi chijen doosare logon se door rakhe। - doosare logon ko snkaramit vayakati ke snparak se bachana chaahie। saath hi rogi ko khud bhi is snbndh men saavadhaani rakhani chaahie। upachaar (Treatment of German measles) paani men ninboo daalakar pien। naariyal ka paani pien। likoresi ki jar ke paaudar mem shahad milaakar rogi ko chataaen। nim ki patatiyon ko daalakar paani garam karen, is paani se snkaramit vayakati ko sanaan karaaen। lahasun ki kaliyon ko pisakar usamen shahad milaakara, rogi ko chataaen। nvala paaudar ko paani ke saath milaakara, is paani se sharir ponchhe। jau ke paani men baadaam ke tel ki kuchh boonde daalakar pien। dhayaan rakhane yogay baaten (Precautions for german measles) - rogi ko eknt kamare men rakhem, jahn ghar ke anay sadasay kam jaate hon। - rogi ko garam paani pine ko dete rahen। khaasakar subah khaali pet jaroor garam paani pine ko den। - rogi ko samaya-samay par tarah tarah ke joos pine ko den। - imayooniti barhaane vaala khaanaa, phal aur sabajiyn khaane ko den। - rogi ko sooraj ki roshani se bacha ke rakhen। - doodh ya doodh se bame amay khaaday padaarath rogi ko n den। - rogi ka kamara hamesha saaph aur havaadaar rakhen। Disease: inaphalooenja (Influenza) Description: inaphalooenja (Influemza) imaphalooemja ko saadhaaran bhaasha men phaloo (flu) ke naam se jaana jaata hai, jisamen shavasan tntar men snkaramam (infection im respiratory system) ho jaata hai। is tarah ka phaloo adhikatar saradiyon ke mausam men vaayaral bimaari ke roop men hota hai। yah un logon ko jayaada parabhaavit karata hai jinaki rog paratirodhak kashamata kisi bimaari ke kaaran kam hui ho। Symptoms: - asaamaanay thakaan mahasoos hona। - kaph - chakakar aana - chhink aana - thnd ke saath bukhaar aanaa, - tavacha ka nila parana - naak bahana hona - pet ya chhaati par dabaav mahasoos hona aur darad hona - marij par behoshi haavi ho - mnsapeshiyon men darad - sns phoolama - sns lene men kathinaai - siradarad hona - ulati Reasons: kaaran (Reasoms of Influenza) inaphalooenja maam ke vaayaras se hi yah rog phailata hai। phaloo ka vaayaras naaka, nkh aur munh ki masakas membaren ke davaara sharir men paravesh karata hai। har baar jab bhi inamen se kisi bhi ng ko haath lagaaya jaata hain, vayakati khud ko khud hi phaloo ke jivaanu se snkaramit karata hai। phaloo tin parakaar ka hota hai, e, bi aur si। taaip e aur bi vaarashik inaphalooenja ka kaaram hote hain jisase lagabhag 20 phisadi log parabhaavit hote hain। taaip e men echa1ena1, echa2ema2 aur echa3ena3 shaamil hain। taaip e ke inphalooenja mem parivaratan hota hai jisase parabhaavit vayakati ko parayaapat imayooniti nahin mil paati। taaip si bhi phaloo ke lakashan darashaata hai lekim is tarah ka phaloo kam hota hai। haalnki tinon tarah ka phaloo ek hi tarah se phailata hai aur inake lakashan bhi ek jaise hi hote hain। jatilataaen- (Complications during influenza) - yuvaa, bachachon tatha 65 ki umar se adhik ke bujuragon men jatilata ho sakati hai। - garabhavati mahilaaon ko bhi phaloo ka khatara jayaada rahata hai। - inphalooenja se nimoniyaa, kaan men snkaramama, saainas smkaraman aur baronkaaitis ka khatara barh jaata hai। - yadi uchach shareni ka phaloo ho to, entivaayaral davaaen upayukat rahati hain, anayatha vayakati ki maut bhi ho sakati hai। Treatments: upachaar (Treatment of Influenza) - garam paani men ninboo daalakar pien - thnda aur baasi khaana n khaaen - logon se haath n milaaen - paami se bhigane ke baad sharir ko achachhi tarah sukhaaen - paratidin vayaayaam karen - sharir ki rog paratirodhak kashamata barhaane vaale khaaday padaarathon ka sevan karen - garabhavati mahilaaen aur bachachon ko pine ka paani ubaalakar den - ashavagndha aur kaalamegh jaisi jari bootiyn sharir ka taapamaan kam karane men madad karati hain - paami men ajavaayan daalakar ubaal len। paani tak tak ubaalen jab tak aadha n rah jaae, is paani ko samas samay par pite rahen। tipasa- (Tips to Prevent Influenza) - sharir ko poori tarah aaraam den - naak ko samaya-samay par saaph karate rahen - garam paani ki botal ya hiting paid se sikaai karen - bina haath dhoe kabhi khaama n khaaen - jayaada se jayaada taral padaarath len, soopa, ninboo paani aadi pite rahen Disease: meminajaaitis (Meningitis) Description: meninajaaitis (Meningitis) meninajaaitis ko dimaagi bukhaar (Dimagi Bukhar) bhi kahate hain। yah aamataur par vaayarasa, baikatiriyaa, kavaka, parajivi, aur kuchh jivom ke snkaraman ke kaaran hota hai। shaaririk dosh ya kamajor paratirakasha paranaali ko aavaratak baikatiriyal meninajaaitis se jora ja sakata hai। yah ek tarah ka inphekashan hota hai jo mashatishak aur rirh ki hadadi ki rakasha karane vaale menbarem men soojan paida kar deta hai। adhiknsh maamalon men isaka kaaran vaayaras hota hai। haalnki, dimaagi bukhaar ke kuchh gaira-snkaraamak kaaran bhi maujood hain। Symptoms: - chhote bachachon mem, niman lakashanon par gaur karana chaahie- (symptoms in toddlers) - bahut tej ya karaah kar rona - tej ya asaamaanay snse - pila ya daanon vaala chehara - laal ya baingani rng ke dhababe - bare bachachon men, niman lakashanon ko dekhama chaahie- (symptoms in younger children) - garadan men akaran - pith aur joron men gnbhir darad - bahut tej sir darad - chamakadaar roshani se chirh hona - bahut thnde haath aur pair - knpana - teji se sns lena - mnsapeshiyon men darad - haathon aur pairom ka thnda hona - bukhaar - siradarad - ulati Reasoms: dimaagi bukhaar ke kaaran (Causes of Meningitis) meminajaaitis men baikatiriya baladasatarim men paravesh karake dimaag aur sapaain kaorad men chala jaata hai। kai baar jukaam ya saaimas ki samasaya hone se bhi yah baikatiriya naak aur munh ke davaara sharir men paravesh kar jaate hain aur dimaag men soojan paida kar dete hain। dimaagi bukhaar (Dimagi Bukhar) ka entibaayotik davaaon se ilaaj kiya ja sakata hai। meninajaaitis ko jnchame ke lie galaas tesat bhi kiya ja sakata hai। galaas tesata- yadi knch ke gilaas ke kimaare ko sharir ke upar hue dhababon par dabaaya jaae to yah phed nahin hote। yah meninagokokakal sepatikaamiya (meningococcal septicaemia) ka lakasham hota hai। is avasatha se pirit vayakati ke sharir par gulaabi rng ke daane ho jaate hain jo baad men baimgani rng ke bare daanon mem tabadil ho jaate hain। Treatments: upachaar (Treatment of Meningitis or Dimagi Bukhar) - sharir ko poori tarah aaraam den। - rogi ko ndhere aur shnt kamare men rakhen। - likavid phood m len। oaaraes ka ghol garam paani men len। - rogi ko anaar ka joos den aur lahasun ka sevan bhi karavaayen। - sharir ke taapamaan ko kam karane ke lie baraph ke tukaron ko kapare mem lapetakar sikaai karen। - yadi rogi ko ulati ho rahi hon, to use ek taraph karavat lekar litaayen jisase ulati ki mahak use m aae। Disease: haarat balaokej (Heart Blockage) Description: haarat balaokej (Heart blockage) haarat balaokej mem manushay ki dharakan suchaaroo roop se kaam karana bnd kar deti hain। is dauraan dharakan rook rook kar chalati hai। kuchh logom me yah samasaya janam ke saath se hi shuroo ho jaati hai jabaki kuchh logon men bare hone par samasaya vikasit hoti hai। janamajaat balaokej ki samasaya ko konagenital haarat balaokej (congenital heart blockage) jabaki baad men hui samasaya ko ekavaayarad haarat balaokej (acquired heart blockage) kahate haim। aadhunik rahana-sahan aur khaane-pine ki aadaton ke chalate adhiknsh logom men haarat balaokej ki samasaya aam hoti ja rahi hai। haarat balaokej ko jnchane ke lie ilekatarokaaradiyogaraam (electro cardiogram) tesat kiya jaata hai। Symptoms: - chhaati men darada, sns phoolana - jaladi thak jaana - siradarad hona - chakakar aana - behosh hona Reasons: balaokej ke kaarana- (Cause of Heart Blockage) haarat men balaokej ya rookaavat palaok ke kaaran hoti hai। palaokasa, kolesataraola, phaita, phaaibar tishayoo aur shavet rakat kanikaaon ka misharan hota hai, jo dhire dhire nason ki divaaron par chipak jaata hai। palaok ka jamaav gaarhepan aur usake tore jaane ki paravaritati ko lekar alaga-alag tarah ke hote hain। agar yah gaarhaapan haarad hogaa, to aise palaok ko satebal kaha jaata hai aur yadi yah mulaayam hoga to ise tore jaane ke anukool maana jaata hai, aur ise anasatebal palaok kaha jaata hai। satebal palaok (Stable Plaque):- satebal palaok se rookaavat ki maatara se koi pharak nahin parataa, m hi isase gnbhir haarat ataik hota hai। is tarah ka palaok dhire dhire barhata hai, aise men rakat paravaah ko nai aaratarij (artries) ka raasata dhoondhane ka mauka mil jaata hai, jise koletaral vesel (collateral vessal) kahate hain। ye vesel balaok ho chuki aaratari ko baaipaas kar deti hain aur dil ki mnsapeshiyon tak aavashayak rakat aur aukasijam pahumchaati hain। anasatebal palaok (Unstable Plaque):- asathaai palaok men, palaok ke tootame para, ek khataranaak thakaka ban jaata hai, aur koletaral ko vikasit hone ka poora samay nahin mil paata hai। vayakati ki mnsapeshiyn (muscle) gnbhir roop se daimej ho jaati hain aur vah kai baar sadan kaaradiek deth (sudden cardiac death) ka shikaar ho jaata hai। Treatments: haarat balaokej se bachane ke lie saamaanay tipasa- (Tips to Prevent Heart Blockage) - dhoomarapaan n karen, yahn tak ki koi doosara dhoomarapaan kar raha ho, to bhi khud ko bachaayem। - hariday ko savasath rakhane ke lie dinacharaya men vayaayaam ko shaamil karana behad jaroori hai। - aisa bhojan karen, jisase hariday ko laabh ho। - hariday ko savasath rakhane ke lie sharir ka vajan miyntarit rakhen। - roj aadha ghnta paidal chalem। - liphat ki jagaha, sirhiyon ka isatemaal karem। Home Remedies: haarat balaokej ke ghareloo upachaara- (home remedies for heart blockage) ek kap doodh men lahasum ki tin se chaar kali daalakar ubaalen। is doodh ko roj pien। ek gilaas doodh men haladi daalakar ubaalen aur gunaguna rahane par shahad daalakar pien। ek gilaas gunagune paani men nimboo ka rasa, kaali mirach aur shahad daalakar pien। do se tin kap adarak ki chaay rojaana pien। isake lie paani men adarak daalakar ubaalem aur shahad milaakar pien। methi daane ko raat bhar paani men bhigaakara, subah methi chabaakar khaayen aur bacha hua paani pi jaaen। khaane men ya salaad men alasi ke bijom ka isatemaal karen। khaame men saamaanay chaaval ki jagah laal yisat chaaval ka isatemaal karen। Disease: kaan men snkaraman (Ear Infectiom) Description: kaan men snkaraman (Ear Infection ) kaan sharir ke sabase mahatavapooran aur snvedanashil ngon men se ek hain। sharir ka yah ek aisa hisasa hai jisaka dhayaan insaan sabase kam rakhata hai। kaan men snkaraman akasar baikatiriyal ya vaayaral smkaraman (Bacterial Viral Infection) ke kaaran hota hai jo ki madhay kaan ko parabhaavit karata hai jisamen chhoti hadadiyon ki pahaari bani hoti hai। isi men kaan ke parade ke pichhe hava se bhari jagah hoti hai। Symptoms: - kaan men darad hona - chakakar aana - sir darad - bukhaar - sunaai kam deta hai Reasoms: kaan men snkaraman kai jokhimon ko paida karata hai। snkaraman agar jayaada ndar nahin gaya ho to kuchh minat ke upachaar aur parakariyaaon ke davaara ise thik kiya ja sakata hai lekin yadi yah ntarik sathaan tak pahunch gaya hai tab aupareshan ki naubat bhi a sakati hai। kaan men snkaramam hone ke kaaran pirit ko niman pareshaaniyn ho sakati hai: * saradarada: kaan ka darad akasar sar men tanaav paida karata hai। * bukhaara: kaan men darad ke kaaram tivar darada, jalan aur bukhaar ho sakata hai। * chakakar aanaa: kaan ka darad kai baar sir men chakakar aane ka kaaran ban jaate hain। * sunane ki kashamataa: yadi is inphekashan ko lnbe samay tak anadekha kiya jaae to kaan ki suname ki shakati khatam ho sakati hai। Treatments: upachaar (Treatment of Ear Infection in Himdi) kaan ke snkaraman se bachane ke lie sabase jaroori hai saapha-saphaai ka vishesh dhayaan rakhanaa। isake atirikat kuchh niman baaten par amal kar bhi kaanon ke snkaramam se bacha ja sakata hai। vaikas ki saphaai (Cleaning of the wax)- kaan men atirikat vaikas kaan men baikatiriya ko barhaakara, kaan men snkaraman paida karati hai। kaan ki vaikas ko chikitasakon davaara sookasham upakaranon se saaph karaaya ja sakata hai। amooman log iyar bad se bhi kaan ki saphaai kar lete hain lekin yadi vekas jayaada hai to use iyar bad se saaph mahin kiya ja sakataa। iyar daraopas ka parayog (Use of Ear Drops)- kai dapha kaan ki dava daalane se bhi kaan ke snkaraman se nijaat mil jaati hai। chikitasak kaan darad ke lie iyar daraop dete hain jisase kaan ke darad ke saath hi vaikas bhi nikal jaati hai। tipasa- (Tips to Prevent Ear Infection) - saradi jukaam mem achachhi tarah se haath dhome ke baad hi khaanaa-pina khaaen। - saradi jukaam men baahar jaane se bachen। bhir vaali jagahom par snkaraman ka khatara jayaada hota hai। - dhoomarapaan se bachen। - bachachon men tikaakaran samay se karavaaen। unahen nayoomokokal tike jaroor lagavaaen। Home Remedies: ghareloo upaaya- (Home Remedies) 1- kaan men darad ho to gainde ke phool ko pisakar usaka ras daalane se aaraam hota hai। 2- namak ko garam karake use kapare men bndh kar kaam ki sikaai karane se bhi kaan ke darad se aaraam milata hai। 3- khaana banaane vaale tel men lahasun daalakar tel garam karen। is tel ki kuchh boonde tin se chaar baar kaan men daalen। 4- tulasi ke pataton ka ras nikaalakar kaan ke aas paas malane se bhi aaraam hota hai। dhayaan rahe ras ko kaan ke mdar mahin daalana hai। 5- seb ke sirake men baraabar maatara mem paani milaakar rooi ko usamen bhigaaen। is rooi ko kaan ke pichhe kuchh der lagaakar rakhem। 6- auliv auyal ko garam karake, gunagune tel ki kuchh boonde kaan men daalen। 7- garam paani ki botal se kaan ki sikaai karen। 8- payaaj ko garam karake use mikasi men pisakar ras nikaal len। payaaj ke ras ki kuchh boonde kaan men daalen। Disease: daayabitik retinopaithi (Diabetic Retinopathy) Description: daayabitik retinopaithi (Diabetic retinopathy) daayabitik retinopaithi ek bimaari hai, jo madhumeh (diabeties) se pirit vayakati ki retina (nkh ka parada jahn tasavir banati hai) ko parabhaavit karati hai। yah retina ko rakat pahunchaane vaali mahin nalikaaon ke kashatigarasat hone ke kaaran hota hai, agar isaka samay par ilaaz n karaaya jaae to pirit vayakati mdhepan ka shikaar ho sakata hai। daayabitik retinopaithi duniya men ndhepan ka sabase bara kaaran hai, jisake maamale har saal barhate ja rahe hain। Symptoms: - nkhon ka baara-baar snkaramit hona - chashame ka nmbar baara-baar badalana - retina se khoon aana - saphed motiyaabind ya kaala motiyaabind - siradarad rahana ya ekaaek mkhon ki roshani kam ho jaana - subah uthane ke baad kam dikhaai dena Reasons: daayabitik retinopaithi ke kaaran (Causes of Diabetic Retinopathy) madhumeh (Diabetes), yadi bahut lnbe samay tak rah jaae to yah sharir ke doosare ngon ko bhi parabhaavit karata hai aur yah parabhaavit ng nkhen bhi ho sakati hain। daayabitiz rakat vaahikaaon ki divaar ko parabhaavit karata hai, jisase retina (jisapar chhavi banati hai) tak aukasijan le jaane vaali naariyn kamazor ho jaati hain। daayabitiz ke marizon men agar shugar ki maatara miyntarit nahin rahati, to vah daayabitik retimopaithi ki samasaya se garasat ho sakate hain। is samasaya ka pata tab chalata hai jab yah bimaari gnbhir roop le leti hai। ndhepan ka ek paramukh kaaran hai ‘daayabitik retinopaithi’ bhi hai। daayabitik retinopaithi ke do mukhay charan hote haim। shurooaati charan ko naan parolipheretiv daayabitik retinopaithi (enapidiaara) kahate hain। is charan men retina kashetar ki nalikaaen kashatigarasat ho jaati haim। saamaanayat bimaari ka yah shurooaati charan hota hai, jisamen lakashanon ka pata mahin chalata hai। kuchh maamalon men kashatigarasat rakat nalikaaon ke phatane se retina ke madhay bhaag men rakat fail jaata hai। is sathiti ko daayabitik maikayulopaithi kahate hain, isase darishati parabhaavit hoti hai aur dhundhala dikhane lagata hai। isake unanat aur vikasit charan ko parolipheretiv daayabitik retinopaithi (pidiaara) kahate hain। yah daayabitik retinopaithi ki sabase sabase gnbhir charam hai। is charan men retima kashetar men kamazor avnchhaniy rakat nalikaaen tezi se panapane lagati hain jo retina ki aukasijan aapoorati mem baadha paida kar use kashatigarasat karati hain। is kaaran retinal ditechament ya galookoma bhi ho sakata hai। karib 20 phisadi madhumeh piriton men pidiaar ki vajah se gnbhir darishati dosh ho sakata hai jo ndhepan ka kaaran banaata hai। Treatments: surakasha ke lie kuchh tipas (Tips to prevent diabetic retinopathy) - samaya- samay par nkhom ki jnch karaayen, yah jmch bachachon men bhi aavashayak hai। - rakat mem kaolesatarol aur shugar ki maatara ko niyntarit rakhen। - agar aapako nkhon men darada, ndhera chhaame jaise lakashan dikhaai den to turnt chikitasak se milem। - daayabitiz ke mariz ko saal men kam se kam ek baar apani mkhon ki jnch karaani chaahie। - daayabitiz hone ke das saal baad har tin mahine par nkhon ki jmch karaayen। - garabhavati mahila agar daayabitik hai to chikitasak se snparak karen। saamaamay upachaar (Treatment for diabetic retinopathy) - vitaamin e yukat khaaday padaarathon ka sevan adhik karen - paalak ko apane bhojan men shaamil karen - kaale ngoor ke bijon ka ras pien - salaad jayaada se jayaada khaaen Disease: galookoma (Glaucoma) Description: galookoma (Glaucoma) galookomaa, kaala motiya ya kmch bimdu roga, tntar men gnbhir evn nirntar kashati karate hue dhire-dhire darishati ko samaapat hi kar deta hai। kisi vasatu se parakaash ki kiranen nkhon tak pahumchati hain, v usaki chhavi darishati patal (Retina) par banaati hai। retina se yah soochana vidayut tarngon davaara masatishak tak netar tntuon davaara pahunchaai jaati hai। nkh men ek taral padaarath bhara hota hai yah taral padaarath nkh ke gole ko chikama kie rahata hai yadi is taral padaarath ka risaav ruk jaae to nkh ke ndar ka daab barh jaata hai। galookoma men ntar netar par daaba, parabhaavit nkhon ki daab sahane ki kashamata se adhik ho jaata hai, isake parinaamasavaroop netar tntu ko kashati pahunchati hai, jisase darishati chali jaati hai। kisi vasatu ko dekhate samay galookoma se garasit vayakati ko keval vasatu ka kendar dikhaai deta hai। samay ke saath sathiti bad se badatar hoti jaati hai। saamaanayata: log is par bahut kam hi dhayaan dete hain, lekin jab dhayaan dete haim tab tak bahut der ho chuki hoti hai। saamaanay taur par yah rog bina kisi lakashan ke vikasit hota hai v donon nkhon ko ek saath parabhaavit karata hai। haalnki yah rog 40 varash se adhik aayu ke vayasakon ke bich paaya jaata hai, phir bhi kuchh maamalon men yah navajaat shishuon ko bhi parabhaavit kar sakata hai। madhumeha, aanuvnshikataa, uchach rakatachaap v hariday rog is rog ke paramukh kaaranon men se hain। vishav satar par kaala motiya lagabhag chhah karor logon ko parabhaavit karata hai aur bhaarat men yah ndhatav ka doosara sabase kaaran hai। Symptoms: - tayoobalaait ya balab ki roshani chaaron or se dhundhali dikhane lagati hai, nkhon men tej darad bhi hone lagata hai। - dhundhalaapana, kai rogiyon ko raat men dikhana bhi bnd ho jaata hai - mitali ya ulati hona - siradarad Reasons: galookoma ke kaaram (Causes of Glaucoma) maamav nkh mem sathit kaaraniya ke pichhe nkhon ko sahi aakaar aur poshan dene vaala taral padaarath (Aqueous Humor Fluid) hota hai, lens ke chaaron or sathit siliyari utatak is taral padaarath ko lagaataar banaate rahate hain yah taral padaarath putaliyon ke davaara nkhon ke bhitari hisase men jaata hai is tarah se nkhom men is taral padaarath ka banana aur bahana lagaataar hota rahata hai। savasath mkhon ke lie yah aavashayak hai nkhon ke bhitari hisase men kitana dabaav rahe yah taral padaarath ki maatar par nirabhar rahata hai। galookoma rogiyon ki nkhon men is taral padaarath ka dabaav atayadhik barh jaata hai kabhi-kabhi nkhon ki bahaav nalikaaon ka maarag rook jaata hai, lekin siliyari utak ise lagaataar banaate hi jaate hain, aise men jab mkhon mem darishati-tntu ke upar taral ka dabaav achaanak barh jaata hai to galookoma ho jaata hai। yadi mkhon men taral ka itana hi dabaav lnbe samay tak bana rahata hai to isase nkhon ke tntu bhi nashat ho sakate hain। samay rahate yadi is bimaari ka ilaaj nahin karaaya jaata hai to isase darishati poori tarah ja sakati hai। Treatments: saamaanay upachaar (Treatment and tips to prevent Glaucoma) - khaane men paalak jayaada khaaen - vitaamin e nkhon ke savaasathay ke lie behad jaroori hai। aise khaaday padaarath khaaem jinase vitaamin e ki poorati ho। - saunph bhi savasath nkhon ke lie achachha ghareloo nusakha hai। Disease: bavaasir (Piles) Description: bavaasir (Piles) ek asaadhay rog hai। ise hemorahoyadas (Haemorrhoids), paailas ya moolavayaadhi bhi kahate hain। bavaasir ko aayuraved men arash yaani diraghakaalin paraanaghaatak bimaari kaha jaata hai। bavaasir men nt ke ntim hisase ya malaashay (gudaa) ki bhitari divaar men rakat ki dhamani aur shiraaon men soojan ho jaati hai aur vo tanakar phail jaati hai। mal tayaag ke vakat jor lagaane ya davaab dene se ya kabaj ke kare mal se ragar khaane se rakat ki nason mem daraar par jaati hai aur natija usamem se khoom ka saraav hone lagata hai। Symptoms: - khujali malaashay men atakane ki amubhooti - khooni bavaasir men gudaadavaar ke ndar soojan hoti hai - khooni bavaasir men masase khooni surakh hote hai aur unase khoon girata hai - darad evn rakatasaraav - bavaasir men jalan tatha darad hone lagata hai - baadi bavaasir men masase kaale rng ke hote hain - baahari bavaasir men gudaadavaar ke baahar ki or ke masase mote-mote daanon jaise ho jaate haim - manovikaar - malaavarodh - masason men khaaj aur soojan hoti hai। Reasons: bavaasir ke kaaran (Causes of Piles) khooni ho ya baadi donon hi bavaasir (Piles) ke lie jo kaarak jimamevaar hote hain vo lagabhag ek hi haim। bavaasir ke kuchh aham kaaran niman hain: kabaj (Constipation) bavaasir ki sabase bari vajah pet men kabaj banama hai। kabaj ki vajah se mal sookha aur kathor ho jaata hai jisaki vajah se usaka nikaas aasaani se nahin ho paataa। malatayaag ke vakat rogi ko kaaphi vakat tak shauchaalay men ukadoo baithe rahama parata hai, jisase rakat vaahaniyon par jor parata hai aur vah phoolakar latak jaati hai। mal ke dabaav se vahn ki dhamaniym chapati ho jaati hain aur jhilaliyn phail jaati hain। jisake kaaran vayakati ko bavaasir (Haemorrhoids) ho jaati hai। talaa-bhuna hua bhojan (Fried and roasted food) jayaada miracha- masaale, tali hui aur chatapati chijem khaane, mnsa, ndaa, rabari, mithaai, malaai jaise der se pachane vaale bhojan karane se bhi bavaasir rog hota hai। aavashayakata se adhik bhojan karana bhi bavaasir ka paramukh kaaran hai। garam paani (Hot water) shauch karane ke baad maladavaar ko garam paami se dhome se bhi bavaasir rog ho sakata hai। davaaiyn (Medicatioms) davaaiyon ka adhik sevan karame ke kaaran bhi bavaasir (Bawasir) rog ho sakata hai। khaasakar disapepasiya aur kisi julaab ki goli ka adhik dinom tak isatemaal karane se। nind men kami (Insomania) nind poori nahin hone ke kaaran pet men khaana sahi tarah se pach mahin paata aur natija kabaj ho jaata hai। kabaj se bavaasir ki shikaayat ho jaati hai। aanuvnshikata (Heridetry) bavaasir (Bawasir) ki bimaari aanuvnshik hai। agar parivaar men aapake daadaa-daadi, naanaa-naani, maataa-pita kisi ko bhi bavaasir thi ya hai to aapako bhi yah bimaari ho sakati hai। yah rog pirhi dar pirhi hota rahata hai। anay vajahen (Other Causes of Piles) - garabhaavasatha me bharoon ka dabaab paranaa। - sharaab aur anay nashile padaarathon ke sevan se bhi bavaasir hota hai। - bavaasir guda ke kainsar ki vajah se ya mootar maarag men rukaavat ki vajah se ya garabhaavasatha men bhi ho sakata hai। Treatments: dekhabhaal aur upachaar (Treatments and Tips to Prevent Piles ) - sabase pahale kabaj ko door kar mal tayaag ko saamaanay aur niyamit karana aavashayak hai। isake liye taral padaarathon, hari sabajiyon evn phalon ka bahutaayaat men sevan karem। baadi bavaasir (Haemorrhoids) ke marij tali hui chizen, miracha-masaalon yukat bhojan n karen। - raat men sote samay ek gilaas paani men isabagol ki bhoosi ke do chamamach daalakar pine se bhi laabh hota hai। - guda ke bhitar raat men sone se pahale aur subah mal tayaag ke poorav malaham lagaana bhi mal nikaas ko sugam karata hai। - guda ke baahar latake aur sooje hue masason par galisarin aur maiganeshiyam salaphet ke misharan ka lep lagaakar patati bndhane se bhi kaaphi aaraam milata hai aur phaayada hota hai। - masason ko hataane ke lie bhi kai vidhiyn upalabadh hai। masasom men injekasham davaara aisi dava ka paravesh kiya jaata hai jisase masase sookh jaate hain। - masasom par ek vishesh upakaran davaara rabar ke chhalale charha die jaate hain, jo masason ka rakat paravaah rokakar unahen sukhaakar nikaal dete hain। - ek anay upakaran davaara masason ko baraf men parivaratit kar nashat kiya jaata hai। - sarajari davaara bhi masason ko kaatakar mikaal diya jaata hai। - bavaasir (Piles) ke marij ko sabase pahale 2 din tak rasaahaar chizon ka sevan karake upavaas rakhana chaahie। isake baad 2 sapataah tak bina pake hua bhojan ka sevan karake upavaas rakhana chaahie। - masason ki soojan barh gai ho ya phir masason se khoon adhik mikal raha hai to mitati ki patati ko baraf se thnda karake phir isako masason par 10 minat tak rakhakar is par garam senk dena chaahie। - bavaasir rog ko thik karane ke lie kuchh upayogi aasan hai jaise- naarishodhana, kapaalabhaati, bhujngaasana, paraanaayaama, pavamamukataasana, shalabhaasana, supatavajaraasana, dhanuraasana, shavaasana, saravngaasana, matasayaasana, halaasana, chakaraasam aadi। Home Remedies: bavaasir ke lie ghareloo upaay Home Remedies for Piles mooli ka niyamit sevan bavaasir ko thik kar deta hai। raat ko sote samay kele khaane chaahie isase rogi ko bahut adhik laabh milata hai। paalaka, bathuaa, patata gobhi, chaulaai, soyaa, kaali jiri ke patate ka saag khaana chaahie। rogi vayakati ko subah tatha shaam ke samay 2 bhigoi hui njir khaami chaahie aur isaka paani pina chaahie। tariphala ka chooran lena chaahie। aisa kuchh dinon tak karame se bavaasir rog jaladi hi thik ho jaata hai। 2 chamamach til chabaakar thnde paani ke saath paratidin sevan karane se bavaasir kuchh hi dinon men thik ho jaata hai। rogi vayakati ko apane bhojan men chukanadara, phool gobhi aur hari sabajiyon ka bahut adhik upayog karana chaahie। hari sabajiyon men paravala, papitaa, bhindi, kela ka phoola, mooli, gaajara, shalajama, karelaa, turai khaana chaahie। gur men belagiri milaakar khaane se rogi vayakati ko bahut adhik laabh milata hai aur bavaasir rog thik ho jaata hai। paka papitaa, paka bela, seba, naashapaati, ngoora, tarabooja, mausami phala, kishamisha, chhuaaraa, munakakaata, njira, naariyala, sntaraa, aama, anaar khaana bavaasir men phaayademnd hota hai। masason par sarason ka tel lagaana chaahie, phir isake baad apane peroo par mitati ki patati karani chaahie aur isake baad enima lena chaahie tatha masason par mitati ka gola rakhana chaahie। raat ko 100 garaam kishamish paani men bhigo den aur ise subah ke samay mem ise usi paani men ise masal den। is paani ko rojaana sevan karane se kuchh hi dinon men bavaasir rog thik ho jaata hai। ninboo ko chirakar us par chaar garaam katatha pisakar burak dem aur use raat men chhat par rakh dem। subah donon tukaron ko choos len, yah khooni bavaasir ki utatam dava hai। chokar samet aate ki roti, gehoon ka daliyaa, haath kutaa- puraana chaavala, sothi chaaval ka bhaata, chana aur usaka satatoo, moonga, kulathi, moth ki daala, chhaachh ka niyamit sevan karana chaahie। Disease: mkhom ka inphekashan (Eye Infection) Descriptiom: nkhom ka inphekashan (Eye Infection) nkhon men inphekashan haanikaarak sookasham jivaanu baikatiriya aur vaayaras ke kaaran hota hai। ye haanikaarak sookasham jivaanu maanasoon ke mahine men sabase jayaada sakariy hote hain। ye nkhon ki upari bhaaga, putali, kaoramiya aur palakon par aakaraman karate hain jisase nkhom men soojana, jalan hoti hai। nkh jarurat se jayaada laal ho jaati hai aur mkhon se jarurat se jayaada paani ka disachaaraj hone lagata hai। Symptoms: - nkhon se paani nikalana - nkhon se mavaad nikalana - dhundhala vijan - nkhon ka sookh jaana - palakon par soojan - nkhom men khoojalaahat - nkhon men darad aur jalan - nkhe laal hona Reasons: nkhon ke inphekashan ke kaaran (Causes and Reasons of Eye Infection) nkhon ke inphekashan se sabase jayaada nkhon ki palaken parabhaavit hoti hai। palakon ke ndaruni hisase men soojan hone se nkhon ki sundarata to khatam hoti hi hai, samay par ilaaj nahin karaane se ghaav hone ka bhi khatara rahata hai। inphekashan jab nkhon ke ndar nsoo ki garnthi ko parabhaavit karata hai to soojan se nsoo ki garnthi bnd ho jaati hai aur yah kaaphi darad karane lagata hai। sabase jayaada gnbhir sathiti tab hoti hai jab inphekashan kaoraniya ko parabhaavit karati hai। isamen kaoraniyal alasar ka khatara rahata hai aur nkhon ki roshani tak chali jaati hai। kmjekativaaitis (Conjunctivitis)- knjekativaaitis nkhon ka sabase kaoman inphekashan hai jise pink aai bhi kahate hain। yah ek vaayaral inphekashan hai jo kaaphi teji se phailata hai। agar mn ko isaka imphekasham hai to navajaat ko bhi yah imphekashan ho sakata hai। vaairal keraatitis (viral keratitis)- pink aai ki tarah yah bhi ek qaomam aai inphekashan hai jo harapis ke vaayaras (Herpes simplex virus) ke kaaran hota hai। yah bhi kaaphi teji se phailata hai। phngal keraatitis (Fungal keratitis)- yah ek phngal inphekashan hai jo nkhon men kntekat lains lagaane se ho sakata hai। 2006 men yah inphekashan us samay characha mem aaya tha jab ek khaas tarah ke kntekat lains solayooshan ke isatemaal se kaaphi log is inphekasham ke shikaar ho gae the। vaise nkhon men phngal inphekashan kisi bhi tarah ke chot se ya phir auragenik maitar ke jaane se hota hai। taraakoma (Trachoma)- yah inphekasham kaaphi gnbhir hota hai aur ganadi jagah men teji se phailata hai। gndagi par pamapane vaale makakhiyon aur kiron ke nkh men ghusane se yah imphekashan hota hai। taraakoma mkhom ke niche vaale palak ko snkaramit karata hai, agar yah lnbe samay tak raha to kaoraniya tak men ghaav hone tak ka khatara rahata hai jisase marij hamesha ke lie ndha ho sakata hai।
