indophathelaamitis (Endophthalmitis)- jab nkhom ka inphekashan nkh ke ndar kaaphi gahare tak asar daal deta hai to use indophathelaamitis kahate hain। yah vaayaral aur baikateriyal donon tarah ke smkaraman se hota hai। nkhon mem gahari chot lagane se bhi isaka khatara rahata hai। Treatments: dekhabhaal aur ilaaj (Care and Treatment of Eye Infectiom) nkhon ke inphekashan ka ilaaj ab kaaphi saral aur aasaan ho gaya hai। entibaayotik aai daraopa, malaham aur senk se kai tarah ke snkaraman ka sahi tarike se ilaaj ho jaata hai। kai tarah ke vaayaral inphekashan kuchh dinon tak rahane ke baad khud hi thik ho jaata hai to gmbhir inphekashan hone par daokatar ko dikhaana jaroori hota hai। mkhom ki dekhabhaal ke saamaanay upachaara- (Tips to Prevent Eye imfection) -tariphala jal se nkhon ko dhote rahen, kaaphi kaam karegaa। -imali ke bij ko chndan ki tarah pisakar nkhon ki palakom par lep lagaane se kaaphi raahat milati hai। -subah uthate hi munh mem thnda paani bharakar munh phulaakar thnde jal se nkhon par chhinte maaren। aisa din mem tin baar karen। yah nkhon ke inphekasham ke lie kaaphi asaradaar hai। -saphed payaaj ke ras men shahad aur karapoor milaakar shishi men rakh len aur ise raat men sote samay nkhon men daalen। nkhon ke sabhi tarah ke inphekasham mem yah kaaphi kaaragar ilaaj hai। -do ratati phitakari ko baarik pisakar gulaab jal men gholakar rakh len। is nechural aai daraop ki do-do boond din men tin baar nkhon men daalen। yah sabhi tarah ke inphekashan men kaaragar hota hai। nkh ka soojana, laali ko kam karata hai aur nkhon men kich aur mavaad ka aana bnd ho jaata hai। amay tipasa- (Other Tips to prevent Eye Infectiom) -jisaki nkhe laal haim unake saamane jaane se bachen। agar unake saamane gae hain to nkhon men nkh daal kar baat nahim karen। unase milane ke baad turnt nkhon saabun se haath dhoen aur phir nkhon ko thnde paani se dhoem। -kmjekativaaitis (conjumctivitis) ke samay sakoola, auphis aur saaravajamik jagahom par enti vaairal sapare ka chhirakaav baara-baar karate rahana chaahie। -agar aap kntekat lains lagaate hain to apane mkhom ko chhoone se pahale haathon ko achachhe tarah se saaph kar len। -pirit vayakati se door rahen aur usaka tauliyaa, rumaala, beda, takiya ko hamesha enti-sepatik likavid se saapha-suthara rakhen। Home Remedies: nkh men hone vaala inphekashana, gnde haathon se nkh ko masalane se, paradooshan se, kisi doosare ke davaara isatemaal kie gae kaajal lagaane ya chashama pahanane se tatha nkhon ki achachhi parakaar saphaai n karane se hota hai। jaanie aai inphekashan se nijaat paane ke ghareloo upaay (Home remedies for eye infection): 1. garam paani (Hot Water)- halake garam paani ke isatemaal se nkh ko dhoen, isase nkhon ke upar jamane vaali gndagi hat jaati hai। isake baad rui ki madad se nkhon ko pochhen। 2. gulaab jal (Rose Water)- gulaab jal se nkh ko dhone se nkhon ka inphekashan kam ho jaata hai। do boomd gulaab jal nkhon men daalen। is upaay ko rojaana din mem do baar karen। 3. paalak aur gaajar ka ras (Spinach & Carrot Juice)- paalak aur gaajar ka ras nkhon ke snkaraman ke lie kaaphi laabhadaayak hota hai kayonki iname paae jaane vaale vitaamin mkhon ke lie kaaphi mahatavapooram hote hain। paalak ke 4 ya 5 pataton ko pisakar usaka ras nichor len। 2 gaajar ko bhi pisakar ras nikaal len। ek gilaas mem aadha kap paani len aur usamen gaajar aur paalak ke ras ko mila kar pien। aisa rojaana karame se nkh ka snkaramam kam hone lagata hai। 4. nvale ka ras (Aaml juice)- nkhon men snkaraman hone par nvale ka ras pime se bahut laabh milata hai। 3 se 4 mvale ke phal ko pis kar usaka ras nikaal len। ek gilaas paami men us ras ko mila kar pien। nvale ke ras ko subah khaali pet aur raat men sone se pahale din men do baar isatemaal karen। kuchh hi dinon men nkhon ka inphekashan door ho jaaegaa। 5. shahad aur paami (Honey and Water)- shahad se nkhon ko dhoma chaahie। isase nkhon ko behad laabh pahumchata hai। ek gilaas paani men 2 chamamach madhuras ko milaakar khuli nkhon men chhapake maaren। aisa karane se nkhon ka snkaraman door hoga aur nkhon ki gmdagi bhi saaph hogi। 6. haladi aur garam paani (Turmeric and Water)- garam paani men haladi ko milaakar rui se nkhon ko ponchhana chaahie। haladi paraakaritik roop se enti baikatiriyal aur enti sepatik gunon se bharapoor hoti hai। yah nkhon ki saphaai bhi karati hai aur snkaraman se bhi door rakhati hai। 7. aaloo (Potato)- aaloo men parachur maatara men sataarach hota hai, jisake isatemaal se nkhon ke snkaraman ko thik kiya ja sakata hai। aaloo ko patale- patale tukaron men kaat lem। raat men sone se pahale us kate hue aaloo ko 15 mimat tak apani nkhon ke upar laga kar rakhen aur baad use utaar den। Disease: piliya (Jaumdice) Description: piliya (Jaundice) piliya ek aisa rog hai jo ek vishesh parakaar ke vaayaras aur kisi kaaranavash sharir men pitat yaani rakat men bilirubin (Bilirubin Disorder) ki maatara barh jaane se hota hai। isamen marij ko pila peshaab hota hai। usake naakhooma, tavacha aur nkhom ka saphed bhaag pila par jaata hai aur marij ko kaaphi kamajori, kabaja, ji michalaanaa, siradarada, bhookh m lagama aadi shikaayat hone lagati hai। yah bahut hi sookasha‍m vishaanu (Virus) se hota hai। shuroo men jab rog dhimi gati se v maamooli hota hai tab isake lakashan dikhaai nahin parate hain, lekin jab yah gnbhir ho jaata hai to marij ki nkhe v naakhoon pile dikhaai dene lagate hain। jin vaayaras se yah hota hai usake aadhaar par mukha‍yath piliya tin parakaar ka hota hai (Types of Jaundice) vaayaral haipetaaitis e, vaayaral haipetaaitis bi tatha vaayaral haipetaaitis naon e v naon bi। sharir mem esiditi ke barh jaane, kaaphi dinon tak maleriya rahane, pitat nali mem pathari atakane, jayaada sharaab pine, adhik mamak aur tikhe padaarathon ke sevan se aur khoon men rakatakanon ki kami hone se bhi piliya (Piliya) rog hota hai। Symptoms: - nkh ke saphed bhaag ka pila ho jaana - aamaashay men soojan hona - ji michalaana - tavacha ka rmg pila ho jaana - daahini pasaliyom ke niche bhaaripan aana aur darad hona - pitat ke kaaran mal ka rng phika ya saphed ho jaana - pet mem darad hona - bhookh nahin lagana - vajan lagaataar kam hona - shaam men thakaa-thaka mahasoos karana aur 102 digari ke aasapaas bukhaar rahana Reasons: piliya rog ke kaaran (Causes and Reasons of Jaundice) jab sharir men laal rakat koshikaaen 120 din ke saaikil men ek nechural parakariya ke tahat tootati hai to vesat baai parodakat ke rup men bilirubin (Bilirubin Disorder) ka utapaadan hota hai। bilirubin ke jarie sharir ki saari gmdagi livar se chhan kar baahar nikalati hai। yah gndagi peshaab aur mal ke jarie baahar nikalati hai। agar livar men snkaraman hai ya phir rakat men bilirubin ki maatara 2.5 se jayaada ho jaati hai to livar ke gndagi saaph karame ki parakariya avarudadh ho jaati hai aur isi parisathiti men piliya ki bimaari ho jaati hai। piliya rog ke anay kaaran (Other Reasons & Causes of Jaundice) agar kisi snkaraman se laal rakat koshika apani saamaamay parakariya se pahale hi tootane lagati hai to rakat men bilirubin ki maatara barhame lagati hai। is parisathiti ko pari hepatik jaonadis kahate hain। maleriyaa, sakil sel enimiyaa, thelisimiya men aur kai aanuvnshik kaaranon se bhi rakat men bilirubin ki maatara achaanak barhane lagati hai jisase piliya (Piliya) rog hota hai। agar kisi kaaran se livar ko nukasaan pahuncha hai to livar se bilirubin banane ki kashamata hi kam ho jaati hai। ise intaraa-hepaatik jaonadis bhi kaha jaata hai। vaayaral haipetaaitis (Viral Hepatitis), livar ka alakohalik hona (Alcohol), tej bukhaar (Fever), livar kaimsar (Liver Cancer), galat davaaon ke sevam aur pairaasitaamol (Medicine Side effects) ke jayaada sevan se bhi intaraa-hepaatik jaonadis hote hain। motaapa men livar saairosis hone ka khatara rahata hai। jisase intaraa-hepaatik jaonadis ki snbhaavana rahati hai। gaol balaadar men patathara, painakariyaaj ka sahi dhng se kaam nahin karanaa, painakariyaaj kainsar ya phir gaol balaadar ke kainsar men bhi livar davaara baai parodakat bilirubin ko sharir se nikaalane ki parakariya bnd ho jaati hai। natija rakat mem bilirubim ki maatara kaaphi barh jaati hai aur gnbhir piliya rog ho jaata hai। Treatmemts: dekhabhaal aur ilaaj (Care amd Treatment for Jaundice) - dihaaidareshan hone par aai vi phalooyadas (IV fluids im case of dehydration) - enti baayotikas (antibiotics) - enti vaayaral dava (antiviral medicines) - balad tarmsaphayoojan (blood transfusions) - sateraoyadas (steroids) - kimotherepi, redieshan therepi aur navajaat ke lie phototherepi (chemotherapy/radiation therapy & phototherapy for newborms) - doodh v paami ubaal kar pien। - taaja v saaph aur garam bhojan karen। - sa‍vacha‍chh shauchaalay ka hi parayog karen। - sirinj ko 20 minat tak ubaal kar hi lagavaaen। - pine ke lie hamesha savachachh aur baikatiriya rahit paani ka hi isatemaal karen। - khaana banaane, parosane, khaane se pahale v baad men aur shauch jaane ke baad men haath saabun se acha‍chhi tarah dhona chaahie। - bhojan jaalidaar alamaari ya dhaka‍kan se dhak kar rakhana chaahie, taaki makakhiyon v dhool se bachaaya ja saken। - rogi bacha‍chon ko daoka‍tar jab tak yah m bata den ki ye rog muka‍t ho chooke hai sa‍kool ya baahar mahin jaane de। - raka‍t dene vaale va‍yakatiyon ki poori tarah jnch karame ke baad hi rakat len। agar rakat men bilirubin ki maatara jayaada hogi to aapako bhi piliya ho sakata hai। Home Remedies: piliya rog sookasham vishaanu ke kaaran hota hai। is rog ke hone par vayakati ke naakhun aur nkhen pili dikhaai deti hain। chikitasa ki bhaasha men piliya ko vaayaral haipetaaitis (Viral Hepatitis) kahate hain। piliya rog saapha-saphaai ke abhaav men ya dooshit paani aur bhojan ke sevan ke kaaran hota hai। piliya rog ke home par vayakati ko bhookh n laganaa, bukhaar rahanaa, ji michalaanaa, sir men darad honaa, peshaab ka pila aana tatha kamajori v thakaan laganaa, jaise lakashan najar aate hain। piliya hone par vayakati ka livar parabhaavit hota hai। yadi samay rahate piliya rog ka upachaar n kiya jaae to vayakati ki maritayu bhi ho sakati hai। jaanem piliya se bachaav ke ghareloo upachaar (Home Remedies for Jaumdice) 1. tamaatar ka ras (Tomato juice)- piliya hone par ek gilaas tamaatar ke ras men ek chutaki namak aur kaali mirach milaakar subah khaali pet pien। aaraam milegaa। 2. mooli ki patati (Radish leaves)- mooli ki patatiyon ko pisakara, usaka ras nikaalen। lagabhag aadha litar mooli ki patatiyon ka ras rojaana pien। das din ke bhitar rogi ko piliya se aaraam milegaa। 3. papite ki patati (Papay leaves)- ek chamamach papite ki patati ke pesat men ek chamamach shahad milaakara, rojaana takariban do haphaton tak khaaen। piliya ke upachaar ke lie yah behad phaayademnd ghareloo nusakha hai। 4. ganana (Sugarcane)- gananaa, paachan kariya ko duroosat karata hai saath hi livar ko bhi behatar tarike se kaaray karane men madad karata hai। upachaar ke lie ek gilaas gamane ke ras men minboo ka ras milaakar rojaana do baar pien। 5. tulasi ki patati (Basil leaves)- tulasi ki das se panadarah patati ka pesat banaakara, gaajar ke ras men mila len। is ras ko rojaanaa, do se tin haphaton tak pien। piliya rog se raahat milegi। 6. jau (Barley)- ek kap jau ko tin litar paani mem achachhi tarah ubaal len aur tin ghnte tak dhak kar rakh den। is paani ko din men kai baar pien। 7. ninboo (Lemon)- ninboo livar ko kashatigarasat hone se bachaata hai। ek gilaas paami men do ninboo nichoren aur pien। 8. baadaam (Almond)- baadaam ki 8 giri, 2 khajoor aur 5 ilaayachi ko paani men raatabhar bhigaakar rakhen। subah sabake chhilake utaarakara, pisakara, pesat taiyaar karen। isamen thora sa makakhan aur chini milakar khaaen। 9. haladi (Turmeric)- ek gilaas gunaguna paani len aur usamen haladi milaayem, is paani ko din bhar men tin se chaar baar pien। piliya ke upachaar ke lie behad parabhaavi upaay hai। 10. chhaachh (Buttermilk)- piliya home par chhaachh behad laabhakaari hai। dahi ko mathakar chhaachh taiyaar karen aur isamen kaali mirach aur bhuna jira milaakar pien। 11. kela (Banana)- pake hue kele ko kuchalakara, usamen shahad milaayen। is tarah ke kele ko din men do baar khaaen। 12. gaajar ka ras (Carrot juice)- gaajar ka taaja ras mikaalakar pien, piliya men raahat milegi। 13. bel ki patati (Wood apple leaves)- bel ki patati ko pisakar paaudar bana len। is paaudar ko paani men milaakar rojaana pien। piliya ke upachaar ke lie behad parabhaavi upaay hai। 14. kaimomaail chaay (Chamomile tea)- kaimomaail piliya rog men behad laabhakaari hai। kaimomaail ki patatiyon ki chaay banaakar pine se piliya rog jaladi thik hota hai। is chaay ko piliya thik hone ke baad bhi pina jaari rakh sakate hain। 15. nvala (Gooseberry)- nvala vitaamin si se bharapoor hota hai। piliya rog men nvale ka sevan karane se behad laabh hota hai। nvale ke sevam se livar bhi majaboot hota hai। Disease: dooradarashita ya dooradarishati dosh (Hyper Myopia) Description: dooradarashita ya dooradarishati dosh (Hyper Myopia) dooradarashita ya dooradarishati dosha, men koi bhi vayakati door ki chizon ko aasaani se aur saaf dekh sakate hain jabaki isamen karib ki chize dhundhali (blurr) dikhaai deti hain। dooradarishati dosh ko savaasathay ki bhaasha men haaiparopiya (hyperopia) kahate hain। dooradarishati dosh kitana gnbhir hai yah aapake dekhame ki kashamata par nirabhar karata hai। dekhane ke lie nkh ke do bhaag jimamedaar hote hain, kaoraniya aur lensa। kaoraniya nkh ke saamane ka paaradarashi hisasa hota hai jabaki lens nkh ke ndar bana hota hai jo ki chizon ko dekhane par unake shep men bhi badalaav karata hai। kaoraniya aur lens donon ek saath kaaray karate hain aur aane vaali roshani ko milaate hain aur ise retina par phokas karate hain। retinaa, aai baol yaani nkh ke gole ke pichhe hota hai। jab nkh mem parakaash paravesh karata hai to us par thik se phokas nahin ho paataa, yahi door darishati dosh hota hai। yadi nkh ka gola saamaanay se chhota ho tab bhi door darishati dosh ho sakata hai। door darishati dosh bahut aam samasaya hai jise aasaani se thik bhi kiya ja sakata hai। Symptoms: - asaamaanay thakaan mahasoos hona। - nkh ke chaaron aur jalan ya darad - tamaavagarasat hona - dhundhala dikhana (nkh ke ekadam paas kaa) - parhane likhane men dikakat hona Reasons: dooradarashita ya dooradarishati dosh ke kaaran (Causes & Reasoms of Hyper Myopia) dooradarashita ya dooradarishati dosh men door ki chijen saaph aur paas ki chijen dhundhali najar aati hain। nkh ke visharaam ki sathiti mem, parakaash ki samntar kiranen darishatipatal ki snvedanashil parat se kuchh pichhe phokas hoti hain। isi kaaran vayakati ko paas ki chijen dekhane men pareshaani hoti hai। isake alaava yadi maata pita ko door darishati dosh hai to yah bachachon ko bhi parabhaavit kar sakata hai। isake alaava umar barhane ke saath bhi yah samasaya shuroo ho sakati hai। dooradarashita ko door karane ke lie sabase aasaan tarika chashama ya kaonataikat lens hota hai। lens ke parayog se nkhon men paravesh karane vaali roshani par behatar tarah se kendarit kar paate hain। Treatments: dooradarashita ya dooradarishati ki rokathaam ke lie tipas (Treatment & Tips to Prevent Hyper Myopia) - let kar nahin parhana chaahie। - parhane likhane ke dauraan behatar roshani honi chaahie। - hari sabajiyn aur phalon ka parayog khaane men jaroor karen। - tivi ya knpayootar par lagaataar kaam na karen, lagaataar na dekhem। - tivi ya knpayootar par kaaray karate vaqat bhi kamare men parayaapat roshani hona jaruri hai। Home Remedies: dooradarashita ya dooradarishati dosh ke ghareloo upaaya- (Home Remedies for Hyper Myopia) nkhon ki raushani tej ho isake lie vitaamin se pooram bhojan karen। doodh aur dahi jaise khaaday padaarath jaroor khaaen। nda bhi nkhon ke lie behad phaayademnd hai। saunpha, mishari aur baadaam ko baraabar maatara men milaakar paaudar banaaen aur subaha- shaam khaaen। baadaam aur gaund se bane ladadoo bhi nkhon ke lie phaayademmd haim। mkhon ki roshani tej karane ke lie salaad (salad) jaroor khaaen। nkhon ke vayaayaam (Eye exsercise) jaroor karem। Disease: munh ke chhaale (Mouth Ulcer) Description: munh ke chhaale (Mouth Ulcer) maauth alasar ko munh men chhaala aana kahate hain। munh ke ndar jo naram aur mulaayam utak hote hain, jise mayookas menbaren (mucous membrane) kahate haim, usi men chhaale parate hain। yah akasar khaane ke dauraam ya kaaphi garam khaane se gaal ke chamare ke katane se hota hai। munh men agar chhaale ho jaaen to kuchh bhi khaane men kaaphi pareshaani hoti hai। khaana to door paani pina bhi mushakil ho jaata hai। chhaale hone par munh men tej jalan aur darad hota hai। kuchh logon ko to bhojan nali tak mem chhaale ho jaate hain। munh men chhaala (Muh ke Chhale) aana ek naaramal bimaari hai, jo kuchh dinom baad apane aap thik ho jaati hai। kuchh logon ko chhaale baara-baar aate hain। aise logon ko apani poori daokatari jnch karaani chaahie, taaki sahi ilaaj kiya ja sake। munh men chhaale hone ke kai kaaran hote haim। kai baar pet ki garami se bhi chhaale ho jaate hain। Symptoms: - chabaane aur barash karane men pareshaani - bhookh mem kami - masaaledaara, khatata aur namakin chij khaane par tej jalam - munh ke mdar saphed aur laal gola-gol chhaale Reasons: munh men chhaalon ke kaaran (Causes of Mouth Ulcer) kabaj (Constipation) lnbe samay tak kabaj rahane se munh men chhaale a jaate hain। aayuraved ke anusaar munh men chhaale pet ki kharaabi tatha pet ki garami ki vajah se hote hain। kabaj isaki mool vajah hai। gaal ya jibh ka katana (Injury in Cheek and Tounge) kai baar koi chij khaate samay dmton ke bich jibh ya gaal ka hisasa a jaata hai, jisaki vajah se chhaale ho jaate hain। aise chhaale munh ki laar se apane-aap thik ho jaate hain। davaaon ke saaid iphekat (Medicine Side Effects) davaaon ke saaid iphekat ki vajah se bhi munh mem chhaale hote hain। lnbe samay tak emtibaoyotik davaaon sevan karame se munh men chhaale aane ki snbhaavana jayaada hoti hai। jayaada entibaoyotik ke sevan se hamaari ntom men laabhadaayak kitaanuon ki snkhaya ghat jaati hai, natija munh men chhaale ho jaate haim। dnton ki galat snrachana (Wrong Structure of Teeth) dnton ki galat snrachana ki vajah se bhi mumh men chhaale hote hain। yadi dmt aare-tirachhe, nukile ya aadhe toote hue hain aur isaki vajah se ve jibh ya munh men chubhate hain ya unase lagaataar ragar lagati rahati hai, to vahn chhaale ho jaate hain। Treatments: ilaaj aur dekhabhaal (Treatment of Mouth Ulcer) - jab tak chhaale khatam mahin ho masaaledaar aur khatata khaana bmd kar den। - khoob paani pien। - gunagune namaka-paani se kulala karen। - mumh ko hamesha saaph rakhen। - darad hone par pen kilar dava le sakate haim। - chhaale vaale jagah par enti-sepatik jel lagaaen। - medikedet maauth vaash se munh saaph karen, kulala karen। - subah subah gaay ke doodh se bane dahi ke saath ek kela khaane se aaraam milata hai। - khoob tamaatar khaaen। tamaatar ka ras ek galaas paami men milaakar kulala karane se chhaale mit jaate hain। - yadi chhaale saamaanay hain, to vitaamin 'bi' kaomapalekas tatha pholik esid ki goliyn 2-3 dim tak lene se chhaale thik ho jaate hain। - chhaale par boro galisarin bhi lagaai ja sakati hai ya poteshiyam paramainganet ke ghol se kulala karane par chhaale khatam hote hain। Home Remedies: munh ke ndar ki satah ke kisi bhi tarah se katane ya usake upar koi phora mikalane se alasar ya chhaala ho jaata hai। munh ka alasar hone par vayakati ka munh tatha jibh parabhaavit ho jaate haim jisase vayakati ko kuchh bhi khaane ya pine men pareshaani hoti hai। jaanie mumh ke chhaalon se bachaav ke ghareloo musakhe (Home remedies for mouth ulcer): 1. maariyal ka doodh (Coconut milk)- naariyal ka doodh munh ke alasar men darad se raahat deta hai saath hi jalan ko door karata hai। upachaar ke lie ek chamamach naariyal ke doodh men thora sa shahad milaakar alasar ke upar lagaaen। is upaay ko din men tim se chaar baar karen। isake alaava naariyal ke doodh se kulala karane par bhi aaraam milata hai। 2. dhaniya ke bij (Coriander seed)- dhaniya ke bij bhi munh ke alasar se raahat dete hain। alasar se hone vaali jalam ko bhi door karate hain। upachaar ke lie paani men dhaniya ke bij daalakar ubaalen aur is paani ko chhaanakar alag rakhen। is paani ko munh men ghuma ghuma kar kulala karen। is upaay ko bhi din bhar men tin se chaar baar karen। 3. beking soda (Baking soda)- beking soda ya sodiyam baai kaarabonet bhi munh ke alasar se nijaat dila sakata hai। esidik khaane- pine se hone vaale alasar men yah behad laabhakaari hai। upachaar ke lie ek chhoti chamamach beking paaudar men paani milaakar pesat taiyaar karen aur parabhaavit sathaan par lagaaem। 4. shahad (Honey)- mumh ke alasar se raahat dene men shahad bhi behad parabhaavi hai। shahad men enti aukasident aur enti maaikarobal gum hote hain। upachaar ke lie rooi ke phaahe ko shahad men dubaakara, parabhaavit sathaan par lagaaen। isi tarah galisarin aur vitaamin i tel ko bhi lagaaya ja sakata hai। 5. elovera (Aloevera)- elovera ka rasa, parabhaavit sathaan par lagaane se alasar se hone vaale darad se raahat milati hai। elovera paraakaritik entisepatik ki tarah kaaray karata hai jisase chhaale jaladi thik hote hain। 6. dhaniya patati (Coriander leaves)- dhaniya patati ko kachacha chabaane se munh ke alasar se raahat milati hai। dhaniya patati men faolik esid ke saath vitaamin bi 1, bi 2, bi 6 aur vitaamin si paaya jaata hai। dhaniya patati ko dndi ke saath lagabhag 10 minat tak chabaana chaahie। isake parayog se munh se aane vaali duragndh se bhi raahat milati hai। 7. tulasi (Basil)- tulasi men enti vaayarala, enti baikatiriyal aur enti phngal gun paae jaate hain। upachaar ke lie 5 se 6 tulasi ki patatiyon ko dhokar achachhi parakaar chabaakar khaaen aur usake baad thora paani pi len। is upaay ko din men do baara, subah aur shaam karen। 8. baraph (Ice)- barapha, alasar ke kaaran munh men home vaale darad se raahat deti hai। baraph ko parabhaavit sathaan par lagaane se, snbmdhit jagah thori der ke lie sunan par jaati hai jisase alasar se hone vaali jalan aur darad se raahat milati hai। Disease: alasar (Ulcer) Description: alasar (Ulcer) pet ya chhoti ntom men hone vaale alasar ko pepatik alasar (Peptic Ulcer) ke roop men jaana jaata hai। pet ke pepatik alasar ko gaisatarik alasar bhi kahate hain। alasar aahaar aur tanaav ya phir pet men amal (acid) ki atirikat maatara jama hone se hota hai। aamaashay ka alasar pet ke alasar se jayaada kaomam bimaari hai। pepatik alasar aamaashay aur pet ke bich ki patali surakasha divaar men ghaav ke baad chhed ho jaane se hota hai। lnbe samay tak entibaayotikasa, darad aur sateraoyad ki dava khaane ke alaava sharaab ke sevan se pet aur aamaashay ka alasar hota hai। pet men esid aur enjaaim ke banane se chhoti nt ke upar aamaashay ke paas chhed ya ghaav ho jaata hai jise alasar kahate hain। adhiknshath yah helikobaikatar paailori (helicobacter pylori) naam ke ek jivaanu ke snkaraman se hota hai। kuchh logon men alasar ke lakashan aasaami se jabaki doosaron men ye jaladi nahin dikhaai parate hain। kabhi-kabhi alasar unahen bhi ho jaata hai, jinahonne isake kisi bhi lakashan ka anubhav nahin kiya hai। Symptoms: - agar pet ka darad alasar ke kaaran ho raha hai, to raat men aur jab bhi aap bhookhe hon, yah achaanak tivar ho sakata hai। - khaana khaame ke do ghnte baad bhookh mahasoos karanaa। - gais aur dakaar men varidadhi। - thakaavat ka ahasaas honaa। - pet bhara hua mahasoos homaa, aur dher saara taral padaarath pi paame men asamarathataa। - bhookh men kami। - vajan ghatanaa। - sine ki hadadiyon aur pet ki naabhi ke bich kisi bhi sathaan par darada। - halaki matali (nausea), jo subah jaagane par sabase aam hoti hai। Reasons: alasar ke kaaran (Causes of Ulcers) koi bhi ek khaas kaaram nahin hota hai jo alasar ke lie utataradaayi hota hai। bahut saare kaaran ke parabhaav se alasar paida hota hai। lekin yah sapashat hai ki pet aur aamaashay ke baach enjaaim aur paachak ras ke asntulan se jo esid banata hai usi se alasar banata hai। aam taur par adhiknsh alasar H. Pylori baikateriya ke snkaraman se hi hota hai। yah baikateriya pet aur chhoti nt ke bich jo surakasha divaar hoti hai, vahin rahata hai। aamataur par yah koi nukasaan nahin pahunchaata hai। lekin isake smkaraman se kabhi-kabhi pet ke ndaruni satah aur nt men soojan ho jaati hai jo baad men alasar ka rup dhaaran kar leta hai। pen kilaras aur enti inphalaametari dava ke lagaataar sevan se chhoti nt aur pet ke bich ki surakasha divaar men soojan aur chhed ho jaata hai jisase alasar hone ki snbhaavana rahati hai। aur bhi hain kai vajah (Other Reason for Ulcer) sharaab aur dhoomarapaan ka jayaada sevam kisi gnbhir bimaari ki vajah se redieshan therepi ki vajah se kise ho sakata hai alasar (Whom May be More Prone to Ulcer) pet ke alasar ke dher saare kaaran hone par bhi jin logon men isake vikasit home ka adhik khatara hota hai, ve hain: ech paailori baikatiriya se snkaramit loga। niyamit roop se daragas ya sui se davaaon ka sevan karane vaale loga। alasar ke paarivaarik itihaas vaale loga। miyamit roop se sharaab pine vaale loga। livara, gurade, ya phepharon se juri bimaariyon vaale loga। 50 saal se adhik umar ke loga। Treatmemts: dekhabhaal aur ilaaj (Treatment for Ulcer) - poha aur saunph ko baraabar maatara mem milaakar chooran bana lijie, 20 garaam chooram ko 2 litar paami mem subah gholakar rakhie, ise raat tak poora pi jaaen। ala‍sar men aaraam milegaa। - patata gobhi aur gaajar ko baraabar maatara men lekar joos bana lijie, is joos ko subaha-shaam eka-ek kap pine se pepatik alasar ke marijon ko aaraam milata hai। - ala‍sar ke marijom ke lie gaay ke doodh se bane ghi ka isatemaal karama phaayademnd hota hai। - ala‍sar ke marijon ko baadaam ka sevan karana chaahie, baadaam pisakar isaka doodh bana lijie, ise subaha-shaam pine se ala‍sar thik ho jaata hai। - sahajan ke pata‍te ko pisakar dahi ke saath pesat banaakar len। is pesa‍t ka sevan din men ek baar karane se ala‍sar men phaayada hota hai। Home Remedies: alasar (ulcer) sharir ki upari tavacha ya mayookas jhilali par ubhara hua ghaav hota hai। alasar jayaadaatar helikobaikatar paayalori (Helicobacter pylori) naam ke jivaanu davaara hota hai। pet ki nt (Intestine) men kai parakaar ke daravay nikalate hain jo bhojan ko pachaame men sahaayak hote hain lekin jab yah daravay jayaada maatara men nikalate hain to pet v mt ki komal tavacha ko jalaane lagate hain। isake kaaran pet men ghaav ban jaata hai। jaamie alasar se bachaav ke ghareloo upaay (Home remedies for ulcer): 1.poha (Bitten rice)- poha alasar ke upachaar men behad phaayademnd hai। poha aur saunph ko baraabar maatara men milaakar paaudar bama len। is paaudar ki 20 garaam maatara ko 2 litar paani men gholakar rakh dijie। dopahar se raat tak is paani ko poora khatam karen। alasar se raahat milegi। 2. patata gobhi aur gaajar (Cabbage and carrot)- patata gobhi men lekatik esid hota hai jisase emino esid banata hai jo pet men rakat ka paravaah barhaata hai। isake saath hi patata gobhi men vitaamin si (vitamim c) bhi uchach maatara men hota hai। patata gobhi aur gaajar ko baraabar maatara men milaakar joos taiyaar karen aur subah shaam eka-ek kap pien। 3. naariyal (Cocomut)- naariyal mem entibaikatiriyal gun paaye jaate hain, jo ki alasar paida karane vaale baikatiriya ko maar dete hain। naariyal ke doodh aur paani men bhi emti- alasar gun paaye jaate hain। alasar ke upachaar ke lie rojaana naariyal paani piem। naariyal ke tel ka sevan bhi alasar se bachaata hai। 4. gaay ka doodh (Cow milk)- haladi men enti baikatiriyal gun hote hain, gaay ke doodh men haladi milaakar pime se bhi alasar rogiyon ko laabh milata hai। 5. baadaam (Almond)- alasar rogiyon ko baadaam pisakara, khaane se laabh hota hai। baadaam ko pisakar usaka doodh jaisa banaakar pien। 6. sahajan (Drum stick)- sahajan ki phali bhi savaasathay ke lihaaj se behad phaayademnd hai। isamen enti baikatiriyal gun hote hain jo rogon se larane mem sahaayak hote hain। sahajan ki phali ko pisakara, dahi ke saath milaakar khaane se alasar rog men aaraam milata hai। 7. shahad (Honey)- kachacha shahad bhi pet ke alasar men behad laabhakaari hai। shahad men galookoj pairaokasaaid (glucose peroxide) paaya jaata hai, jo pet men maujood haanikaarak baikatiriya ko khatam kar deta hai। isake saath hi shahad ke sevan se pet ki jalan se bhi aaraam milata hai। 8. kela (Banana)- kela men entibaikatiriyal tatav paae jaate hain। kela khaane se esiditi se bhi raahat milati hai। kachacha aur paka donon hi tarah ka kela khaane se alasar rogiyon ko behad aaraam milata hai। kachache kele ki sabaji banaakar usamen ek chutaki hing milaakar khaaen। 9. lahasun (Garlic)- lahasun pet ke alasar mem behad laabhakaari hai। upachaar ke lie do se tin lahasun ki kaliyon ko kuchalakara, paani ke saath khaaen। 10. belaphal (Wood apple)- pet ke alasar men belaphal aur usaki patatiyon ka sevan bhi behad laabhadaayak hai। patatiyon men maujood teninas pet ko, kisi bhi tarah ke nukasaan se bachaata hai। belaphal ka ras bhi pet ki jalan aur darad ko door kara, alasar se bachaata hai। Disease: daayariya (Diarrhea) Description: daayariya (Diarrhea) lagaataar looj moshan yaani patala dasat aanaa, ulati hona daayariya kahalaata hai। daayariya vaayarala, baikateriyal snkaraman ke kaaran to hota hi hai lekin sabase kaoman kaaran hai khaana-paan mem garabari, paradooshit paani aur nt ki garabari। dim men agar tim se adhik baar paani ke saath patala dasat ho raha ho to yah daayariya ka lakashan hai। daayariya men sharir men paani ki kami ho jaati hai jise dihaaidareshan kahate hain jo kaaphi gnbhir hota hai। isase sharir kamajor ho jaata hai, sharir men snkaraman phailane ka khatara kaaphi barh jaata hai। samay par ilaaj mahin hone par marij ki jaan bhi ja sakati hai। aam taur par daayariya 3 se 7 dinon tak pareshaan karata hai। daayariya vaise to kabhi bhi ho sakata hai, lekin barasaat men vaayaral daayariya jayaada pareshaam karata hai। isaki vajah gnda paani aur khaanaa-pina hai। daayariya achaanak ho jaata hai aur koras poora hone ke baad hi khatam hota hai। pet men jayaada esiditi banane se bhi daayariya hoti hai। yah sabhi umar ke logon ko pareshaan karata hai। ekayoot daayariya (Acute Diarhea) vayasakom ko saal bhar men ek baar aur bare bachachon ko do baar hota hai। is bimaari mem sabase jayaada khatara dihaaidareshan se hota hai, jisamen sharir se saara paami aur khatam ho jaata hai। nt men paani jaane se pahale hi vo paas ho jaata hai। Symptoms: - nton men soojan se hua daayariya - patala dasat ya looj moshan (paani ki taraha) agar do haphate tak rahe। - dasat ke saath khoona, nv aur pota aata hai। isase sharir kaaphi kamajor ho jaata hai। - ulati, mitali aame ke saath patala dasat aata hai। yah pet aur nt mem esiditi banane se hota hai। Reasons: daayariya ke kaaran (Causes & Reasons of Diarrhea) vaayaral daayariya (Viral Diarrhea) vaayaral inphekashan se sabase jayaada daayariya hota hai। isake lakashan kabhi saamaanay to kabhi kaaphi gnbhir ho jaate hain। patala dasata, looj moshana, pet men maror aana aur bukhaar isake saamaamay lakashan hain। vaayaral daayariya 3 se 7 din tak rahata hai। vaayaral daayariya niman vaayaral snkaraman ke kaaran hote hain rotaavaayaras (Rotavirus)- navajaat bachachom men rotaavaayaras vaayaral snkaraman se vaayaral daayariya ka khatara rahata hai। isase bachane ke lie bachachon ko enti rotaavaayaras injekashan bhi lagaaya jaata hai। norovaayaras (Norovirus)- yah vaayaral daayariya vayasakon aur sakool jaate bachachon ko sabase jayaada pareshaan karata hai। narasimg homa, de keyar sentar aur resatorent men isake snkaraman ka khatara sabase jayaada rahata hai। edenovaayarasa(Adenovirus)- yah vaayaral snkaramam har umar ke logon ko hota hai। baikatiriyal snkaraman se daayariya (Bacterial infections) baikatiriyal snkaraman se hua daayariya kaaphi siriyas hota hai। baikatiriyal snkaraman paradooshit paani, bhojana, phood pavaaijaning se hoti hai। baikatiriyal snkaraman se hui daayariya men lagaataar ulati aanaa, lagaataar looj moshan hote rahanaa, dasat ke saath siraph paani aane ki shikaayat se marij ki haalat kaaphi gnbhir ho jaati hai। baikatiriyal smkaraman se pet men gais bhi ban jaati hai। gnbhir baikatiriyal snkaraman mem kabhi-kabhi dasat ke saath khoona, pota aur nv bhi aati hai। aur bhi hain kai vajah (Some more causes) nton men soojan ke baad bhi daayariya hota hai i-kolaai ke snkaraman se bhi daayariya hota hai alakohal sevan ke saaid iphekat men bhi daayariya hota hai daayabitij ke marij ko bhi daayariya ki shikaayat rahati hai rediyotherepi, kimotherepi men bhi daayariya ki shikaayat hoti hai kisi khaas entibaayotikas ke sevan se bhi daayariya hota hai, khaasakar vaise enti baayotikas jo nt par parabhaav daalate hain parajivi jo paradooshit paani aur khaame ke jarie hamaare pet men jaata hai, vo hamaare paachan tmtar ko bigaar deta hai aur jisase daayariya ki shikaayat hoti hai kainsar ki davaa, vajan ghataane ki davaa, balad pareshar ki dava ke saaid iphekat ki vajah se bhi daayariya hota hai elaraji se bhi daayariya hoti hai, khaasakar vaise chij khaame se masalana- aaratiphishiyal savitanar ya doodh men laikatoj ki maatara rahane se daayariya ho sakata hai। Treatments: ilaaj aur dekhabhaal (Treatment and Care for Diarrhea) - daayariya hone par tela-masaalon vaale khaane se parahej karana chaahie। - daayariya men doodh ya doodh se bane padaarath nahin khaana chaahie, marij ki haalat aur bigar jaati hai। - kele, chaavala, seb ka murababa aur tosat ka misharan jise baraat kahate hain, isake sevan se daayariya mem raahat milati hai। - kachacha kela aur chaaval nton ki gati ko niyntarit karane aur dasat rokane men sahaayata karate hain। - parayaapat maatara men taral padaarath len lekin agar phir bhi daayariya barh raha ho to turnt daokatar se snparak karen। Home Remedies: jab vayakati ki paachan kariya (Digestive System) suchaaroo roop se kaaray karana bnd kar deti hai, tab use ulati aur patale dasat hone lagate hain। yahi sathiti daayariya kahalaati hai। daayariyaa, baikatiriyal tatha vaayaral inphekashan (Bacterial and Viral Infectiom) ke kaaran hota hai, jo dooshit bhojan ya khaane ke davaara vayakati ke sharir men pahunch kara, paachan kariya ko parabhaavit karate hain। daayariya kai dauraan vayakati ke pet men darad hota hai, pet men ainthana, ji michalaana aadi samasayaaen bhi ho sakati hain। daayariya ke dauraan vayakati ko di-haaidareshan (Dehydration) ho sakata hai, jisase sathiti aur bhi bigar sakati hai। daayariya ke lakashan vayakati men do se chaar din mem ubharate hain। jaanie daayariya se bachaav ke lie kuchh ghareloo upachaar (Home Remedies of Diarrhea) niche diye gae upachaaron ke davaara daayariya bimaari men raahat paai ja sakati hai: 1. dahi (Yogurt)- dahi men maujood baikatiriyaa, sharir men maujood vishaile baikatiriya ka naash kara, daayariya se bachaate hain। daayariya ke upachaar ke lie do katori dahi khaane se hi behad aaraam milata hai। saade chaaval men dahi milaakar bhi khaai ja sakati hai। 2. adarak (Ginger)- adarak ka parayog phood paoijaning (food poisoning) hone par bhi kiya jaata hai, aise men daayariya se raahat dene men bhi adarak kaaphi parabhaavashaali hai। adarak ke parayog se pet ki ainthan (stomach cramps) aur darad se bhi raahat milati hai। upachaar ke lie adarak ko kadadookas karake, usamen shahad (honey) milaakar khaaem। isake tumrat baad paani n pien। adarak ki chaay (bina doodh ki) bhi kaaphi aaraam deti hai। 3. methi daana (Methidama)- daayariya ke ilaaj ke lie methi daana behad phaayademnd bataaya gaya hai। ek chhoti chamamach methi daama ko chabaakara, ek bari chamamach dahi khaane se daayariya se nijaat milati hai। isake alaava ek chamamach methi daana aur jira (cumin) ko bhoom kar paaudar bana len aur do bari chamamach dahi men milaakar khaaen। is misharan ko din bhar men tin baar khaane se behad aaraam milata hai। 4. seb ka siraka (Apple cider vinegar)- seb ka siraka bhi daayariya men behad phaayademnd hai। seb ke sirake ka esidik guna, daayariya ke baikatiriya ko khatam kar deta hai। upachaar ke lie ek gilaas paani men ek chamamach siraka milaaen aur pi len। is misharan ko ek din men do se tin baar tab tak pien jab tak daayariya thik n ho jaae। 5. kela (Banama)- kele men kaaphi maatara men paikatin tatav (pectin content) aur pauteshiyam hota hai, isalie daayariya men kela khaane ki salaah di jaati hai। daayariya hone par do se tin pake hue kela roj khaaen। 6. kaimomaail chaay (Chamomile tea)- kaimomaail daayariya ke upachaar men behad phaayademnd hai। daayariya ke upachaar ke lie kaimomaail ki chaay banaakar pien। 7. saphed chaaval (White rice)- saadaa, saphed gile chaaval bhi daayariya ke dauraan khaane ki salaah di jaati hai। is tarah ke chaaval supaachay hote haim। is tarah ke chaaval khaane se dasat kam aate haim। saada chaaval ko thora gila karake khaaem। savaad ke lie chaaval men dahi milaakar kha sakate hain। 8. gaajar ka soop (Carrot soup)- gaajar ka soop bhi daayariya men behad phaayademnd hai। daayariya ke dauraan sharir men hui poshak tatavon (nutrients) ki kami ko poora karame ke saath hi gaajar ka soop imayooniti (immunity) ko majaboot karata hai। soop banaane ke lie, gaajar ko kaat kar ubaal len aur jab gaajar ubalakar paani men ghul jaae taba, paani ko chhaan kar alag kara len। isamen savaadaanusaar namaka, bhuna jira aur kaalimirach paaudar milaaen। Disease: susati (Lethargy) Description: susati (Lethargy) kai baar sharir men saphoorati (energy) nahin rahati। sharir ekadam thaka hua mahasoos karata hai, aur bahut kamajori mahasoos hoti hai। kai baar aalas itana hota hai ki hamesha nind aati rahati hai। isi avasatha ko lithaaraji ya susati kahate hain। tanaavapooran maahaul ya poshan ki kami ke kaaran sharir kamajor hone lagata hai। kai baar raat men achachhi nind n sone par bhi agale din thaka hua mahasoos karate hain। lekin jayaada susati sharir ke lie behad haanikaarak bhi hai। kai baar yah susati maut ki vajah bhi ho sakati hai, kayonki jayaada susati se baren ke selas bhi susat hone lagate hain aur dhire dhire kaaray karana bnd kar dete hain। poore sharir ki savabhaavik parakariya dhimi par jaati hai, jo kai samasayaaon ka kaaran ho sakati hai। aise men sharir ko ekativ banaaye rakhama behad jaroori hota hai। Symptoms: - eknt achachha lagana - kamajori mahasoos hona (Weakness in Body) - kisi kaam men man n lagana - chhote se chhota kaam karane men chirachiraana - har samay nimd aur aalas aana - har samay lete rahane ka man homa - man men hamesha nakaaraatamak vichaar aana Reasons: susati ke kaaram (Causes of Lethargy) susati ka amubhav sabhi ko hota hai, lekin thora aaraam karane ya raat ki nind ke baada, agali subah tak susati door ho jaati hai। yadi isake baad bhi susati bani rahe to yah bimaari ka snket ho sakata hai। kisi bhi vayakati ki susati ka asar n keval usake shaaririk balaki maamasik v saamaajik satar par bhi parata hai। susati, vayasat dinacharayaa, kharaab jivam shaili, bimaariyn, amiyamit v asntulit khaana-paan v anay kaaranon se ho sakati hai। aamataur par achachhi nind lene aur aur dinacharaya mem badalaav se is samasaya ko kaaphi had tak thik kiya ja sakata hai lekin kai baar chikitasak ki salaah leni hi parati hai। is samasaya ke anay kaaran (Reasons of Lethargy) kamajori ki vajah se। jayaada tamaavagarasat rahane se। nind poori m hone ki vajah se। sharir men vitaamin ki kami se। sharir men khoon ki kami ki vajah se। Treatmemts: susati se bachane ke upaay (Tips to Prevent from Lethargy) - roj yog aur vayaayaam karen। - subah ki taaji hava men tahalen। - tanaavamukat rahane ka parayaas karen। - khaane men vitaamin ki maatara barhaaen। - kam se kam 8 ghmte ki nind jaroor len। - nvale ka murababa bhi sharir ko saphoorati deta hai। - halaka sngita, halaki aavaaj men sunen। isase bhi maanasik susati door hoti hai। - kai baar sugmdhit telon ki maalish se bhi sharir ki susati aur susati mitaai ja sakati hai। - sntulit aur paushatik bhojan karen, jisamen hari sabajiyn, daalen, dahi aur mausami phal shaamil hon। - apani ungaliyon ke poron se chehare ki masaaj karen। aisa karane se balad sarakuleshan barhegaa, jisase vayakati ekativ mahasoos karegaa। Home Remedies: bhaagadaur bhari aadhunik jindagi aur kai tarah ke tanaava, m keval shaaririk balaki maanasik roop se bhi vayakati ko thaka dete hain। thakaavat har kisi ko hoti hai paramatu kai logon ko poore sharir men darad ki shikaayat rahati hai। darad ko kam karame ke lie log akasar penakilar le lete hain। ye davaaen tunrat aaraam deti hain paranatu lamabe samay tak isaka parayog mukasaan pahuncha sakata hai। aaie jaanen thakaavat se bachaav ke lie ghareloo nusakhe (Home remedies for lethargy) 1. garin ti (Green tea)- thakaavat ko door karane ke lie ek kap garin ti pina behad parabhaavi hai। niyamit roop se garin ti pine se vajan bhi kntarol men rahata hai। mnsapeshiyom men darad (muscle pain) hone par aap garin ti behad laabhakaari hai। 2. adarak ki chaay (Ginger tea)- adarak ki chaay kudarati penakilar ke roop men kaaray karati hai। yah vayakati ko tarotaaja bhi mahasoos karaati hai। tulasi ke kaarhe men adarak milaakar bhi piya ja sakata hai। 3. saunph (Saunf)- kisi pakavaan men savaad barhaane ke saath hi saunph sns men taajaghi laane men bhi behad parabhaavakaari hai। saunph ka parayog rasoi men zaroor hota hai। saunph khaane se pet saaf rahata hai aur aap khud ko tarotaaja mahasoos karate hai। 4. ajavaayan (Ajwain)- ajavaayan ke patate bhi darad nivaarak dava ki tarah kaam karate hain। yah sharir ke toote-phute ki ng ki maramamat karane aur joron ke darad men bahut laabhaparad hote hain। 5. kadadoo ke bij (Pumpkin seed)- kadadoo ke bij men maigamishiyam hota hai, jo aalas v thakaavat se larane men madad karata hai। aadhe ghnte ki ekasarasaaij men agar aap thaka hua mahasoos karati hain to isaka matalab hai ki aapamen maiganishiyam ki kami hai। vayaayaam ke dauraan sharir men aukasijan ke niramaan ke lie maiganishiyam jaroori hai। isaki kami ki vajah se thakaavat jaladi hoti hai। 6. akharot (Wallnut)- akharot men omega 3 phaiti esid paaya jaata hai। omega 3 phaiti esid n keval thakaam aur aalas se raahat deta hai, balaki yah avasaad se bhi bachaata hai। isalie akharot khaane se aapaki jhapakiyom ki samasaya door hogi। 7. anaaj (Whole grain)- anaaj men phaaibar ki maatara adhik hoti hai। isalie aalas aur thakaan mitaane men yah madadagaar saabit hota hai। anaaj men kaomapalekas kaarabohaaidaret (complex carbohydrate) hote hain। ye thakaan se larane men madadagaar hote hain। 8. laal mirach (Red chilly)- laal mirach men vitaamin si paaya jaata hai, jo thakaan door karata hai। laal mirach se dimaag ekativ rahata hai aur ham hamesha tarotaaja mahasoos karate hain। 9. dahi (Curd)- dahi men maujood achachhe baikatiriya paacham tntar (immune system) ko majaboot rakhate haim। 4 sapataah tak din men do baar yadi dahi khaaya jaae to shaaririk aur maanasik sehat ke saath rog paratirodhak kashamata bhi barhati hai aur thakaan kam hoti hai। Disease: masatishak ka daura (Cerebral Stroke) Description: hamaare sharir men masatishak aur maariyom ko paraamavaayu (Oxygen) aur poshak tatavon ki nirntar aapoorati rakat vaahikaaon se rakat ke davaara ki jaati hai। jab bhi in rakatavaahikaaon men kisi kaaran kashati pahunchati hai ya avarodh niramaan hota hai tab masatishak ke kuchh hisason ko rakat ki aapoorati bnd ho jaati hai। jis tarah haraday ko rakat ki aapoorati n hone par haridayaghaat a jaata hai, usi parakaar masatishak ke kuchh hisase ko 3 se 4 minat se jayaada rakat n milane par paraanavaayu aur poshak tatavon ke abhaav men nashat hone lagata hai, ise hi masatishak ka daura bhi kahate hain। Symptoms: - kamajori mahasoos hona (Weakness in Body) - disha aur niradesh samajhane men pareshaani - siradarad hona - bharam ki sathiti - bolane men takaliph hona - ji michalaana aur ulati hona - sharir ke ek hi taraph ke chehare, haath ya tng men sunanapan - dhire ya asapashat bolana - achaanak larakharaanaa, chakakar aanaa, sharir ka sntulan bigarama - ek ya donon nkhon se dekhane men kathinaai Reasons: masatishak ke daure ke kaaran (Causes & Reasons of Cerebral Stroke) masatishak ka daura hone ke mukhayata: 2 kaaran hote hain, jo niman hain: 1. arakatata masatishak ka daura (Ischemic stroke)- daura parane ka sabase aam kaaran hai। yah dimaag ke kisi rakatavaahini ke snkiran hone ya avarodhar niramaan hone ke kaaran hota hai। yah bhi do parakaar ka hota hai- 1.1. tharomabotik satarok (Thrombotic stroke)- is parakaar ke masatishak ke daure mem masatishak ki rakat vaahini men khoom ke jam jaane ke kaaran ya thakake ke kaaran avarodh ho jaata hai। jin rogiyon men khoon ke ndar kolesataraol ka paramaan jayaada hota hai, aise rogiyon ki rakatavaahini men bhitari satar par vasa jama ho jaati hai jise palaak kahate hai। is par khoon ka thakaka jama ho jaane par dhire-dhire poori rakatavaahini men avarodh hone lagata hai aur masatishak ke us hisase ko rakat n milane par tharomabotik satarok par jaata hai। 1.2. inbolik satarok (Embolic stroke)- is parakaar ke masatishak ke daure mem rakat ka thakaka ya injekashan ya salaain davaara galati se rakat vaahini men paravesh kiya hua hava ka chhota bulabula masatishak ke kisi chhoti rakatavaahini mem phasane ke kaaran rakatavaahini mem avarodh niramaan ho jaata hai aur masatishak ke us hisase ko rakat n milame par inbolik satarok par jaata hai। 2. rakatasataraav masatishak ka daura (Hemorrhagic stroke)- masatishak ki kisi rakatavaahimi men rakatasataraav hone ke kaaran hone vaale is parakaar ke masatishak ke daure behad gnbhir hote hai। uchach rakatachaapa, rakat vaahimi ki janamajaat vikariti ya rakat vaahini men phulaav ke kaaran masatishak men rakatasataraav ho sakata hai। isake do parakaar hain- 2.1. intaraa- karaaniyal haimarej (Intra-cranial hemorrhage)- is parakaar men masatishak ke kisi rakatavaahini men rakatasataraav home ke kaaran masatishak ke us hisase ko rakat ki aapoorati men kami aane ke kaaran baren selas ko kashati pahunchati hai। is parakaar ke masatishak ke daure ka paramukh kaaran uchach rakatadaab hai। lagaataar kai samay tak uchach rakatachaap ke kaaran rakatavaahini kamajor aur kari ho jaati hai aur parinaamata: phat jaati hai। 2.2. saba- aarakanoid haimarej (Sub-archnoid hemorrhage)- is parakaar men masatishak aur kapaal ke bich ke satar men kisi rakatavaahini men rakatasataraav hone ke kaaram sab aarakanoid sapes men rakat ekatarit ho jaata hai। isaka paramukh kaaran rakat vaahini ki janamajaat vikariti ya rakat vaahini men phulaav hota hai। is parakaar men rogi ko tej saradarad ka anubhav hota hai। 2.3. tarnsent ishachemik ataik (Transient ischemic attack)- ek tisare parakaar ka bhi masatishak ka asathaai daura hota hai jisame satarok ke lakashan kuchh mimaton se lekar kuchh ghnto tak hi rahate hain aur baad men thik ho jaate hain। ise tarnsent ishachemik ataik (Transient ischemic attack) ya tiaaie (TIA) kaha jaata hai। yah is baat ki chetaavani deta hai ki aapako koi samasaya hai aur isaka ilaaj n karaane par nikat bhavishay men aapako satarok par sakata hai। Treatmemts: masatishak ka daure se bachane ke lie upaay (Treatments & Tips to Prevents Cerebral Stroke) - sharaab aur dhoomarapaan bnd karen। - phala, sabajiyn itayaadi aahaar lena chaahie। - tanaav se door rahen। niyamit vayaayaam aur yog karen। - agar aap motaape ke shikaar hai to apana vajam niyntarit rakhen। - agar baara-baar siradarad ki pareshaani hoti hai to chikitasak se isaki jnch karaaen। - agar aap uchach rakatachaap (Hypertension), madhumeh (Diabetes), haraday rog (Heart disease) se pirit hain to niyamit daokatar se jnch karaate rahen। Disease: maayopiya (Myopia) Descriptiom: aajakal adhikaash logon ki nkhon men ripharaikativ (Refractive) vikaar yaami kiranon ke vakar ki samasaya ke lakashan dikhaai dene lage hain। isamen nikat darishati dosh yaani maayopiya (Myopia) se sabase jayaada log parabhaavit hain। chikitasakon ke anusaara, bachapan men dekhane ki kashamata ka vikaas aur kishoraavasatha men nkh ki lnbaai barhati hai lekin nikat darishati dosh hone ki vajah se yah kuchh jayaada hi barh jaati hai। aisi sathiti men nkh men jaanevaala parakaash retina par kendarit nahin hotaa। isi vajah se tasavir dhundhali dikhaai deti hai lekin is dosh ko kaonatekat lens ya sarajari se thik karaaya ja sakata hai। Symptoms: - chakakar aana - bachachon ko sakool men balaik borad par likha hua n dikhana - telivijan dhundhala dikhana - nkhom ka bhainga hona - doori par likhe akashar n parh paana - sir men darad rahana Reasons: maayopiya ke kaarana- (Causes & Reasons of Myopia) aise log jo nikat darishati dosh ki samasaya se pareshaam hain yaani ki jinahen thori door ki chijem bhi saaph dikhaai nahin detim, use ripharekativ erar (Refractive error) kahate haim। maayopiya se garasat logon men aaibaol bahut lnbi ho jaati hai ya phir kaoraniya (Cornia) bahut jayaada karavi ho jaata hai jisase nkh mem pahunchane vaala parakaash thik tarah se phokas nahin kar paataa। aise men kisi bhi chij ki tasavira, retima par n banakara, usake saamane ban jaati hai jisase chijen dhundhali dikhaai deti hain। yah samasaya umar ke saath barhati jaati hai। maayopiya ki samasaya se joojh rahe log chashama ya kntekat lains ke jariye samasaya se nijaat pa sakate hain lekin samasaya jayaada ho to aupareshan davaara maayopiya ka ilaaj snbhav hai। isake alaava niman kaaran bhi hain: (Other Reasoms & Causes of Myopia) daayabitij (Daibetes) se garasit hone para। aamuvnshiki (Genetic Disorder) kaaranon se bhi aisa ho sakata hai। lnbe samay tak ek hi lains ka parayog karanaa। (Use of lenses) kisi bhi chij ko bahut paas se ghoorakar kaaray karamaa। kam roshani men koi kaaray karanaa, jaise parhana ya tivi dekhanaa। Treatments: maayopiya se bachaav ke lie saamaanay upachaar (Treatment & tips for Myopia) - barithing vayaayaam karen। - tariphala chooran rojaana lem। - lnbe samay tak telivijan dekhame ya parhane se bachen। - jahn kaam karen, vahn parayaapat roshani honi chaahie। - nkhom ki roshani barhaane ke lie mvala ka parayog karen। - munh men paani bhar kar nkhon ko taaje paani se dhoen। - paradooshan ya dhoop mem nikalame se pahale nkhon par chashama pahanen। - likaresi ki jar ka paaudar aur shahad milaakar doodh ke saath len। - naariyala, mishari, saunph aur baadaam ko milaakar mikasar taiyaar karen aur paaudar banaayen। din men do baar khaaen। Disease: khararaate lena (Snoring) Description: sote vakat sns ke saath tej aavaaj aur vaaibareshan (Sound & Vibration) aama khararaate (Snoring) kahalaata hai। khararaate lena saadhaarana-si pareshaani hai, lekin jab yah bimaari ka roop le leti hai to gmbhir samasaya ban jaati hai। sns lene men baara-baar rukaavat hone par sharir men aukasijan ka leval kam ho jaata hai, jisase bipi barh jaata hai। sharir men aukasijan kam hote hi dil ko aukasijan ke lie jayaada pareshar lagaana parata hai। jab yah samasaya barh jaati hai to haarat ataik bhi ho sakata hai। Symptoms: - subah uthane par gale aur naak ka sookha hona - din ke samay bhi nind mahasoos hona - chhote chhote kaamon ke baad bhi thakaan mahasoos hona aur aalas aana - gale aur naak se tej aavaaj nikalana - sote vakat munh khul jaana aur hava nikalana Reasons: khararaate ya sanoring ke kaarana- (Causes & Reasons of Snoring) jayaadaatar logon ko lagata hai ki khararaate aane ki vajah jayaada thakaan hai isalie ve ise anadekha kar dete hain। isase samasaya gnbhir ho jaati hai। daraasala, sote samay sns men rukaavat khararaate aane ki mukhay vajah hai। gale ke pichhale hisase ke snkare ho jaane par aukasijan snkari jagah se hoti hui jaati hai, jisase aasapaas ke tishoo vaaibaret (Tissue Vibrate) hote hain। isi se khararaate aate hain। kai baar log pith ke bal sote hain, jisase jibh pichhe ki taraph ho jaati hai। taaloo ke pichhe yoovayal (taaloo ke pichhe thoraa-sa lataka hua mmsa) par jaakar lag jaati hai, jisase sns lene aur chhorane men rukaavat aane lag jaati hai। isase sns ke saath aavaaj aur vaaibareshan hone lagata hai। niche vaale deti hai। aise men sns leme aur chhodane ke lie pareshar lagaana parata hai, jis kaaran vaaibareshan hota hai। naak ki hadadi terhi hona (Crooked Nose Bome) aur usamen mns barha (Meat soar) honaa। isamen bhi sns leme ke lie pareshar lagaana parata hai। Treatments: khararaate ya sanoring se bachaav ke lie upaaya- (Tips & Treatments to Prevent Smoring) - sone ki pojishan badalem। - nashe vaale hai। Disease: sanabaram (Sunburm) Description: sanabaran ya dhoop se jhulasana (Sunburn) dhoop ke kaaran tavacha ka parabhaavit homa aam baat hai। koi bhi vayakati yadi dhoop men jayaada der rahata se aaraam milata hai। Disease: kaali khmsi (Whooping Cough) Description: kaali khnsi (Whooping Cough) vahooping kaph ya kaali khnsi (Whooping cough) gnbhir kisam ki khmsi hoti hai, jo jayaadaatar 5 se bachaav ke ghareloo upaay (Home Remedies for Whooping Cough) 1. suhaagaa, kalamishoraa, phitakari, kaala namak aur yavakashaar ko pisakar chooran taiyaar kar lem। ise tave par bhoonakar 2-2 garaam ki ki jata ki bhasam karake lagabhag 1 garaam ka chautha bhaag shahad men milaakar ya paani se khaaen। isase 2-3 baar men hi khnsi ka veg v khnsi khatam ho jaati hai। 6. adarak ke ras ko shahad men bhare aur khujali vaale chakate ho jaanaa। - bina kisi vajah ke lagaataar daayariya bane rahanaa। - bina kisi vajah ke lagaataar thakaam bane rahama aur teji se vajan giranaa। - munh men ghaav ho jaanaa। - munh men saphed chhaale jaise mishaan honaa। - yaadadaashat men kami, dipareshan ya anay dimaagi bimaari - lnbe samay tak bukhaar rahana Reasons: edas ke kaarak (Causes of Aids in Hindi) duniyaabhar mem edas ki phailane ki sabase bari vajah (Causes of Aids) asurakashit yaun snbndhon ko maana jaata hai। lekin kai anay kaaran bhi hai jo edas ke lie jimamevaar maane jaate hain: asurakashit sekas (Unsafe Sex):- ek se adhik saathiyom ke saath yaun snbndh bamaane se echaaaivi edas phail sakata hai। yah samalaingik snbndhom men bhi ho sakata hai। snkaramit rogi davaara (From HIV+ Victim):- echaaaivi paojitiv purush ya mahila ke saath asurakashit yaun snbndh banaane ke kaaran bhi yah phailata hai। snkaramit khoon charhaane (Through Blood Transfusion):- bina jnch kiya hua raka‍t garahan karane ke kaaran bhi echaaaivi se pirit hone ka khatara rahata hai। yah edas ko phailaane ki doosari sabase bari vajah maani jaati hai। snkaramit sui ke isatemaal se (Through Infected Needles):- daragas ki samasaya na siraph nashe tak simit hai balaki agar ek hi injekashan se kai log daragas len to yah edas ka kaaram ban sakata hai। siraph daragas hi nahin davaai lene ke dauraan bhi snkaramit sui ka isatemaal haamikaarak hota hai। snkaramit baled se (Through Infected Blood):- saath hi naai ke yahn bina sataralaaijad (rogaanu-mukata) usatara ya puraana inaphekated baled (Imfected Blade) isatemaal karane se bhi yah phail sakata hai। snkaramit maata se (HIV Positive Mother):- echaaaivi snkaramit maata ke davaara yah bachache mem khoon ya parasav ke samay aur doodh pilaane ke dauraan pahunch jaata hai। Treatmemts: edas se bachaav (Tips to prevent AIDS in Hindi) surakashit sekas (Use Safety):- edasa, echaaaivi snkaraman aur anay sekas snkaramit bimaariyn rokane ke lie hamesha snbndh banaate samay kndom aadi ka parayog karana chaahie। apane jivanasaathi ke parati vaphaadaar rahana chaahie aur ek se adhik va‍yakati se yaunasnbndh bamaane se bachana chaahie। isatemaal ki gai suiyon ka parayog na karen (Use Disposable Syringe):- sui lagavaate samay hamesha yah dhayaan rakhen ki disapojebal sirinj ya suiyon ka hi isatemaal ho। khoon ke lena-den se pahale jnch (Test Before Blood Transfusion):- khoon lene ya dene se pahale usaki jnch avashay kar len। yadi aap echa.aai.vi smkaramit ya edas garasit hain to rakatadaan na karen। garabhavati mahilaaen dhayaam rakhen (Tips for HIV+ Pregnant):- garabhavati mahilaaon ko apana echaaaivi tesat jaroor karaana chaahie। agar jnch paojitiv hai to bachacha ho jaane ke baad echaaaivi se garasat mn ko bachache ko apana doodh nahin pilaana chaahie। is kes men botal se doodh pilaana behatar maama jaata hai। shak home par echa.aai.vi tesat (HIV AIDS Test):- yadi aap ko echa.aai.vi edas hone ka sndeh ho to turnt apama echa.aai.vi parikashan karaana chaahie। echaaaivi edas ki davaaiyn (HIV AIDS Drugs):- echaaaivi paojitiv vayakati ko ilaaj ke dauraan enti-retarovaayaral daragas die jaate hain। Disease: jika vaayaras (Zik Virus) Description: ibola vaayaras ke baad duniyaabhar men aatmk phailaani vaali nai bimaari hai jikaa। jika vaayaras logon ke lie itana khataranaak hai ki vishav savaasathay sngathan ne jika vaayaras par ga‍lobal imarajensi ghoshit ki hai। jika vaayaras baraajil samet kai anay ameriki deshom men phaila hua hai aur inahin deshom ke aane vaale logon ke davaara isake vishav ke anay deshon men phailane ke aasaar hain। aaiye jaanen jika vaayaras aur isake snkaraman ke vishay men pooran jaanakaari (Zik Virus Information in Hindi)। Symptoms: - nkhen laal hona - jorom men darad - bukhaar - ulati - kamazori Treatments: jika vaayaras ka ilaaj (Treatment of Zik Virus in Hindi) * sidisi ke anusaar jika inphekashan se larane ke lie abhi kisi injekashan ya davaai ko ijaad nahin kiya gaya hai। isase pirit vayakati ko poori tarah se aaraam karana chaahie, khoob saara paani pima chaahie, bukhaar ki saamaanay davaai leni chaahie। * jika vaayaras se snkaramit hone par khud ko machachhar ke kaatane se bachaana chaahie anayatha yah vaayaras machachharon davaara anay logon men pahunch sakata hai। pirit rogi ka machachharon se bachaav bahut jaroori hai। nota: bukhaar aane par esaparim (Aspirin), baroophem jaisi davaaiym bilakul nahin leni chaahie। garabhavati mahilaaon ke lie khaas niradesh (Tips For Pregnant Women) sidisi ke davaara anay deshon men rahane vaali garabhavati mahilaaon ko yah sujhaav diya gaya hai ki vah apharikaa, dakashin amerika ya jika parabhaavit anay deshom men na jaaen। jika vaayaras se parabhaavit jagahon par rahane vaali garabhavati mahilaaon ko niman baaton ka khayaal rakhana chaahie: * khud ko machachharon ke kaatane se bachaana chaahie। * raat ko sote samay machachharadaani ka parayog karana chaahie aur machachharon ke kaatane se bachame vaali karim lagaani chaahie। * agar machachharon ke kaatane par siradarada, hala‍ka bukhaara, laal nkhen, joron mem darad jaise lakashan dikhen to turnt daokatar se salaah leni chaahie। * agar garabhavati nahin hain to kuchh dinom ke lie pareganensi ke palaan ko taal dena chaahie। garabhavati mahilaaon ko machachharon se bachane ki poori koshish karani chaahie kayomki jika vaayaras ke kaaran unake garabh men pal rahe bachachon ke masatishak ko sabase adhik nukasaan hota hai।
